Tang-hng e5 Kou3-su7
Lek8-ai3 m7 si7 thiaN3-thang3
Chai7-cha2 Chi-na2 hun choe3 Liat8-kok e5 si5, Chhou2-kok Kiong-ong5 kap Chin3-kok  Le7-kong ti7 Ian-leng5 e5 sou2-chai7 kau-chian3;  Chhou2-peng toa7 pai7, Kiong-ong5 chit8 bak8 tioh8 siong.  I nia2 peng e5 chong2 si-leng7-koaN mia5 kio3 Chu2-hoan2, sim-lai7 put-chi2 hoan5-lo2.   M7-ku2 i chit8 e5 phiah chin m7 ho2,  chiu7-si7 ai3 chiah8 chiu2; na7 chiah8 chiu2 chiu7  khun3 kui-mi5 kui-jit8; in-ui7 chhut-kun, sou2- i2 kim3 chiu2.   I u7 chit8 e5 lou5-pok8, mia5 Iong5- kok, put-chi2 gau5 khoan2-thai7 i, chin gau5  thiaN3 i e5 chu2-lang5, khoaN3-kiN3 Chu2-hoan2  hoan5-lo2 kau3 an2-ni, siuN7 i peng5-sou3 ai3 chiah8  chiu2, chiu7 phang5 chit8 toa7 au, tng cheng3  lang5 e5 bin7-cheng5 phian3 i kong2 si7 te5.   Chu2-hoan2 chit8-e7 phiN7 chiu7 chai-kio3 si7 chiu2;  chiu7 siuN7, Che si7 Iong5-kok thiaN3 goa2, sou3-i2  chhong3 chiu2 phian3 kong2 si7 te5, lai5 ho7 goa2 chiah8.  I chiu7 ka7 i lim-loh8-khi3, koh kio3 phang5 te5 lai5.   Iong5-kok iu5-goan5 chiong  chiu2 hou7 i; bo5 siuN7 chit8 au ke3 chit8 au;  chiah8-liau2 soa3 toa7 chui3, to2 ti7 tiuN3-piN5 lai7,  khun3 kau3 put-ti thian-te7.    Chhou2 Kiong-ong5 siuN7 keh jit8 beh kohkap Chin3-kok  kau-chian3; chiu7 chhe lang5  khi3 chhiaN2 Chu2-boan2 lai5 chham-siong5; siaN2  chai Chu2-hoan2 chiu2-chui3 na2 si2 chit8 poaN- iuN7.   Chiu7 siuN7 ka-ki7 ia7 tioh8-siong, choan  kho3 Chu2-hoan2 chit8 lang5; taN I an2-ni, beh  thai3 oe7 koh kau-chian3 tit?   Kou-put- chiong thau3 mi5 thiu peng to3-khi3.   Chiu7 chiong Chu2-hoan2 kau-thok chit8 e5 chin  gau5 choh8-chiN3, mia5 kio3 Iong2 Iu5-ki,  lai5 po2-hou7 I, kiaN-liau2 hou7 Chin3-kok liah8  khi3, chiu7 chin leng5-jiok8.   Kau3 keh-jit8  e5 jit8 beh tau3, Chu2-hoan2 chiu2-chui3 cheng- sin5, chiah chai chiah e5 tai7-chi3, chiu7 kong2,  Iong5-kok hai7 goa2, Iong5-kok hai7 goa2; goa2  thai3 u7 bin7 thang koh kiN3 goa2 e5 ong5?    Chiu7 ka-ki7 chu7-chin7 lai5 si2.     
Chiau3 an2-ni khoaN3, Chu2-hoan2 e5 lou5-pok8 Iong5-kok, phang5 chiu2 hou7 Chu2-hoan2 chiah8 e5 si5, peng3 bo5 poaN3  tiam2 beh hai7 Chu2 hoan2 e5 i3-su3 ;put-ko3 in-ui7 Chu2- hoan2 peng5-sou3 ai3 chiah8 chiu2 chiu2, sou2-i2 chiong chiu2 hou7 i chiah8, ai3 tit i hoaN-hi2, sng3-si7 chhut ti7 thiaN3-thang3  e5 sim; bo5 liau7 Chu2-hoan2 keng3-jian5 in-ui7 an2-ni lai5 gou7 toa7-su7, soa3 liau2 siN-mia7.   Hian7-si5 e5 peng5-iu2 siong5- siong5 khng3 lang5 chiah8-hun lim-chiu2, kiam2 m7-si7 iu5- goan5 chhut ti7 ho2-n3?   M7-ku2 au7-lai5 in-ui7 hit e5 lang5  soa3 tiau5 hun boe7 koe2-tit, ti3-kau3 kheng-ka tong7-san2; a2-si7 in-ui7 chiu2-chui3;  
lai5 lau7 chhut tai7-chi3, kiam2 m7  si7 ho2-i3 piN3 chiaN5 phaiN2-i3 lah?   So2-i2 chin sim thiaN3  peng5-iu2 e5, long2 tioh8 chhut ti7 jin5-ai3, m7 thang chhut  ti7 lek8-ai3, na7 si7 lek8-ai3, chiu7 bo5 sng3 si7 chin thiaN3-thang3.   Chim-gian5 u7 kong2, ¡§ThiaN3 kiaN2-ji5 e5, chiu7- si7 hai7 kiaN2-ji5, ¡¨ ia7 si7 chit e5 i3-su3.     
Kau2 ok lian5-lui7 chiu2 sng
Song3-kok u7 chit8 keng chiu2-tiam3, chiu2 ia7 chin ho2, ke3-chiN5 ia7 kong-to7, chih-chiap  lang5-kheh ia7 chin un-khun5, chio-pai5 ia7  koa3 kau3 koaiN5.   Chong2-si7 long2 bo5 lang5 boe2, sim7-chi3 chiu2 ia7 pai5 kau3 soa3 sng  khi3.   Tiam3 chu2-lang5 siuN7-liau2 chin ki5- koai3, chiu7 mng7 i e5 peng5-iu2 kong2, Che si7  sim2-mih8 ian5-kou3?  I e5 peng5-iu2 kong2, KiaN  lin2 e5 mng5-khau2 hit chiah kau2 thai3 ok.    Tiam3 chu2-lang5 kong2, Kau2 ok an3-chaiN2-iuN7  oe7 hou7 chiu2 bo5 seng-li2?  I e5 peng5-iu2  kong2, Kau2 ok lang5 chiu7 m7-kaN2 khi3 lin3  hia.   Au7-lai5 tiam5-chu2 tui3 goa7-bin7 chhe  chit8 e5 gin2-na2 theh8 chiN5 koaN7 chiu2-pan5,  beh lai5 tah chiu2; hit chiah kau2 ko2-jian5  chau2 jip, beh khi3 ka7 i.   Hit e5 gin2-na2 kiaN  chit8-e7, chau2 kau2 be2-a2 tit8-khi3; chiah chai  chiu2 e5 bo5 lang5 tah, si7 ui7-tioh8 an2-ni e5 ian5-kou3.      
TaN Ia5-sou e5 to7-li2, boe7 kong2 tit m7-si7 ho2 e5 to7-li2, ia7  boe7 kong2 tit si7 bo5 kong-to7, ia7 boe7 kong2 tit bo5 eng7  ho2-le2 chih-chiap lang5, ia7 m7 si7 bo5 u7 ho2 e5 chio-pai5;  m7-ku2 iau2 u7 lang5 m7 kaN2 oa2--lai5.   Chit e5 ian5-kou3 sui- jian5 oe7 kong2 tit si7 bo5 siu7 Seng3-sin5 e5 kam2-tong7,  chong2-si7 hit tiong-kan, ia7 boe7 bian2-tit u7 tam7-poh8  si7 chhin-chhiuN7 hit ho7 ok kau2 e5 cho2-tong3.  So2-i2 hoan7-su7 tioh8 ka-ki7 choe3 ho2 sou2 kiaN5 e5 bo5-iuN7,  ti7 ka3-si7 tioh8 toan-chong bo5 sia5, gian5-gu2 toan-chiaN3  bo5 thang hiam5, ho7 tui3-tek8 ka-ki7 kian3-siau3, bo5 te3  thang kong2 lan2 e5 phaiN2( The5-to2¡G7, 8).        
Gau5 tu5 be5 sin3
Nng7 chheng ni5 cheng5 Tiong-kok u7 chit8- e5 lang5, hok8-siN3 Se-bun5, tan-mia5 kio3 Pa3,  choe3 Giap8-siaN5 e5 koaiN7-koaN.   Tng i khi3  chiap jim7 e5 si5, khoaN3-kiN3 hia e5 jin5-ian chin  hi-bi5, pah hang7 su7 long2 hong-hoe3; i chiu7  chha5-kho2 hit e5 goan5-in.   Chha5-liau2 chiu7 chai hia u7 chit8 cheng2 e5 phaiN2 hong-siok8, chiu7-si7 chit8-e5 ang-i5  
teh chok koai3.   In-ui7  chai7 hit sou2-chai7 u7 chit8 tiau5 ho5, tak8 ni5 khia7- chhiu e5 si5 ho5 chui2 chiu7 tiong3-khi2--lai5, ti3- kau3 im-tioh8 hia e5 lang5 e5 chhan5-hng5 chhu3- theh8 sun2-sit chin choe7.   Hit e5 lau7 ang-i5  siN chhut iau5-gian5 kong2 ho5-sin5 teh siu7-khi3,  tioh8 eng7 mih8 lai5 che3-hian3; ia7 tioh8 chiong  chit8 e5 be7 chhut-ke3 e5 cha-bou2 gin2-na2 chng  sui2-sui2, chiong lou5-tek pak8 choe3 chun5 hou7 i  che7, chiah ka7 i pang3 hou7 chui2 lau5 khi3;  lau5 bo5 loa7-hng7 chiu7 tim5-loh8--khi3, ho7 choe3  sang3 hou7 ho5-sin5 choe3 bou2.   Tak8 ni5 long2  tioh8 an2-ni.   Koh hia u7 saN e5 lau7-toa7, ia7  kap hit e5 ang-i5 tau3-khang; na7 khoaN3-kiN3  u7 chit8 e5 khah ho2-giah8 e5 lang5, in chiu7  kong2 i e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2 oe7 eng7-tit choe3 ho5- sin5 e5 bou2.   Hiah e5 ho2-giah8 lang5 kou3-tioh8 i  e5 kiaN2, chiu7 chiong chiN-gun5 lai5 mai2-chiok  in, in chiu7 tng2 chih8-koan kong2, ho5-sin5 m7  tihN8 chit e5, si7 ai3 hit e5.   So2-i2 ti3-kau3 ho2-giah8  lang5 long2 poaN-khi3 pat8 sou2-chai7; chhun  hiah e5 song3-hiong lang5.   Io3-koh tak8-ni5 u7  chui2-chai, sou2-i2 peh-siN3 chin kan-khou2.    Se-bun5 Pa3 i2-keng chai si7 an2-ni, siuN7 na7  beh eng7 chhui3 kong2 si7 bo5 lou7-eng7, in-ui7  cheng3 peh-siN3 be5 sin3 chin chhim, boe7  bian2-tit oe7 eng7 bo5 cheng5-li2 e5 oe7 lai5 pian7- lun7.   Chiu7 hoan-hu3 saN e5 lau5-toa7 kong2,  Na7 beh sang3 cha-bou2 gin2-na2 hou7 ho5-sin5  choe3 bou2 e5 si5, goa2 ia7 beh lai5 khi3 pai3 i;  tak8-e5 kong2, Ho2.     
Kau3 hit e5 si5, hit saN e5 lau7-toa7 ko2-jian5  lai5  chhiaN2 Se-bun5 Pa3 khi3 khoaN3.   KiaN5 kau3  ho5-piN e5 si5, khoaN3-kiN3 kang2-chheng lang5 oe-oe khoeh-khoeh teh theng3-hau7. Koh tiap-a2-ku2 chiah khoaN3-kiN3 hit e5 lau7 ang-i5 lai5, u7 si3 e5 tou5-te7 kun-sui5 i; ka-ki7 liah8 choe3  i si7 thoe3 sin5 pan7 su7,  put-chi2 kiau-ngou7 e5 khoan2.   Koh khoaN3 hit e5 beh hou7 ho5-sin5  choe3 bou2 e5 cha-bou2 gin2-na2, siN choe3 ia7 peng5-siong5.   Se-bun5 Pa3 chiu7 tiau3  hit e5 lau7 ang-i5 lai5 ka7 i kong2, Goa2 khoaN3 chit e5 cha-bou2 gin2-na2  bo5 sim2-mih8 sui2, theng3-hau7 goa2 keng2 chit8 e5 khah piau-ti3 e5 chiah ka7 i sang3  khi3, chhiaN2 li2 chiong goa2 e5 oe7 khi3 ka7 ho5-sin5 kong2.    Chiu7 bo5 iong5-un2 i ke kong2 oe7, kio3 nng7 e5 kun-lang5 ka7 I liah2-khi2-lai5  thiam7-loh8 ho5--nih8; i pun2-sin ia7 chng-choe3 chin sin3 e5 khoan2, cheng2-tun3 I-koan, eng7 khian5-seng5 lai5 khia7 ti7 ho5-piN, theng3-hau7 i to3-tng2 lai5 he5-hok.     
Kau3 u7 tiap-a2-ku2, bo5 khoaN3-kiN3 hit e5 lau7 ang-i5 to3-tog2-lai5,  chiu7 tui3 cheng3 lang5 kong2, chit e5 lau7 lang5 choe3 tai7-chi3 chin ban7, kau3 taN iau2-be7 to3-tng2-lai5.    
Chiu7 kio3 nng7  e5 siau3-lian5 e5 ang-i5 lai5, ka7 i kong2, Lin2 su-bu2 khah lau7 lah, choe3 tai7-chi3 chin ban7, li2  khi3 mng7 i khoaN3 ho5-sin5 kong2 an3-chaiN2-iuN7;  tioh8 liam5-piN to3-lai5 he5-hok goa2.   Chiu7  kio3 kun-lang5 koh ka7 in thoa-loh8-khi3.     
Keh cham2-jian5 ku2, iu5-goan5 bo5 tong7 bo5 cheng7; chiu7 tiau3 hit saN e5 lau7-toa7 lai5 kong2, Tau3-ti2 si7 hu7-jin5-lang5 long2 boe7 pan7-su7,  khi3-liau2 soa3 bo5 beh to3-tng2-lai5.   Lin2 saN lang5 khah lau2-lian7, tak8-hang7 tai7-chi3 khah oe7 hiau2-tit; chhian2 li2 chiong goa2 e5 i3-su3 khi3 ka7 ho5-sin5  kong2; tioh8 koaN2-kin2 lai5 he5-hok.   Ia7 bo5 iong5-un2 in hun-sou3, kio3  kun-lang5 long2 ka7 in thoa-khi3, thiam7 ti7 ho5--nih8.   Cheng3 peh-siN3  khoaN3-liau2 toa7 kiaN, Se-bun5 Pa3 iu5-goan5 ke2 choe3 chin  khian5-seng5 lai5 theng3-hau7; m7-ku2 ia7 si7 bo5 poaN3-lang5 oe7 to3-tng2-lai5 he5-hok.  Chiu7 koh tiau3 hiah e5 te7-po2 chhiam-siu2 lai5, ka7  in kong2, Goa2 khoaN3 hu7-jin5-lang5 kap lau7-lang5 long2 si7 bo5 lou7-eng7, tak8-e5 u7 khi3 bo5 he5- thau5; lin2 tiong-kan sim8-mih8 lang5 choe3 tai7- chi3 khah me2-liah8, tioh8 khi3 chhui-pek in.  Hiah e5 lang5 toa7 kiaN, tak8-e5 khap8-thau5  kiu5 kong2, Goan2 long2 m7-kaN2 lah.  Se-bun5  Pa3 chiu7 kong2, ChhiaN2 koh theng3-hau7  tiap-a2-ku2. Cheng3-lang5 sim-koaN phok8-phok8 chheng2, kha-chhiu2 ngiauh8-ngiauh8 chhoah.    Koh ke3 u7 hiah ku2, Se-bun5 Pa3 koh mng7 cheng3-lang5 kong2,  Lin2 phah-sng3 chaiN2-iuN7?   Tai7-ke kong2, Goan2 cheng5 long2 hou7 hit e5  ang-i5 phian3-khi3; taN m7 kaN2 lah.   Se-bun5 Pa3 chiah kong2, Au7-lai5  na7 u7 lang5 koh kong2 ho5-sin5 beh chhoa7 bou2, goa2 chiu7 beh eng7 i  khi3 choe3 hm5-lang5.   Tui3 an2-ni chiah kah cheng3-lang5 to3-khi3.     
Au7-lai5 Se-bun5 Pa3 khoaN3 hit e5 toe7-se3 e5 koaiN5-ke7, lai5 khui hit tiau5  ho5; sui-jian5 tu2-tioh8 khia7-chhiu, ia7 long2 bo5 chui2-chai, peh-siN3 long2 koh poaN to3-tng2-lai5, bo5 loa7-ku2 chiu7 chin heng-ong7.  U7 lang5 hiam5 kong2, Se-bun5 Pa3 eng7 an2-ni e5 hoat-tou7 si7 siuN ngi7,  bo5 u7 jin5-ai3.   Su7-put-ti chit kui2 e5 lang5 hai7 chin choe7 e5  peh-siN3, keng-ke3 kui2-na7 chap8 ni5 ku2, koaN-hu2 long2 bo5 hoat-tou7 thang  ti7; chiu7-si7 hou7 chit kui2 e5 si2, in e5 choe7 ia7 iau2 pou2 boe7 ke3,  ho5-hong3 koh oe7 tu5-khi3 au7-lai5 e5 ho7-hoan7.     
TaN hian7-si5 u7 koa2 hong-sui2 sian-siN, kap pok-koa3,  khoaN3-mia7 khoaN3-jit8 e5 lang5, kong2 in e5 sou2 toan3 si7  chin tioh8, bo5 chha bo5 chhok; lin2 chhiaN2 ban7 chiah  sin3 i, kio3 in ka-ki7 seng khi3 khoaN3  in e5 hong-sui2, sng3 in ka-ki7 e5 mia7-un7;  na7 ko2-jian5 u7 eng3-giam7, au7-lai5 chiah khi3 sin3 i ia7 be7 ti5.     
 
 
Chit-hi5 tiou3 toa7-tai7
Kou2-cha2 Chi-na2 chhit-kok e5 si5, Che5-kok  Ui-ong5 che7-ui7 te7 poeh ni5, Chhou2-kok u7  khi2 chin choe7 peng beh lai5 kong-phah  Che5-kok, Ui-ong5 chiu7 chhe Sun5-u Khun  khi3 Tio7-kok chhiaN2 kiu3-peng, ia7 sang3 Tio7- kok e5 gun5 chit8 pah kim kap si3 chap8 chiah  be2.   Sun5-u Khun m7 ho2 hiam5 ong5 e5 le2-mih8  siuN pok8, chiu7 toa7 chhio3, bo7-iaN ia7 lak--lok8- lai5.   Ong5 chiu7 mug7 kong2, Li2 hiam5 le2-mih8  khah khin mah?  Sun5-u Khun kong2, Sin5  m7 kaN2 hiam5.   Ong5 kong2, Li2 chhio3 siaN2-su7?   Sun5-u Khun chiu7 in3 i kong, Goa2 kin-a2-jit8  tui3 tang-peng5 hia lai5, khoaN3-kiN3 chit8 lang5  pai5 chit8 e5 ti-kha kap chit8 cheng chiu2, sio  hiuN teh he7 kong2, Kiu5 sin5 tioh8 po2-pi3, hou7  goa2 e5 koaiN5-chhan5 ke7-chhan5 long2 ho2 siu- seng5, hou7 goa2 e5 gou7-kak moa2-moa2 si7, toa7- pun7 lau5, soe3-pun7 tiN7, u7 thang chiah8 iah8 u7  thang thio3.   Goa2 khoaN3 I sou2 eng7 e5 mih8  chin chio2, i sou2 kiu5 e5 ng3-bang7 iu7 chin toa7,  sou2-i2 chiah chiah ai3 chhio3.     
Ui-ong5 chai i e5 i3-su3, chiu7 ke-thiN ng5- kim nng7 ban7 niu2, peh8-gek8 ji7 chap8 te3, be2  si3 pah phit, chhia ia7 kang2 pah tiuN.   Sun5- u Khun chiah jip8 Tio7-kok, ko2-jian5 chioh- tioh8 cheng-peng chap8 ban7, chian3-chhia  chit8 chheng tiuN.   Chhou2-kok e5 peng thiaN- liau8, thau3-mi5 koaN2-kin2 chau2 to3 khi3.     
Lun7 kau3 hian7-si5 pai3 ngou2-sing e5 lang5 si7 kap hit  e5 choh-chhan5 lang5 sio-siang7, ka-ki7 boe2 nng7 iN5-a2 kim  hiuN chek, a2-si7 pi7-pan7 tam7-poh8 bo5 iu5 bo5 iam5 e5 che3- mih2, taN kau3 bio7-lai7 khi3 hau3, siuN7 beh kiu5 chiN5-chai5,  kiu5 hok-khi3, a2-si7 kiu5 siN kiaN2.   Ho2 kai-chai3 si7 hit e5  ngou2-siong7 u7 bak8-chiu boe7 oe7 khoaN3, u7 hi7-khang boe7  oe7 thiaN, u7 phiN7-khang ia7 m7 chai chu-bi7.   Na7 beh  sio2-khoa2 u7 leng5-siaN3, a2-si7 u7 tam7-poh8 ti3-sek, khoaN3- kiN lang5 eng7 chit khoan2 chhou-siok8 e5 hiuN chek, bo5  iaN2 e5 kim-gun5, kap hiah e5 chiah8 boe7 jip8-chhui3 e5 che3- mih8, lai5 kiu5 it-khai3 e5 toa7 hok-khi3, khah ke ma7  chiong hit e5 lang5 ka7 i koaN2 chhut mng5 goa7, soa3  chek-pi7 hit e5 lang5 kong2, Li2 khoaN3 goa2 si7 thou5 chhiok8  chha5 khek e5, boe7 oe7 hun-piat chin-ke2 phang-chhau3,  chiah eng7 chit ho7 lai5 phian3 goa2 mah?  So2-i2 Seng3-keng u7 kong2, Lang5 keng3-pai3 Siong7-te3,  tek-khak tioh8 eng7 sim seng5-sit2 lai5 keng3-pai3 I.     
 
Tioh8 kiu5 ka-ki7
Kou2-cha2 Ha7-tiau5 e5 si5, u7 chit8 e5 ong5 mia5  Pek-khe2, kap Iu2-hou7 ti7 Kam-tek8 e5 sou2- chai7 sio thai5; Pek-khe2 thai5-su.   I e5  cheng3 jin5-sin5 chhiaN2 i koh cheng2-tun3  peng-be2 kap i kau-chian3.   Pek-khe2 kong2,  M7-bian2 koh chian3 lah; goa2 e5 toe7 ia7 boe7  khah chio2 I, peh-siN3 ia7 pi2 i khah choe7,  hoan2-tng2 si7 goa2 thai5-su, che tek-khak si7  goa2 e5 tek-heng7 m7 ho2, ka3-si7 ia7 m7 ho2.   Tui3  an2-ni Pek-khe2 chiu7 che7 ia7 bo5 kiu5 ho2 ui7,  chiah8 ia7 si7 bo5 chhe7 ho2 bi7, gak8-khi3 ia7 bo5 beh siu-li2, kiaN2-ji5 ia7 bo5 ka7 i chng-thaN7, koh  chun-keng3 si7-toa7, thiaN3-thang3 si7-soe3, keng2-soan2 gau5 lang5, lai5 tau3 liau7-li2 kok- su7.   TaN-chiah ke3 chit8 ni5 na7-tiaN7, hit e5 Iu2-hou7 soa3 ka-ki7 lai5 hang5 i.    
 TaN chit-tiap8 e5 lang5 teh thoan5-to7, mui2-mui2 kong2 lang5 e5 sim thai3 ngi7, bo5 hiah-nih8 khoai3 kam2-hoa3.   Goa2 khoaN3 chit ku3 oe7 ia7 bo5 tek-khak long2 an2-ni.   TaN ai3 tai7-seng chhiaN2 mng7 thoan5-to7--e5, to7-hah8 u7 joa7 chhim, cphin2-heng7 u7 joa7 ho2.   Na7 si7 ka-ki7 e5 to7-hak8 ia7 sio2-khoa2, phin2-heng7 ia7 bo5 thang o-lo2, chit8-e7 kong2- khi2 to7-li2, chhin3-chhai2 thoa-tang thoa-sai, put-tap  Put-chhit, lam7-sam2 kong2-long2 teh , chiu7 ka7 i ke3 khi3;  na7 choe3 tai7-chi3, chhut-chai7 in e5 i3-su3, koai7-phiah khek-pok8, bo5 chhun5 liong5-sim, goa2 na7 chit khoan2 e5 thoan5 to7-li2, goa2 kiam2 thang kong2 si7 lang5 e5 sim- koaN thai3 ngi7 mah?   Siok8-gu2 kong2, Chiong sim pi2 sim.   Koh kong2, Ka-ki7 si3-niu2-ng2 tioh8 tu5-khi2- lai5.   Na7 beh ka-ki7 bo5 hoaN-hi2 kang2-kiu3 Seng3-keng,  bo5 beh chiau3 Seng3-keng lai5 kiaN5, hoan2-tng2 khi3 khng3 lang5 tioh8 chha5-kho2 Seng3-keng, than3 Seng3-keng e5 oe7 lai5 kiaN5, an2-ni kiam2 m7 si7 chu7-siong man5-tun2 mah?  
KhoaN3 lang5 teh kong2 oe
7Chai7-cha2 Khong2-chu2 chhut-goa7 kiaN5-iu5,  be2 te3 bo5 tioh8 lou7, soa3 khi3 chiah8-tioh8 choh-chhan5 lang5 e5 tiu7-a2.  Hit e5  long5-hu siu7-khi3, chiong hit chiah be2 thoa khi3 eng7 soh-a2 pak8 teh.  Khong2-chu2 kio3 Chu2-kong3 khi3 tho2.  Chu2-kong3 eng7  khiam-sun3 le2-mau7 e5 bin7-sek, kap i kong2 chin choe7 ho2 oe7, ia7 ka7 i che7 m7-tioh8.   
Hit e5 long5-hu m7 heng5 i, Khong2-chu2 kong2, Goa2  chiau3 lang5 e5 hoat-tou7 ho2-ho2 ka7 i kong2, i khiok m7 thiaN; che si7 chhin-chhiuN7 eng7 seng-le2 teh khoan2-thai7 ia2-siu3, toaN5 gak8-khi3  hou7 chiau2 thiaN, sng3 si7 goa2 e5 m7 tioh8,m7-si7 i e5 m7 tioh8.  Chiu7 kah be2-hu khi3; hit e5 be2-hu chit8-e7 khoaN3-kiN3 choh-chhan5 lang5  chiu7 kong2, Li2 sou2 choh e5 chhan5, tui3 tang-hai2 kau3 sai-hai2,  goa2 e5 be2 chhut-lai5, beh tah8-loh8 khi3 chhe7 chiah8, chaiN2-iuN7 oe7 bian2-tit chiah8-tioh8 li2 e5 tiu7-a2 leh?  Hit e5 long5-hu thiaN-liau2 toa7 hoaN-hi2, chiu7 chiong be2 thau2 khi2-lai5, hou7 i khan to3-khi3.   
TaN lun7-kau3 lan2 e5 lang5 teh kau-chiap ong2-lai5, ia7 tioh8 i5-si5 che3-gi5, kian3 ki ji5 chok; na7 chip i chit8 e5 phiah, liah8 si2-pan2 lai5 choe3, tek-khak si7 bo5 li7-ek. Phi2-lun7 tang-thiN beh kau3, chiu7 tioh8 pi7-pan7 mi5-hiu5, he7-thiN tioh8 pi7-pan7 joah8-saN, chhui3-ta tioh8 pi7-pan7 te5 thng, iau tioh8 pi7-pan7 png7; che si7 tiaN7-tioh8 e5 li2- khi3.  Thoan5-to7 e5 iu5-goan5 tioh8 an2-ni.   Phi2-lun7 na7 kap thou2-thun2 m7 bat seng3-to7 e5 lang5 kong2, tioh8 eng7 khah khoai3 bat khah chhian2-hian7 e5 to7-li2, in chiah thiaN- liau2 oe7 beng5-pek8; na7 tu2-tioh8 khah su-bun5 e5 thak8- chheh-lang5, tioh8 eng7 khah chhim khah o3-biau7 e5 to7- li2, in thiaN-liau2 chiah oe7 jip8 hi7.  Siat-su2 na7 kap phok-hak8 su-bun5 e5 lang5, eng7 hit ho7 ha7-teng2 chhou- lou2 e5 oe7 kap i kong2, tu2-tioh8 iong5-hu siok8-chu2 hoan2- tng2 long7-khi2 bun5-bek8, an2-ni chiu7 hiah e5 su-bun5 lang5 thiaN-liau2 hoan2-tng2 oe7 khoaN3-khin, hiah e5 chhou-kha chhiah-chhiu2 e5, iu7 na2 chhin-chhiuN7 ah-a2 teh thiaN lui5, chu7-jian5 thiaN-liau2 chiu7 boe7 loh8 hi7, iah8 beh thai3 u7 kong-hau7 leh?  Kho2-kian3 thoan5-to7 e5 lang5, tioh8 e7 bun5, iah8 tioh8 oe7 bu2, u7 si5 chiau3 lan2 peng5- siong5, u7 si5 tioh8 eng7 bun5-nga2.  Sou2-i2 tong-si5 Po2-lo5 teh thoan5-to7, i si7 khoaN3 kau3 sim2-mih8 toe7-hng, tui3 sim2-mih8 ho7 lang5, eng-kai tioh8 kong2 sim2-mih8 oe7, long2 bo5 chip si2 koat.  Chhin-chhiuN7 Seng3-keng u7 kong2, M7 thang eng7 chin-chu hiat hou7 ti kau2.  Chim- chiok lai5 siuN7 chit e5 i3-su3, thang chai chin-chu u7  chin-chu e5 lou7-eng5, ti kau2 u7 ti kau2 e5 sou2 ai3; beh thai3 oe7 siang7 chit8 khoan2 lai5 gi7-lun7 tit leh?  
Siu2 tu thai7 tho3
Chong-chu2 u7 kong2, Song3-kok u7 chit8 e5 choh-chhan5 lang5, khoaN3-kiN3 chit8 chiah  chhiN-kiaN chau2 e5 thou3-a2, chong5-lai5 tong7- tioh8 chhiu7-tu soa3 si2-khi3.  Hit e5 choh-chhan5 lang5 chiu7 giau5-gi5 hit chang5 chhiu7-tu, si7 oe7 soah thou3, chiu7  
pang3-sak i keng-choh e5 su7, choan-kang lai5 toa3 chhiu7-tu e7 theng3- hau7, ng3-bang7 khoaN3 u7 thou3 oe7 chau2--lai5, thang hou7 lan2 khioh-tioh8.   
TaN lun7-kau3 thiN-kha-e7 e5 mih8, tak8-hang7 lan2 to u7 hun7, put-ko3 tioh8 eng7 ke3-chiN3 lai5 khi3 boe2, na7 kan-ta khoaN3 teh him-sian7 si7 bo5 lou7-eng7.  In-ui7 hian7-si5 e5 lang5 na7 khoaN3-kiN3 koan-ka chu2-te7, a2-si7 giap8-hou7 kiaN2- sun, tit-tioh8 in si7-toa7-lang5 e5 giap8-san2, kui jit8 chiah8- pa2 eng5-eng5, iah8 bo5 choe3 sim2-mih8 thau5-lou7, kan-ta si3- koe3 thit-tho5 hoaN-hi2 khoai3-lok8, chiu7 kong2, Hit-e5 si7 u7 toa3 sit8-lok8 lai5 chhut-si3, a2-si7 kong2, Thian-chai5 ka- ki7 lai5.  Che put-ji5-ko3 si7 kio3 lang5 m7 thang tui3-tiong7 chiN5 gun5 ke3-thau5.  M7 ku2 hit ho7 pin5-toaN m7 ai3 than3 e5 lang5 siong5-siong5 eng7 che lai5 kong2, ti3-kau3 gou7 lai5   gou7 khi3, ham7-hai7 m7-si7 sio2-khoa2.  An2-ni kiam2 bo5 kap  chit e5 Siu2-tu thai7-thou3 e5 lang5 siang7 khoan2 e5 gong7  mah?  Thai3 m7 siuN7 lang5 oah8 ti7 se3-kan, sui-jian5 thiN bo5 go7 lang5, ia7 tioh8 lan2 pun2-sin chhun-chhiu2 khi3 theh8 lai5 khng3 hit chhui3--nih8.  Ho5-hong3 Siong7-te3 siN lan2 u7 kha u7 chhiu2, si7 beh hou7 lan2 un7-tong7 choe3 tai7-chi3, m7-na7 pang-chan7 ka-ki7, ia7 ai3 hou7 pat8 lang5 tit- tioh8 li7-ek.  Siok8-gu2 u7 kong2, ThiN-toe7 iN5 lin-lin, chhoan3 go7 si7 toaN7 sin.  Koh lang5 sng3 si7 ban7-hang7 mih8 te7-it leng5-khiau2 e5, thai3 thang ka-ki7 chau5-that? Chiu7-si7 cheng-siN khim5-siu3 ma7 tioh8 si3-koe3 khi3 tho2 chiah8, boh8-kioh lang5 si7 te7-it hoat8-phoat e5; kiam2 u7 kong2, siN lan2 e5 seng-khu, si7 beh choe3 saN-a2 ke3, pak- tou2 si7 beh choe3 png7-tau2 na7-tiaN7?  Sui-jian5 chou2-chiuN7 u7 lau5 tam7-poh8 san2-giap8, kau3-giah8 hou7 lan2 chit8-si3- lang5 thang chiah8, chheng7, eng7, ia7 m7 thang kui-jit8 bu5 sou2 su7-su7.  Song3-tiau5 Liok8 Siong7-san u7 chit8 chhiu2 koa, chiu7-si7 choe3 lai5 ka3-si7 chit khoan2 e5 lang5; koa- nih8 kong2:   
ThiaN, thiaN, thiaN 
Hou7 goa2 tioh8-boa5 thiN chu3-tiaN7, 
Na7 beh pin5-toaN7 oe7 iau koaN5, 
M7-thang iau koaN5 chiah oan3-mia7, 
ThiN-nih8 sin5-beng5 u7 teh thiaN  
 
He2-chhiN oe7 sio goan5-ia2
Chi-na2 Liat8-kok e5 si5-tai7, Chhou2-kok e5 pian-kai3 Ti-liong5 e5 toe7-hng u7 chit8 e5 cha-bou2 gin2-na2, kap Gou5-kok  pian-kai3 e5 cha-bou2 gin2-na2 saN-kap chhai2-sng.  Gou5-kok e5 cha-bou2 gin2-na2 in-ui7 kun2-chhio3, gou7 siong-tioh8 Pi-liong5 e5 cha-bou2  gin2-na2.  Pi-liong5 e5 lang5 chiu7 chhoa7 hit e5 tioh8-siong e5 cha-bou2 gin2-na2 khi3 chek-pi7 Gou5-kok e5 lang5.  Gou5-kok e5 lang5 in-ui7 kong2  oe7 bo5 khiam-sun3, soa3 hou7 Pi-liong5 e5 lang5 ka7 i thai5 khi3.  Gou5- kok e5 lang5 au7-lai5 khi3 Pi-liong5 po3-siu5, chiong hit e5 lang5 choan5-ke  ka7 i thai5-si2 liau2-liau2.  Pi-liong5 e5 toe7-hng koaN thiaN-liau2 chin siu7-khi3 kong2, Gou5-kok e5 lang5 ho2 toa7-taN2, chiah8 goa2 chin kau3, chiu7 nia2 peng khi3 kong-kek i, bo5 lun7 lau7-e5 chiN2-e5 it-chin7 chau5-biat8.   
Tng hit si5 Gou5-ong5 I5-mui7 thiaN-kiN3 chit e5 tai7-chi3, ia7 toa7 siu7-khi3, chiu7 hoat peng khi3 kong-phah chhou2-kok e5 siaN5-ti5.  Tui3 an2-ni Gou5, Chhou2 nng7 kok chiu7 tiaN7-tiaN7 sio-thai5.  Gou5-kok chiu7 phai3 Kong-chu2 Kong nia2 peng khi3 cheng Chhou2-kok, ti7 Koe-hu2 e5 toe7-hng toa7 sio-thai5; Chhou2-peng thai5-su, lian5 goan5-soe3 chiong3-koaN, u7-e5 si2, u7-e5 hou7 liah8 khi3.  Gou5-peng soa3 khi3 kong- phah Chhou2-kok e5 kiaN-siaN5.  Kai-chai3 Chhou2-ong5 chau2 li7, ki5-u5 e5 thou2-toe7 long2 hou7 in chiam3 khi3.  Au7-lai5 Chhou2-kok e5 jin5-sin5 jip8 Chin5-kok khi3 chioh peng lai5 khek-hok8 Chhou2-kok e5 toe7.  Chhou2-ong5  in-ui7 keng-ke3 chit pai2 e5 thai5-su, chiu7 eng7 sim lai5 pan7 kok e5 cheng3-su7, thiaN3-thang3 i e5 peh-siN3, keng3-tiong7 i e5 jin5-sin5; kau3 kui2 chap8 ni5 au7,  Gou5-kok ia7 hou7 Chhou2-kok biat8-khi3.   
Siok8-gu2 kong2, Sio2-khoa2 m7 pou2, toa7 khang chiu7 kan-khou2.  Chit8 liap8 chit8 liap8 e5 he2-chhiN na7 bo5 hoa, oe7 sio pian3 soaN-ia2.  Chit8 tih chit8 tih e5 chui2-choaN5 na7 bo5 soah, oe7 piN3-chiaN5 kang-ho5.  Bo5 lun7 si7 sio2-khoa2 e5 tai7-chi3, tioh8 siat-hoat hou7 kui tiok8, m7 thang chhut- chai7 i un7-tong7, kau3 chit8-e7 hoat-choh e5 si5, soa3 boe7 siu-sip8 tit.  Chhin-chhiuN7 Au-chiu chit nng7 ni5 e5 toa7 kau-chian3, kiam2 m7 si7 tui3 O3-kok Hong5-thai3-chu2 e5 khi2-in mah?  Hoe7-iu2 e5 choe3 su7, koh tioh8 chin soe3-ji7, m7 thang liah8 choe3 sio2-khoa2 lai5 bo5 kin2-sin7, kiaN-liau2 oe7 toa7-toa7 chou2-tong3 kau3-hoe7 e5 chin3-pou7.     
 
U7 le2-sou3 e5 tit-tioh8 siuN2
Chai7-cha2 Liat8-kok e5 si5, Tio7 Siong-chu2 Kap Ti3 Pek put-bok8, bo5 joa7-ku2 soa3 jia2- Khi2 kau-chian3.  Siong-chu2 tong3 boe7 tiau5, peng pai7 chau2 jip8 Chin3-iong5 siaN5, hou7 Ti3 Pek ui5-khun3 chin ku2.  Au7-lai5 khui-tit i e5 chham-bou5 TiuN Beng7-tam5 ho2-taN2 khi3 kiN3 Han5, Gui7, nng7 lang5, soe3 in lai5 poan7 Ti3 Pek, kap Siong-chu2 lian5-hap8, hoan2-tng2 kong-phah Ti3 Pek, kau3 Ti3 Pek biat8 khi3 liau2.  Teh siuN2-su3 kong-sin5 e5 si5, khiok si7 Ko Hek tit-tioh8 siong7-teng2 siuN2.  Beng7- tam5 siuN7 m7 chhut, chiu7 kong2, Ti7 Chin3- tong5 siaN5 e5 su7, Ko Hek ia7 bo5 taa8 kong-lo5, an3-chaiN2-iuN7 i siuN2 siong7-teng2?  Siong-chu2 in3 i kong2, Goa2 ti7 Chin3-iong5 e5 si5, kok-ka chin gui5-hiam2, goa2 e5 ui7 long2 boe7 po2-tit, cheng3 jin5-sin5 e5 tiong-kan, chiu7 tak8 e5 long2 u7 kiau-ngou7 bu2-ban7 goa2 e5 i3-su3, chi2-u7 Ko Hek iu5-goan5 chin khiam-pi, bo5 sit kun- sin5 e5 le2-sou3; sou2-i2 chiah siuN2 i siong7-teng2.     
Hit si5 Khong2-chu2 thiaN-kiN3 chit ho7 oe7, chiu7 kong2, An2-ni chin ho2; Siong-chu2 siuN2 chit e5 lang5, chiu7 thiN-kha-e7 choe3 jin5- sin5 e5, long2 m7 kaN2 sit-le2 lah.     
TaN se3-kan lang5 tai7-khai3 long2 si7 an2-ni; na7 hit e5  lang5 u7 chai5 u7 se3 thang hou7 kho3, lang5 chiu7 pah-poaN lai5 hong7-seng5, chin gau5 phou5-thaN2; iah8 na7 hit e5 lang5 khah sit se3, a2-si7 chiN5 i2-keng liau2, lang5 chiu7 hoan2- tng2 kong2 i e5 si7-hui, leng7-goa7 chit khoan2 e5 bin7-bak8 teh khoan2-thai7 i.  Chit khoan2 e5 lang5 siang7 te7-it choe7.  Ia5-sou u7 kong2, Lang5 ti7 Siong7-te3 e5 bin7-cheng5, tak8-hang7 tai7-chi3 long2 tioh8 khiam-pi, chiah oe7 tit- tioh8 Siong7-te3 e5 siuN2-su3; na7 kiau-ngou7 chu7-khoa, sui-jian5 u7 kong-lo3, ia7 bo5 tek-khak oe7 tit-tioh8 Siong7-te3 e5 siuN2-su3.  Sou2-i2 Hoat-li7-sai3 lang5 e5 ki5-to2, boe7 oe7 siu7- tioh8 hoaN-hi2 chiap-lap8; na7-si7 thiu-hiong3 e5 lang5 teh ki5-to2, hoan2-tng2 tit-tioh8 Siong7-te3 aN3-loh8-lai5 thiaN i.     
 
Sui5-ki eng3-pian3
Kou2-cha2 u7 chit8 e5 beng2 lang5, kio3 choe3 Pian7 Chong, khoaN3-kiN3 u7 nng7 chiah hou2 kong-ke chiah8 chit8 chiah gu5.  Pian7 Chong chiu7 beh khi3 phah hit nng7 chiah  hou2; u7 kun toe3 i e5 lang5 kong2, ChhiaN2 ban7 chiah; hou2 sng3 si7 beng2-siu3, gu5 si7 ho2 chiah8 e5 mih8.  Hian7-chai7 nng7 chiah hou2, saN-kap chiah8 chit8 chiah gu5, gu5 ki3-jian5 si7 ho2 e5 chiah8-mih8, nng7 chiah hou2 tek-khak oe7 saN- chiN chiah8; na7 saN-chiN chiah8, chiu7 oe7 sio- ka7; iah8 sio-ka7 liau2 toa7 chiah-e5 oe7 tioh8- siong, soe3 chiah-e5 oe7 si2.  Li2 theng3-hau7 tiap-a2-ku2, thai5 chit8 chiah tioh2-siong e5 hou2, kiam2 bo5 it-ku2 liong2-tek mah?  An2-ni li2 chiu7 m7-bian2 phah hou2 e5 lo5-khou2, koh tit-tioh2 thai5-si2 nng7 chiah hou2 e5 ho2 mia5-siaN.  Pian7 Chong chiu7 theng3-hau7 bo5 tiap-a2-ku2, ko2-jian5 nng7 chiah hou2 saN-chiN chiah8 soa3 sio-ka7, soe3 chiah-e5 ka7 kau3 beh-si2 beh-si2, toa7 chiah-e5 ia7 tioh8 tang7 siong.  Pian7 Chong chiah oa2 khi3 chiong nng7 chiah long2 tuh8--si2; kng to3-lai5 e5 si5, lang5 m7-chai, chin o-lo2 i, kong2 i chit8 e5 lang5 phah-si2 nng7 chiah hou2, hit e5 mia5-siaN chiu7 chin thau2.     
TaN bo5 lun7 toh-loh8 chit8 teng2 e5 lang5 teh choe3 tai7-chi3, m7 thang it-bi7 kho3 iong2-beng2, sai2 seng3-te7, ngi7-ngi7 beh choe3; long2 tioh8 sui5-ki eng3-pian3, khoaN3 si5-se5 chiah thang tin2-tang7, chiu7 khah m7 bian2 hui3 siuN choe7 e5 khui3-lat8, koh seng5-kong ia7 toa7.  
Chin gau5 chhu2 po2
Chhou2-kok u7 chit8 e5 lang5, siN3 Pian7 mia5 Ho5, ti7 soaN-nih8 tit-tioh8 chit8 te3 chhou gek8, chiu7 theh8 khi3 hian3 hou7 Chhou2-kok Le7-ong5, ka7 i kong2,lai7 bin7 u7 po2 gek8, Le7-ong5 kio3 tok-gek8 e5 sai-hu7 lai5 khoaN3; hit e5 sai- hu7 kong2, Si7 chit8 te3 chioh8-thau5, thai3 u7 sim2-mih8 ki5-kha2?  Le7-ong5 kong2 Pian7 Ho5 si7 khi-phian3 i, chiu7 chiong to3-kha ka7 cham7-khi2-lai5.  Au7-lai5 Le7-ong5 si2-khi2, Bu2- ong5 soa3-chiap lai5 che7 ui7.  Pian7 Ho5 koh chiong hit te3 chhou-gek8  theh8 khi3 hian3 hou7 Bu2-ong5.  Bu2-ong5 iu5-goan5 tiau3 gek8-kang lai5 khoaN3, ia7 kong2 siN7 chioh8-thau5.  Bu2-ong5 ia7 kong2 i si7 khi kun, chiong chiaN3-kha ia7 ka7 cham7-khi2-lai5.  Ke3 bo5 joa7-ku2, Bu2- ong5 ia7 si2, chiu7 oaN7 Bun5-ong5 teh che7 ui7.  Chit e5 Pian7 Ho5 chiah chiong hit te3 gek8 theh8 khi3 ti7 soaN-kha, ti7 hia tit-tit khau3, chiok-chiok u7 saN-mi5 saN-jit8, sim7-chi3 bak8-sai2  
lau5-liau2, soa3 lau5 huih chhut-lai5.  Bun5-ong5 chiu7 kio3 lang5 khi3 mng7 i, Si7 sim2-mih8 ian5-kou3?  Kok-lai7 e5 lang5 siu7 cham7-kha e5 heng5-hoat8 si7 chin choe7, li2 siaN2-su7 khau3 kau3 chit khoan2 e5 chham2-chhoeh?  Pian7 Ho5 chiah kong2, Goa2 m7 si7 in-ui7 teh khau3 goa2 e5 kha cham7-khi2-lai5, si7 in-ui7 beng5-beng5 si7 po2-gek8, lai5 liah8 choe3 si7 chioh8-thau5, hian7-hian7 si7 lau2-sit8 oe7, ka7 liah8 choe3 kong2 peh8-chhat8; sou2-i2 khau3-liau2 chiah oe7 chiah-nih thong3-sim lah.  Ong5 thiaN-kiN3 che  oe7, chiu7 phai3 tok-gek8 e5 sai-hu7, lai5 boa5 hit  te3 chioh8-thau5, ko2-jian5 lai7-bin7 hian2 chhut po2-gek8, soa3 chiong hit te3 gek8 mia5 kio3 Ho5--si7 e5 phek.  Kau3 Chin5 Si2-hong5 e5 si5, Chiong hit te3 phek khek choe3 Hong5-te3 in3; au7-lai5 liu5-thoan5 choe3 kok-po2.     
TaN Ia5-sou e5 to7-li2, kiam2 m7 si7 bo5 te3 thang chhu2 e5 po2 mah?  Ia5-sou u7 kong2, Thian-kok si7 chhin-chhiuN7 khng3 ti7 hng5-nih8 e5 po2-poe3, lang5 khoaN3-kiN3, chiu7 chiong i sou2 u7 e5 khi3 boe7, lai5 boe2 hit te3 hng5.  Kho2-sioh lang5 m7 na7 m7 bat si7 po2, hoan2-tng2 eng7 choe7-choe7 hang7 lai5 hui2-pong3.  Kau3-hoe7 chhou-siat e5 si5, tu2-tioh8 chin choe7 e5 khun2-tiok8, siu7 chin choe7 e5 leng5-jiok8; m7 na7 chhin-chhiuN7 Pian7 Ho5 hou7 lang5 cham7 kha na7-tiaN7, sim-chi3u e5 pang3-sak siN3-mia7 lai5 kan-cheng3 to7-li2.  Kai-chai3 thoan5-to7 e5 lang5 long2 bo5 loe2-chi3, thau5-cheng5-e5 poah8-loh8-khi3, au7-bin7-e5 koh chan7-khi2-lai5.  Sou2-i2 chit-tiap8 kau3-hoe7 u7 thang chiah-nih heng-ong7.  Siat-su2 lang5 na7 oe7 chhin- chhiuN7 Chhou2 Bun5-ong5 e5 khoan2, chim-chiok lai5 chhui2-mou5, chin ke2 liam5-piN chiu7 beng5-pek8.    
Sian7 iu2 sian7 po3
Chai7-cha2 Song3-kok u7 chit8 ke-khau2 put- chi2 gau5 choe3 ho2-su7, tak8-hang7 chiau3 jin5-ai3 kong-gi7 lai5 kiaN5.  Keng-ke3 saN te7 lang5 long2 bo5 koe2-oaN7.  Au7-lai5 in chhu3-nih8 u7 chit8 chiah ou-gu5 hut-jian5 siN chit8 chiah peh8 e5 gu5-a2-kiaN2.  Chiu7 khi3 mng7 Khong2-chu2; Khong2-chu2 kong2, Che si7 ho2 e5 tiau7-thau5, thang eng7 lai5 che3-hian3 Siong2-te3.  Ke3 u7 chit8 ni5 ku2, in lau7-pe7 e5 bak8-chiu ia7 bo5 choe3 thiaN3, hut-jian5-kan chhiN-mi5 khi3.  Hit chiah ou-gu5 iu7-koh siN chit8 chiah peh8 gu5-a2-kiaN2. In lau7-pe7 kah in kiaN2 khi3 mng7 Khong2- chu2; in kiaN2 chiu7 in3 i kong2, Ku7-ni5 khi3 mng7 i, kong2-liau2 ia7 bo5 iaN2, koh hoan2-tng2 li2 e5 bak8-chiu ia7 bo5 khoaN3-kiN3, mih-sai2 koh khi3 mng7 i?   In lau7-pe7 chiu7 kong2, Seng3-jin5 e5 oe7 sui-jian5 chiam7-si5 be7 eng3-giam7, au7-lai5 tek-khak u7 eng2-hiong2; tai7-chi3 iau2-be7 liau2, li2 thang khi3 mng7 i.   
I e5 kiaN2 chiu7 koh khi3 mng7 Khong2-chu2; Khong2-chu2 iu5-goan5 kong2 si7 ho2 tiau7-thau5, kah in khi3 hian3-che3 hou7 Siong7-te3.  In kiaN2 to3-lai5 ka7 in lau7-pe7 kong2, iu5-goan5 chiau3 Khong2-chu2 e5 oe7 khi3 kiaN5; koh ke3 chit8 ni5, lian5 in kiaN2 e5 bak8-chiu ia7 soa3 chhiN-mi5.     
Au7-lai5 Chhou2-kok nia2 peng lai5 kong- Phah Song3-kok, chiong siaN5-ti5 ui5-khun3 chin ku2, niu5-chhau2 chiah8 kau3 long2 chin7, peh-siN3 chiong in e5 kiaN2 oaN7 pat8 lang5 e5 kiaN2 thai5 khi2-lai5 chiah8; in ui7 ka-ki7 siN e5, thai5 boe7  loh8 chhiu2.  Bo5 chha5-liau7 chiu7 eng7 si2-lang5 e5 kut-thau5 lai5 hiaN5; oe7 sio-thai5 e5, long tioh8 khi3 kap tui3-tek8 chiap-tin7;  lang5 si2 chit8 poaN3 khah ke, khoaN3 he chham2 a8 m7 chham2?  Kai-chai3 in pe7-a2-kiaN2 in-ui7 long chhiN-mi5, bo5 tiau3 khi3 choe3 peng, chiah bo5 tu2-tioh8 chit ho7 e5 kan-khou2.  Kau3 au7-lai5 Chhou2-peng the3-khi3, in pe7-a2-kiaN2 e5 bak8- chiu ia7 soa3 ho2-lo2-khi3 lah.  
Koh chit8 hang7, Iong5 Hou2 ti7 Lou2-kok choe3 jiau2-loan7 e5 si5, Lou2-kok e5 jin5-kun beng7-leng7 chiong siaN5-mng5 koaiN-khi2-lai5; na7 liah8 tioh8 Iong5 Hou2 e5, beh tang7-tang7 siuN2 in, na7 pang3 hou7 chau2-khi2, chiu7 beh  tang7-tang7 pan7 in e5 choe7.  Iong5 Hou2 hou7 lang5 ui5-khun3 ti7 lai7-bin7, boe7 tit chhut khi3, chiu7 siuN7 beh eng7 khiam3 koah au5 lai5 chu7- chin7.  U7 chit8 e5 kou3 siaN5-mng5 e5 ka7 i kong2, ThiN-kha-e7 e5 lou7 chin choe7, mih-sai2 tioh8 an2-ni lai5 kiaN5 te2-lou7; goa2 pang3 li2 chhut khi3.  Iong5 Hou2 chiu7 kiah8 kiam3 theh8 chhiuN, phah chhut ui5-goa7 lai5, chau2 kau3 siaN5-mng5 kha, kou3 siaN5-mng5 e5 chiu7 ka7 i  khui.  Iong5 Hou2 beh chhut siaN5 e5 si5, hoan2-tng2 eng7 chhiuN tui3 kou3 siaN5-mng5-e5 e5 chhiu2-tou2 tuh8 chit8 khang.  Hit e5 kou3 siaN5- mng5 e5 sim-lai7 am3-chiN7 oan3-hun7 kong2, Chit e5 lang5 ia7 chin bo5 gi7, goa2 piaN3-mia7 lai5 pang3 i chhut khi3, i hoan2-tng2 ka7 goa2 tuh8 chit8-e7, chit ho7 lang5 tu2-tioh8 chit ho7 e5 chai- eh, sng3 si7 eng-kai.      
Au7-lai5 Lou2-kok e5 jin5-kun thiaN-kiN Iong5 Hou2 i2-keng chau2 chhut siaN5 goa7, chiu7 toa7 siu7-khi3, mng7 khoaN3 tui3 sim2-mih8 siaN5-mui5 to5-chau2, chiu7 chiong kou3 siaN5-mng5 e5 long2- chong2 liah8 lai5; na7 khoaN3 u7 tioh8-siong e5, chiu7 kong2 si7 u7 kap Iong5 Hou2 ti2-tek8 tong3 boe7 tiau5, an2-ni tioh8 tang7-tang7 siuN2 in; bo5 tioh8 siong e5, chiu7 gi5 in m7 kheng2 chhut- lat8, a2-si7 thau pang3 i chau2, long2 ka7 i tang7-tang7 heng5-hoat8.   
TaN Seng3-keng u7 kong2, Hoan7-su7 long2 kap sin3 Chu2 e5 lang5 u7 li7-ek.  An2-ni thang chai lang5 ti7 chit se3-kan, long2 tioh8 chin7-sim chun-than3 to7-li2 lai5 choe3 tai7-chi3, bo5 lun7 tu2-tioh8 sim2-mih8 hoan7-lan7 kan-khou2, a2-si7 siu7-tioh8 sim2-mih8  
chhi3-lian7, boe7-oe7 kong2-tit m7-si7 ka-ki7 u7 li7-ek e5 sou2-chai7.  Kho2-sioh u7 chit8 khoan2 chhian2-kian3 e5 lang5, na7 tu2-tioh8 khah bo5 chheng3-i3 e5 su7, a2-si7 gu7- tioh8 sio2-khoa2 e5 chhi3-lian7, chiu7 oan3-thiN hun7-toe7, loe2 chit-e5, me7 hit-e5, kong2 thiN bo5 bak8-chiu, lang5 bo5 kong-to7, sian7-sim to2 teh go7, ok-sim ti3 se-bo7.  Khiok m7 chai sou2 tu2-tioh8 e5 hoan7-lan7 kap sou2 siu7 e5 chhi3-lian7, chiaN3 si7 i pun2-sin toa7-toa7 u7 li7-ek e5 sou2-chai7. 
Ki5-koai3 e5 tai7-chi3
SaN chheng ni5 cheng5, Chiu Bu2-ong5 khi2 peng hoat8 Tiu7-ong5.  Kau3 tek-seng3 to3-lai5 e5 si5, u7 tiau3 nng7 e5 siu7 liah8 e5 peng-a2 lai5. Bu2-ong5 mng7 in kong2, Lin2 kok-nih8 u7 chhut sim2-mih8 ki5-koai3 e5 su7 bo5?  Chit8 e5 peng-a2 kong2, Goan2 kok-lai7 ki5-koai3 e5 tai7- chi3, chiu7-si7 chheng-thian pek8-jit8 khoaN3- kiN3 thiN-teng2 e5 chhiN, iah8 loh8 ang5-hou7 chhin-chhiuN7 loh8 huih e5 khoan2.  Iau2 chit8 e5 peng-a2 kong2, Chit e5 tai7-chi3 sui-jian5 si7 ki5-koai3, sng3 si7 sio2-khoa2; goan2 kok-nih8 te7 it toa7 ki5-koai3 e5 tai7-chi3, chiu7-si7 kiaN2-ji5 m7 thiaN lau7-pe7 e5 oe7, sio2-ti7 m7 thiaN hiaN-ko e5 oe7, jin5-sin5 m7 thiaN kun-ong5 e5 oe7, chit ho7 chiah thang sng3 si7 toa7 ki5-koai3 e5 tai7-chi3. Bu2-ong5 thiaN-kiN3 chit ho7 oe7, chiu7 ngiauh- khi2-lai5, ka7 hit e5 peng-a2 kiaN5 chit8 e5 toa7 le2. Che Bu2-ong5 m7 si7 chun-keng3 hit e5 liah8 lai5 e5 peng-a2, si7 chun-keng3 i sou2 kong2 e5 oe7.   
TaN lan2 chia e5 hu7-jin5-lang5, beng5-beng5 si7 thiN siN chu7-jian5 chit8 siang oe7 kiaN5 oe7 chau2 e5 ho2 kha, khiok  tian-to3 hui3 chin choe7 sim-sin5, siu7 chin choe7 kan- khou2 thang3-thiaN3, lai5 pak8 kau3 soe3-soe3-soe3, phaiN2 kiaN5 phaiN2 tah8, na2 chhin-chhiuN7 tai3-chit8 e5 khoan2.  Koh chit8 hang7 beng5-beng5 si7 te7-it tok8, chin khou2 chin kui3 e5 a-phian3 hun, khioh ka7 i khoaN3 choe3 thng5-tiN bit8-tiN e5 mih8.  Cha2-cha2 am3-am3, chhit-chong5 peh- chong5, ia7 si7 beh ou2 lai5 chiah8, kheng-ka tong7-san2, bou2-kiaN2 pang3-lang3 teh, ia7 bo5 iau3-kin2.  Iah8 koh beng5-beng5 si7 chit8 sin hit ho7 thou5 chhiok8, a2 si7 chha5 khek, choa2 kou5 e5 mih8,u7 bak8-chiu boe7 khoaN3, u7 hi7- khang boe7 thiaN, u7 chhui3 boe7 kong2 oe7, bo5 leng5 bo5 siaN3 e5 ngou2-siong7, khiok bo5 lun7 si7 chun-kui3, ha7- chian7, song3-hiong, ho2-giah8, ta-pou, cha-bou2, lau7-lang5 gin2-na2, gong7-e5 sek-e5, tak8 teng2-ho7 e5 lang5 long2 teh  liau2 chiN5 liau2 kang khi3 keng3-pai3 i.  Che kiam2 m7 si7 lan2 chia ia7 saN hang7 te7 it toa7 ki5-koai3 e5 tai7-chi3 mah?   
 
Kou3 cheng5 bo5 kou3 au7
Chong Chiu ti7 Tiau-leng5 e5 sou2-chai7 teh  kiaN5-iu5, khoaN3-kiN3 tui3 lam5-hng u7 chit8  chiah chhiok-chiau2 pe lai5, sit8 tng5 u7 chhit chhioh, bak8-chiu e5 toa7 beh kau3 chit8 chhun3; pe lai5 e5 si5, tui3 Chong Chiu e5 thau5- khak ka7 khap8 chit8-e7, chiah pe khi3 hioh  ti7 bin7-thau5-cheng5 e5 lat8-chi2 chhiu7 nih8. Chong Chiu chiu7 kong2, Che si7 sim2-mih8 chiau2, sit8 sui-jian5 tng5.  thai3 boe7 liam5- chiap8, bak8-chiu hiah toa7, khiok bo5 beng5- lang2?  Chiu7 bi oa2 khi3, siuN7 beh eng7 toaN7- chi2 ka7 toaN7.  Hut-jian5 khoaN3-kiN3 chit8 chiah am-pou5-che5, hioh ti7 chhiu7-teng2 im3-ng2 e5 sou2-chai7, toa7-soe3 siaN thi5 kau3 put-chi2 ho2 thiaN, chhin-chhiuN7 chin tek-koat e3 khoan2; khiok m7 chai au7-bin7 u7 chit8 chiah chhau2-kau5 beh lai5 liah8 i.  Hit chiah chhau2-kau5 kou3 so5 oa2 beh khi3 liah8 am-pou5- che5; khiok m7 chai au7-bin7 hit chiah chhiok-chiau2 khoaN3-kiN3, ia7 thiau3 oa2 lai5 beh tok i.  Hit chiah chhiok-chiau2 beh tok hit be2 chhau2-kau5 e5 si5, ia7 m7 chai Chong Chiu eng7 toaN7-chi2 beh ka7 i toaN7. Chong Chiu khoaN3 chit ho7 khoan2-sit,  chiu7 chiah8 chit8 kiaN, chiah thou2-khui3 kong2, Se3-kan tak8 hang7 to si7 an2-ni, long2 si7 kou3 ti7 bak8-chiu cheng5 e5 li7-ek, bo5 kou3 au7-bin7 e5 ham7-hai7; goa2 na7 kan-ta kou3 beh toaN7 hit chiah chiau2, m7 chai au7-bin7 u7 hou2 a2-si7 sai beh lai5 ka7 goa2 a2 bo5.  Chiu7 chiong toaN7-chi2 kap keng siu-khi2-lai5, koaN2-kin2 chau2 to3-khi3.    
TaN lun7-kau3 se3-kan lang5, tai7-khai3 long2 si7 an2-ni; u7-e5 kho3 i kiong5-beng2 lai5 khi-hu7 nng2-chiaN2, u7-e5 si7- toa7 khi-hu7 si7-soe3, a2-si7 ho2-giah8 khi-hu7 song3-hiong, chun-kui3 leng5-jiok8 pi-chian7; chi2-u7 kou3 bak8-chiu- cheng5 e5 khoaN3-oah8, long2 bo5 kou3 au7-lai5 e5 ho7-hoan7. Thai3 m7 siuN7 bo5 lun7 hou7 lan2 an2-chaiN2-iuN7 e5 u7 se3-lek8, an2-chaiN2-iuN7 e5 hu3-kui3, ia7 iau2 u7 chit8-e5 koh-khah kiong5, koh khah toa7, te7-it hu3-kui3 e5, khia7 ti7 lan2 e5 ka-chiah-au7 teh kam-tok lan2?  Siok8-gu2 kong2, Ok be2 ok lang5 khia5; koh kong2, Lang5 beh hai7 lang5 ThiN m7-kheng2, ThiN beh hai7 lang5 ti7 bak8-cheng5. Lang5 na7 siuN7 kau3 tui3 thiN-nih8 u7 Siong7-te3 teh kam3- chhat, chiu7 ka-ki7 e5 choe7, to bo5 te3 thang siam2-pi7, beh thai3 u7 eng5 thang khi3 khi-hu7 lang5 leh?    
Kho3 se3 hou7 se3 gou7
Chhong Chu2 e5 chheh u7 kong2, Gou5 ong5 u7 chit8 jit8 toa3 chin choe7 kun-lang5, chiuN7- khi3 chit8 cho7 kau5 soaN, khoaN3-kiN3 soaN-teng2 chin choe7 kau5, put-chi2 hoaN-hi2.  Hiah e5 kau5 khoaN3-kiN3 kui kun5 e5 lang5 lai5, chiu7 si3- soaN3 lam7-sam2 chau2, bih tui3 chhiu7-na5 lai7 jip8 khi3.  Tok8-tok8 iau2 u7 chit8 chiah kau5, chu7-chu7 chai7-chai7, long2 bo5 kiaN-hiaN5, ti7 Gou5 ong5 e5 bin7-cheng5, chhin-chhiuN7 beh tian2 i e5 pun2-su7.  Hit si5 Gou5 ong5 chiu7 hoat chit8 ki chiN3, siong3 cheng-cheng tui3 hit chiah kau5, ka7 i sia7-khi3.  Kau5 khoaN3- kiN3 Gou5 ong5 choh8 lai5 e5 chiN3 put-chi2 kin2, i ia7 bo5 chhiN-choh8, bo5 kiaN-hiaN5, ho2-le2 ho2- le2 tui3 hit ki chiN3 chiap-khi3-lai5.  Gou5 ong5 khoaN3-kiN3 an2-ni, chiu7 hoan-hu3 kun-lang5 tai7-ke koaN2-kin2 lai5 ka7 i choh8, liam5-piN chiong hit chiah kau5 ka7 sia7 si2.   
Lun7 kau3 se3-kan chiu2, sek, chai5, khi3, i2-kip2 oe7 hou7 lang5 hoan7-choe7 e5 tai7-chi3, long2 si7 kui2-ong5 e5 tok8 chiN3.  Na7 beng5-pek8 to7-li2 e5 lang5, eng-kai tioh8 liong7- cha2 siam2 hou7 hng7-hng7.  Siat-su2 ka-ki7 kho3 i chhong- beng5, tiau5-i3 ai3 kap kui2 ong5 choe3-sng2 kun2-chhio3, i na7 chiN3 lai5.  goa2 chiu7 chhun-chhiu2 lai5 khi3 chiap i. Che kiam2 m7 si7 beng5-beng5 ka-ki7 beh khi3 tho2 si2 mah? An2-ni thau5-mng5 teh chhi3 he2, tek-khak si7 bo5 thang lau5 teh.   
Goa2 ia7 u7 nng7-saN e5 peng5-iu2, ti7 chap8 ni5 cheng5 e5 si5, i khoaN3 pat8 lang5 teh chiah8 a-phian3 hun, chiu7 ai3 oa2 khi3 bak; goa2 chiu7 siong5-siong5 teh kah in m7 thang piN3 hit ho7.  In tai7-ke sou2 in3 si7 chhin-chhiuN7 put-chi2 u7 pa2-chhi5 e5 khoan2, kong2 in phah phun5 choe7 ni5 lah, tek-khak m7 bian2 kiaN oe7 tiau5.  Bo5 siuN7 chit kui2 ni5 lai5, tak8 e5 long2 tiau5 chin toa7, tai7-ke  khiok ia7 chai tioh8 koe2, m7 ku2 koe2 long2 boe7 tit khi2- lai5.  Sui-jian5 be7 kau3 kheng-ka tong7-san2, chong2-si7 au7-lai5 m7 chai beh chaiN2-iuN7 ui5-chi2; phah-sng3 kaN2 bo5 sim2-mih8 bang7 lah.     
Iah8 u7 lang5 peng5-sou3 chin lau2-sit8, long2 m7 bat poah8-kiau2; bo5 siuN7 saN kui2 ni5 cheng5, chia u7 chhut chit8 khoan2 seng-li2, kio3-choe3 Teng7-ki5 tu-sek boe2-boe7; tai7-seng lang5 boe2 sio2-khoa2, tauh8-tauh8 u7 than3 tam7-poh8.  Siok8-gu2 kong2, Poah8-kiau2 ham-khak khi2, choe3 chhat8 thau-mi bi2.  Tak8-e5 na2 poah8 na2 toa7; keh nng7 ni5 goa7, hut-jian5 tu2-tioh8 toa7 hong-thai, tu ke3 tit8-tit8 loh8, khah sio2 pun2 e5, liau2  
kau3 chhun3-chhau2 put liu5; u7 chit8 e5 khah sio2 pun2 e5, kui2 chap8 ban7 gun5 teh choe3 seng-li2, ia7 in-ui7 an2-ni phah-thiah boe7 tit8, choe3 i chau2 khi3 goa7-kok, lian5-lui7 hiah e5 tui3 gun5-hang5 ka7 i po2 ke e5 chin choe7 lang5; ki5-u5 liau2 gou7 chhit ban7 gun5 e5, ia7 u7 chap8 goa7 e5.  Tai7-seng teh  boe2-boe7, tak8-e5 ia7 chai che m7 si7 seng-li2, si7 chhin- chhiuN7 teh poah8-kiau2; m7-ku2 tak8 e5 kho3 in gau5 siuN7, gau5 phah-sng3, na2 chin u7 pa2-chhi5; khiok m7 chai ThiN choe3 tai7, hou7 lang5 long2 boe7 phah-sng3 tit.  Siok8-gu2 kong2, Lang5 gau5, m7-ku2 ThiN beh choe3 tui3 thau5; ia7 kong2, ChiN5 si3 kha, lang5 nng7 kha.  Chiau3 khoaN3 m7- na7 si3 kha, kui2-na7 chap8 ki to u7, koh u7 sit8 oe7 pe, m7 si7 hou7 lang5 jip oe7 tioh8.     
Koh chit8 hang7, Siong7-hai2 u7 chit8 e5 toa7 seng-li2 lang5, ti7 hit sou2-chai7 ia7 si7 chin u7 mia5-siaN e5 lang5; i u7 chit8 e5 kiaN2, ia7 chin chhut-lat8 chai-poe5, hou7 i thak8- chheh,koh hou7 i khi3 Tang-kiaN liu5-hak8.  To3-khi3 Siong7-hai2 e5 si5, to ji7-chap8 goa7 he3 lah.  Ia7 siuN7 ai3 khi3 pun2 kok tak8 seng2 iu5-lek8; chiu7 toa3 gun5 tui3 Hok-kian3 loh8-lai5.  Koh bo5 loa7 ku2 chiu7 jip2 Kng2- tang khi3.  Hit si5 chiu7 u7 lang5 chhoa7 i khi3 chhit- tho5 keng si3-koe3 kiaN5.  I ka-ki7 ia7 siuN7 che sng3 si7 m7 ho2 e5 sou2-chai7, m7 thang lai5 khah ho2.  Koh chit8-e7 siuN7, Goa2 ka-ki7 na7 u7 chiat-che3, beh thai3 u7 iau3-kin2. Bo5 siuN7 tui3 an2-ni soa3 chim3-chu3 loh8-khi3.  Toa3 hia khai geh8 goa7 jit8 ku2, m7 na7 chiN5 liau2 na7-tiaN7, soa3 kui seng-khu siN kau3 choan5 si7 chhng, na2 thai2-ko e5 chit2 iuN7.  Hit si5 chiah chai thang hoan2-hoe2, koaN2-kin2 che7 chun5 beh to3-khi3.  Ti7 chun5-nih8 e5 si5, bo5 sim2-mih8 tai7-chi3; ka-ki7 siuN7 kin-a2-jit8 piN3 kau3 an2-ni, thai3 u7 bin7 thang to3-khi3 kiN3 lang5?  Chiu7 peh-chiuN7 chun5- pho teng2, thiau3 tui3 hai2-nih8 loh8-khi3 si2.  Sou2-i2 kiN3-na7 oe7 ham7-hai7 lang5 e5 su7, chong2 tioh8 tai7-seng siam2 li7 i khah ho2.  Siok8-gu2 kong2, Boh8-tit siN thiaN3, khah ho2 bat ioh8; si7 chin u7 iaN2.   
Chhin-bak8 khoaN3 iau2-be7 si7 chin-sit8
Chai7-cha2 Khong2-chu2 ti7 Tin5, Chhai3, nng7 kok e5 tiong-kan, tu2-tioh8 jiau2-loan7 e5 su7, niu5-sit8 long2 choat8 tng7; saN jit8 bo5 chiah8-tioh8 poaN3 liap8 gou7 kak.  Hit si5 Khong2-chu2 to2 ti7 bin5-chhng5-nih8, Gan5 Hoe5 ti7 goa7-bin7 tit-tioh8 tam7-poh8 bi2, chiu7 koaN2-kin2 khi3 chu2.  Kau3 beh sek8 e5 si5, Khong2-chu2 khoaN3-kiN3 Gan5 Hoe5 chhun chhiu2 loh8-khi3 khaN-a2 lai7, theh8 png7 khi2-lai5 chiah8.  Koh ke3 u7 hiah ku2,  
chiah sang3 png7 lai5 hou7 Khong2-chu2.  Khong2-chu2 ke2 choe3 bo5 khoaN3-kiN3, tiau5-kou3-i3 kong2, Goa2 bang7-kiN3 chit8 e5 lang5 eng7 i chiah8-liau2 e5 mih8 hou7 goa2 chiah8.  Gan5 Hoe5 in3 i kong2, M7 si7, tu2-a2 in-ui7 u7 chit8 te3 ian-thun5 ka-lauh8 ti7 khaN-a8 lai7, na7 siuN7 chiong an2-ni khng3 teh, si7 bo5 chheng-khi3, na7 chham hit jiah e5 png7 hiat kak8, iu7 chin phah-sng2, sou2-i2 goa2 chiah liam-khi2-lai5 chiah8.  Khong2-chu2 thiaN-liau2 chiah thou2-khui3 kong2, Sou2 oe7 sin3 tit e5 si7 bak8-chiu, na7-si7 bak8-chiu iau2- be7 kau3-giah8 thang sin3; sou2 oe7 kho3-tit e5 si7 sim, m7-ku2 sim iu5-goan5 bo5 kau3-giah8 thang kho3.  Lin2 cheng3 hak8-seng iau3-kin2 tioh8 oe7 ki3-tit chit chan5 tai7-chi3, bat lang5 chin-chiaN3 m7 si7 iong5-iN7.     
TaN siok8-gu2 u7 kong2, Pek-bun5 put-ju5 it kian3; ia7 kong2, Bak8-chiu khoaN3-kiN3 chiah u7 sit8-chai7, hi7-khang thiaN-liau2 boe7 chun2-chin5 tit.  Na7 chiau3 teng2-bin7 e5 kou3-su7 khoaN3-khi2-lai5, m7-tan7-na7 hi7-khang thiaN-kiN3 si7 bo5 iaN2, chiu7 si7 chhin-bak8 khoaN3-kiN3, ia7 iau2-be7 oe7 liah8 choe3 si7 sit8-chai7.  Sou2-i2 lang5 ti7 chit se3-kan lai5- ong2 kau-chiap, long2 tioh8 ai3 tai7-ke saN khoan-iong5, tai7-ke sio-niu7, m7 thang in-ui7 chit8 tiam2-a2 sio2-khoa2 tai7-chi3, chiu7 khng3 chit8 e5 oan3-hun7 ti7 sim-nih8; a2-si7 in-ui7 chit8 poaN3 ku3 oe7 m7 sio teng3 thiaN, chiu7 tai7-ke m7 ho2.  U7 si5 chin choe7 tai7-chi3, lan2 sui-jian5 khoaN3- liau2 chin chheng-chho2, thiaN-liau2 chin beng5-pek8, m7 ku2 kiaN-liau2 hit loe7-tiong e5 chin-cheng5 sit8-i3, lan2 iau2-be7 chap8-hun7 siong5-se3 chai; m7 tat8-tioh8 hoan7-su7 sio2-khoa2 niu7 lang5 chit8 tiam2-a2, kiam2 m7 si7 seng2 chin choe7 e5 hoan5-lo2, ia7 bian2-tit tai7-ke teh saN-chiN.  Siok8- gu2 u7 kong2, KhoaN3 taN7 chhin3 hoe, kiam2-chhai2 si7 in-ui7 an2-ni.  
Iam2 ni2 to7 leng5
Chian2 kok e5 si5, Ti3 Pek u7 eng7 peng khi3 kong-biat8 in siN3 Hoan7-e5.   Hit si5 u7 chit8 e5  lang5 khi3 thau-theh8 siN3 Hoan7-e5 e5 leng5,  chiu7-si7 chhin-chhiuN7 giang-a2 e5 khoan2, chong2-si7 khah toa7 ki.   Hit e5 chhat8 gia5-khi2-lai5 pe7 ti7 keng-thau5 teng2 chiu7 toa7 pou7 chau2.   Hit leng5-lai7 e5 chih8 khap8-tioh8 leng5 chiu7 gin-giang  hau2; chhat8 chit8-e7 thiaN-kiN3, chiu7 siuN7 kiaN-liau2 pat8 lang5 tek-khak  ia7 thiaN oe7 tioh8, chiu7 koaN2-kin2 tui3 ka-ki7 e5 hi7-khang am-teh,  ka-ki7 chiu7 khah bothiaN5-kiN3, ia7 siuN7 pat8 lang5 si7 thiaN boe7 tioh8.  Che kiam2 m7 si7 gong7 kau3 boe7 hiau2-tit thang kong2 mah?     
 
TaN na7 lun7 kau3 se3-kan ia7 chin choe7 chit khoan2 e5 lang5, tak8 hang7 khui-sim-su7 to kaN2 choe3; iah8 na7 ti7 cheng3 lang5 e5 bin7-cheng5, chiu7 eng7 choe7-choe7 hong- hoat lai jia kham3, liah8 choe3 lang5 long2 m7 chai, che kiam2 m7 si7 chhin-chhiuN7 Iam2-ni2 to7 leng5 e5 kian3-sek mah?  Siok8-gu2 u7 kong2, Koe-nng7 bat8-bat8 to u7 phang7; ia7 kong2, Ai3 tit lang5 m7 chai, tu5-hui lan2 bo5 choe3.  Sou2-i2 chin-chiaN3 kun-chu2 e5 lang5, sui-jian5 ka-ki7 chit8 lang5 che7 ti7 chhu3-lai7, ia7 si7 m7 kaN2 chun5 chit8  tiam2 e5 phaiN2 liam7-thau5; put-ko3 si7 kin2-ban7, tek-khak u7 lang3 chai e5 si3-jit8.  Ho5-hong3 ti7 koaiN5-koaiN5 u7 chit8 e5 Siong7-te3 teh kam3-chhat; lan2 sim-lai7 teh siuN7, chhui3 be7 kong2, kha be7 kiaN5, I chiu7 i2-keng chai. An2-ni choe3 lang5 kiam2 m7 tioh8 si5-si5 khek-hhek lai5 sio2-sim mah?    
Bin7 tng5 chit8 tng7
Han3 Bu2-te3 u7 chit8 jit8 kap hiah e5 jin5-sin5 teh lun7-khi2 siong3-chheh e5 oe7 kong, Lang5 phiN7-e7 jin5-tiong na7 tng5 u7 chit8 chhun3, chiu7 u7 chit8 pah ni5 e5 he3-siu7.  Hit-si5 Tong-hong Sok ti7 piN-a2, thiaN-liau2 chiu7 toa7 chhio3, hah8- hah8 hau8.  U7 kun-sui5 hong5-te3 e5 lang5 chhut chau3 kong2, Tong-hong Sok chhio3 kau3 an2- ni, si7 bo5 keng3 jin5-kun e5 le2-sou3.  Tong-hong Sok thiaN-liau2 chiu7 chiong ka-ki7 e5 bo7 thng3-khi2-lai5,  sit-le2 sia7-choe7 e5 si5 tioh8 thng3 bo7-a2, kong2, Sin5 m7-kaN2 chhio3 Pe3-ha7, si7 teh  chhio3 PhiN5 Chou2 e5 bin7 chin tng5.  Bu2-te3 chiu7 mng7 I kong2, Li2 thai3-e7 chai PhiN5 Chou2 e5 bin7 tng5 leh?  Tong5-hong Sok in3 kong2, PhiN5 Chou2 chiah8 peh-pah he3, na7 chiau3 Pe3-ha7 kong2 an2-ni, chiu7 i e5 jin5-tiong u7 peh  chhun3 tng5; koh chham chhui3-e7-tau2, hiah8-a2, phiN7, choe3 chit8-e7 sng3, i e5 bin7 kiam2 m7 si7 tng7-goa7 tng5 mah?  Bu2-te3 thiaN-liau2, ia7 soa3 toa7 chhio3.  
 Hian7-si5 e5 lang5 khah choe7 iau2 si7 kong2 siong3-mia7 e5 su7 si7 u7 iaN2.  Khiok na7 si7 lang5 e5 hoaN-hi2, khoai3- lok8, iu-chhiu5, ut-bun7, i2-kip8 chhong-beng5 gu5-gong7, ti3-sek, ham-ban7, che tui3 bin7 lai5 siong3, u7 tam7-poh8 khoaN3 oe7 chhut.  Na7 lun7 kau3 su3-chi ngou2-koan, oe7 hun-piat lang5 e5 ho2-phaiN2, a2-si7 kong2 sim2-mih8, Lam5 kiuN-ge5, lu2 ou7-nng7, chiah si7 hu3-kui3, che kiam2 bo5 tu2- ho2 chhin-chhiuN7 teng2-bin7 sou2 kong2 hit khoan2 e5 ho2 chhio3?  Siok8-gu2 kong2, Siong7 te3 sim tng2; kho2-kian3 lang5 na7 u7 ho2 e5 sim, chu7-jian5 oe7 hoat-chhut chit8 khoan2 ho2 e5 siong7; na7 u7 phaiN2 e5 sim, chiu7 oe7 hoat- chhut hit khoan2 phaiN2 e5 siong7.  Sou2-i2 lang5 ai3 beh  u7 ho2 e5 siong7,  
tai7-seng sim-lai7 tioh8 chun5 u7 chit8 tiam2 ho2 e5 sim.  Lang5 kong2, PhaiN2-bin7-chhiuN, phaiN2- bin7-chhiuN; na7 si7 bo5 jin5-chu5 e5 lang5 siong5-siong5 u7 hian2-chhut chit khoan2 e5 bin7-mau7; m7 ku2 ia7 u7 kong2, Chhat8 sim he5-siuN7 bin7; an2-ni thang chai siong3-su e5 oe7 long2 si7 peh8-chhat8 liau2-liau2.    
Tang5-sim hiap8-lek8
Lam5-pak tiau5 e5 si5, pak-hng Thou2-kok- hun7 e5 Ong5, mia5-kio3 A-chha5, u7 ji7-chap8 e5 kiaN2.  Kau3 i phoa3-piN7 siong-tiong7, chai- kio3 i oe7 si2, hit-tiap8 chiu7 hoan-hu3 i hiah e5 kiaN2 kok lang5 kiah8 chit8 ki chiN3 lai5.  Tai7- ke chiu7 kiah8 lai5 hou7 i.  A-chha5 chiu7 kiah8 chit8 ki hou7 i e5 kiaN2, mia5 Bou7-li7-ian5, kio3 i  at-khoaN3-bai7 teh; hit ki chiN3 chit8-e7 at chiu7 tng7.  Chiu7 koh kah i chiong chap8- kau2 ki chiN3 lak8 choe3 chit8-e7, at-khoaN3 leh; sui-jian5 chin eng7 lat8, ia7 si7 at boe7 tng7.  A-chha5 chiah hoan-hu3 i hiah e5 kiaN2 kong2, Lin2 chiah e5 iau3-kin2 iau3-kin2 tioh8 oe7 ki3-tit. kou-toaN chit8 ki, si7 khoai3-khoai3 chih8, na7 lak8 choe3 chit8-e7, chiu7 oh-tit at.  Lin2 tioh8 tang5-sim hiap8-lek8, chiah oe7 po2-tit kok-ka.  Kong2-liau2 chiu7 ke3-sin khi3.     
TaN se3-kan su7 bo5 lun7 choe3 sim2-mih8, long2 tioh8 oe7 tang5-sim hiap8-lek8, chiah choe3 oe7 chiaN5.  Lang5 kong2, Ka ho5,ban7-su7 seng5, sit8-chai7 kai3 u7 iaN2.  Chhi3-khoaN3 ke-lai7 na7 teh heng-ong7 e5 si5, lai7-bin7 sui-jian5 chin  choe7 lang5, ia7 long2 kui-kui ku2-ku2, toa7 ui3 toa7, soe3 ui3 soe3, saN chhun5 saN keng3, tai7-ke ho5-ho2, jin7-chin choe3 in e5 kang.  Ia7 na7 ke-lai7 put-bok8, tak8-jit8 chhau2-nau7, sui-jian5 hit si5 iau2 ho2-khoaN3, koh m7 bian2 joa7 ku2, tek-khak oe7 pai7; che si7 tiaN7-tioh8 e5 li2-khi3. Chhin-chhiuN7 Tiong-kok sui kong2 si7 kiong7-ho5, m7- ku2 lang5 e5 sim long2 bo5 kiong7-ho5, sou2-i2 keng-ke3 chit gou7 ni5 ku2, kok-lai7 iu5-goan5 iau2-be7 peng5-cheng7.   
Iah8 chiu7-si7 lan2 e5 kau3-hoe7, keng3 koh khah tioh8 an2-ni.  In-ui7 lang5 ti7 chit se3-kan, boe7 bian2-tit tioh8 chin7 choe3-lang5 e5 pun2-hun7; teh hok8-sai7 Siong7-te3, siat-hoat kau3-hoe7, ia7 tioh8 tang5-sim hiap8-lek8, kau3- hoe7 chiah oe7 heng-ong7, kok lang5 chin7 in e5 sim, than3 Ia5-sou Ki-tok sou2 kong2 e5 oe7, Lin2 e5 lai7-bin7 eng- kai tioh8 u7 iam5, ia7 tai7-ke tioh8 saN ho5-ho2, an2-ni lai5 kiaN5. 
 
Tioh8 kiaN5 hou7 lang5 te3
Chai7-cha2 Che5 Hoan5-kong ai3 chheng7 chi2-sek e5 i-hok8, in kok-lai7 e5 jin5-sin5 peh- siN3 ia7 long2 chin hoaN-hi2 chheng7 chi2-sek  e5 saN-a2-khou3.  Tng hit si5 chi2-sek e5 pou3-lui7, pi2 pat8-mih2 sek-e5 e5 ke3-chiN5, ke kui3 u7 gou7 pe7.  Hoan5-kong sim-lai7 put-chi2 iu-chiu5,  chiu7 tui3 i e5 chaiN2-siong3 Koan2 Tiong kong2, Goa2 ai3 chheng7 chi2-sek-e5 m7 ku2 chi2-sek-e5 chin kui3, hian7-chai7 thong kok  e5 peh-siN3, tak8-e5 to hoaN-hi2 chheng7 chi2- sek, goa2 beh eng7 sim2-mih8 hoat-tou7 lai5 kim3-chi2 in leh?  Koan2 Tiong7 kong2, Kun thai3 m7 ka-ki7 tai7-seng boh8-tit chheng7 chi2- sek e5, chhi3-khoaN3-mai7 teh?  Ia7 na7 tui3 sin-piN kun-te3 e5 lang5, chiu7 ka7 in kong2, Goa2 put-chi2 m7 ai3 phiN7-tioh8 chit ho7 chi2- sek e5 bi7, si7 chin m7 ho2; siat-su2 thai3-kam3 na7 chheng7 chi2-sek e5 saN lai5, tioh8 ka7 i kong2, Li2 the3-khi3 kui2 hoah8, goa2 put-chi2 m7 ai3 phiN7-tioh8 chi2-sek e5 khi3-bi7.  Hoan5-kong hit si5 chiu7 in3 i kong2, Ho2, goa2 beh chiau3 li2 e5 oe7 lai5 chhi3-khoaN3-mai7.  Ko2-jian5 tng hit jit8 ti7 i e5 keng-lai7, chiu7 bo5 u7 chheng7 chi2-sek e5 i-hok8 e5; te7-ji7 jit8, chiu7 siaN5-lai7 ia7 bo5 lang5 beh chheng7; te7-saN jit8 chiu7 kok-lai7 e5 lang5, long2 bo5 beh chheng7 chi2-sek e5 I-hok8 lah.     
Chheh-nih8 u7 kong2, In e5 seng-khu na7 choe3 tit  chiaN3, iau2-be7 chhut beng7-leng7 lang5 chiu7 te3 i lai5 kiaN5; in pun2-sin na7 choe3 put cheng3, sui-jian5 u7 beng7-leng7, lang5 ia7 m7 an2-ni kiaN5.  Hian7-si5 iau2 u7 koa2 hit ho7 lang5, tok8-tok8 khng3 lang5 tioh8 thiaN3 lang5 chhin-chiuN7 ka-ki7, iah8 ka-ki7 iu7 bo5 an2-ni choe3; khng3 lang5 tioh8 hoan2-hoe2 jin7 choe7, ka-ki7 iu7 bo5 an2- ni kiaN5; khng3 lang5 m7 thang tham-chai5 kong2 peh8- chhat8, m7 ku2 ka-ki7 chin tham-chai5, ai3 kong2 peh8- chhat8.  An2-ni na7 lan2 ka-ki7 bo5 seng kiaN5 chhut lai5, sou2 khng3 lang5 e5 oe7, kiam2 u7 lang5 beh thiaN lan2 mah? Sou2-i2 lan2 Kau3-hoe7 e5 peng5-iu2 teh kiaN5-tah8, cham2-jian5 tioh8 chin soe3-ji7, chiah boe7 chou2-gai7-tioh8 to7-li2 e5  chin3-pou7. 
Kin2 su7 khoaN pan7
Tiong-kok Tong5-tiau5 e5 si5, u7 chit8 e5 tai7-sin5 siN3 Poe5 mia5 Tou7, in-ui7 hong kong-chiok ti7 Chin3 e5 sou2-chai7, sou2-i2 lang5 kong2 Poe5 Chin3-kong.  U7 chit8 jit8 hut-jian5 lang5 lai5 po3 i kong2, Li2 e5 in3 phah-m7-kiN3 lah.  PiN-a2 e5 lang5 thiaN-kiN3 an2-ni, tai7-ke toa7 kiaN, bin7 long2 sit-sek.  (Kou2-cha2 choe3 koaN e5 lang5 in3 na7 phah-m7-kiN3,  
koaN liau2 boe7 soah tit, u7 si5 oe7 u7 choe7).  Tok8-tok8 Chin3-kong long2 bo5 sim2-mih8 khoa3-i3, iu5-goan5 kio3 lang5 pi7- pan7 ian5-siah8 lai5 chhiaN2 lang5-kheh, hoaN- hoaN hi2-hi2, long2 bo5 hoan5-lo2.  Cheng3-lang5 m7 chai i e5 i3-su3, put-chi2 ki5-koai3.  Kau3 poaN3-mi5 e5 si5, hut-jian5 u7 lang5 lai5 ka7 i kong2, In3 koh ti7-teh lah.  Chin3-kong ia7 bo5 hoaN-hi2 e5 khoan2.  Au7-lai5 u7 lang5 mng7 i kong2, An3-chaiN2-iuN7 li2 thai3 an2-ni?  Chin3-kong chiah kong2, Che in3 put-ko3 si7 ge5-iah8 thau-theh8 khi3 eng7 chit8-e7; khoaN-khoaN-si7 chu7-jian5 ka-ki7 koh theh8-lai5 he7-the; na7-si7 chhiN-kong5 chhe7, pek siuN kin2, kiaN-liau2 thau-theh8 in3 e5 lang5 bo5 hoat-tou7 thang theh8 to3-tng2-lai5, tek-khak chiong in3 hiat loh2 chui2-nih8, a2-si7 he2-nih8 sio; (in-ui7 thau- theh8 in3 e5 lang5 si7 si2 choe7); an2-ni chiu7 bo5 hoat-tou7 thang chhe7 liau2.   
Teng2-bin7 chit chat e5 kou3-su7, m7 si7 kah lang5 hoan7- su7 pang3 bo5-iau3 bo5-kin2, si7 kong2 bo5-lun7 tu2-tioh8 sim2- mih8 kin2-kip e5 tai7-chi3, long2 tioh8 sim-koaN liah8-tiaN7, phah-sng3 hou7 ho2, m7-thang pak-lai7 ju5 chhiang2- chhiang2, chhiN-kong5 tit8-tit8 pek, chiu7 bo5 iau3-kin2 e5 tai7-chi3, ia7 long2-chhut chin toa7 e5 su7 lai5.  U7 si5 ko3- jin5 e5 tai7-chi3, pek kau3 chu7-chin7; ia7 na7 khah thoan5- the2 e5 su7, chiu7 pek kau3 piN3 chiaN5 hoan2-poan7 e5 toa7 choe7.  Siong5-siong5 bat khoaN3 lang5 ka-ki7 phaiN2 ki3- ti5, mih8 siu-liau2 boe7 ki3 tit, lam7-sam2 bu5-loa7 lang5, hai7 lang5 khi3 siu7 chin choe7 e5 kan-khou2; kau3 au7-lai5 koh chhe7 tioh8, i ia7 m7 jin7 ka-ki7 m7 tioh8, hoan2-tng2 gi5 si7 hit e5 lang5 theh8-lai5 chhang3-teh heng5 i.  Siok8-gu2 kong2, Kin2-su7 khoaN pan7; kho2-kian3 seng3-te7 siuN-kip e5 lang5, kai3 gau5 long3-phoa3 tai7-chi3.   
Chin2-che3 lang5 tioh8 kip8-si5
Chong Chiu kek8 song3-hiong e5 si5-chun7,khi3 kin3 Kam Ho5-hou5, kiu5 beh ka7 i chioh tam7-poh8 bi2-niu5.  Kam Ho5-hou5 kong2, ChhiaN2 theng3-hau7 teh, koh keh bo5 kui2 jit8, goa2 beh tit-tioh8 chit8 e5 khah ho2 toe7-hng e5 kheh, goa2 chiah saN pah e5 gun5 chioh li2; an2-ni ho2 m7?  Chong Chiu thiaN-liau2 m7 hoaN-hi2, chiu7 siat chit8 e5 phi3-ju7 kong2, Goa2 cha7-jit8 lai5 e5 si5, ti7 lou7-nih8 u7 thiaN-kiN3 teh  au5-kio3 e5 siaN-im, goa2 chiu7 si3-koe3 khoaN3, khoaN3 to bo5 lang5, goan5-lai5 si7 ti7 chhia-lou7-kau nih8, u7 chit8 be2 chit-a2-hi5 teh au5-kio3. Goa2 chiu7 mng7 i kong2, Li2 an3-chaiN2-iuN7 thai3 lai5 tiam3 chia?  Kio3 goa2 beh sim2-mih8 su7?  Hit e5 chit-a2-hi5 kong2, Goa2 si7 tang-hai2 e5 pho2-sin5, li2  
kheng2 eng7 chit8 chin chui2, a2- si7 chit8 tau2 chui2, lai5 kiu3 goa2 e5 oah8-mia7 bo5?  Goa2 chiu7 ka7 i kong2, ChhiaN2 theng3- hau7 teh, goa2 beh loh8 lam5 khi3 kia5-iu5, chiah khng3 Gou5 Oat8 nng7 kok e5 ong5, chiong se-kang e5 chui2 khui hou7 thau3 lai5, thang ngia5-chih li2 to3-khi3 hai2-nih2, an2-ni ho2 m7?  Hit chiah chit-a2-hi5 siu7-khi3 kong2, Goa2 put-ko3 chit8 si5 chhau3-khiau2 tu2-tioh8 chit ho7 e5 kan-lan5, chi2-u7 beh kiu5 chit8 chin a2-si7 chit8 tau2 e5 chui2, chit8 tiau5 mia7 chiu7 oe7 oah2; na7 chiau3 li2 kong2, put-ju5 khi3 koe- chhi7-nih8 e5 hi5-pou2 tiam3, khoaN3 goa2 chiu7 ho2.     
TaN lun7-kau3 hian7-si5 e5 song3-hiong lang5, ia7 chin choe7 long2 boe7 sng3 tit.  Hit tiong-kan u7 koa2 si7 in- ui7 phiau5, tou2, im2 lai5 ti3-kau3 an2-ni, sng3 si7 chu7-chok chu7-siu7, che m7 bian2 kong2; ia7 u7 koa2 si7 tai3-chit8, khe5-kha, phoa3-siuN3, thai2-ko, chhiN-mi5, a2-si7 kou-khou2 e5 lau7-lang5, in-ui7 put-heng7 lai5 ti3-kau3 an2-ni.  U7 koa2 hou7 Chu5-hui7-iN7 siu-iong5 khi3; m7 ku2 iau2 chin-choe7, koaN-hu2 chiau3-kou3 thai3 oe7 chiau5 tioh8?  An2-ni tek- khak tioh8 kho3 chiah e5 u7 chiN5 e5 lang5, chiau3 in e2 lek8- liong7, than3 hit e5 si5-ki lai5 pang-chan7 in, hou7 in chek- siau2 seng5 to, oe7 tang3 tou7 jit8.  Na7 beh phah-ka-lauh8 chit8-liap8 png7-liap8, kong3-si2 saN chiah kau2.  Tng lang5 bin7-cheng5 kong2, Si7 goa2 theh8 boe7 khi2; na7 bo5, goa2 to kam-goan7 choe3 ho2 su7; an2-ni kiam2 m7 si7 kap  teng2-bin7 hit e5 kou3-su7 sio-siang7 mah?  Seng3-keng Ma2-thai3 25 chiuN 42-45 chat kong2, In-ui7 goa2 iau, lin2 m7 bat hou7 goa2 chiah8; goa2 chhui3-ta, lin2 m7 bat hou7 goa2 lim; goa2 chhut-goa7, lin2 m7 bat hou7 goa2 toa3, goa2 thng3-pak-theh, lin2 m7 bat hou7 goa2 chheng7; goa2 phoa3-piN7 kap ti7 kaN-nih8, lin2 m7 bat khoaN3-kou3 goa2. In ia7 beh in3 kong2, Chu2 ah, goan2 sim2-mih8 si5 khoaN3- kiN3 li2 iau, a2-si7 chhui3-ta, a2-si chhut-goa7, a2-si7 thng3- pak-theh, a2-si7 phoa3-piN7, a2-si7 ti7 kaN-nih8, lai5 bo5 hok8- sai7 li2 ah?  I chiu7 beh in3 i kong2, Goa2 sit8-chai7 ka7 lin2 kong2, Lin2-ki3-jian5 bo5 kiaN5 i ti7 chiah e5 chi3-bi5 soe3-e5 e5 chit8 e5, chiu7-si7 bo5 kiaN5 i ti7 goa2.  
Ho7 hok oh-tit hun-piat
Tiong-kok e5 pak-hng, oa2-kun7 goa7-kok e5 pian-kai3, mia5 kio3 Sai3-chiuN7.  Ti7 kou2- cha2 e5 si5, hit sou2-chai7 u7 chit8 e5 lau7-lang5, in tau chhi7 chit8 chiah be2, bo5 tiuN-ti5 soa3 phah-m7-kiN3, tai7-khai3 si7 chau2 tui3 pak-peng5 Ou5-jin5 e5 toe7-hng khi3.  Lang5 chiu7 lai5 tham3 i, soa3 ka7 i an-ui3.  Hit e5 lau7-lang5 kong2, Chit e5 tai7-chi3 bo5 tek-khak; si7  
hok-khi3 ia7 kaN2.  Ke3 bo5 kui2 geh8 jit8, hit chiah sit-loh8 khi3 e5 be2, hut-jian5 chham chit8 chiah Ou5 jin5 e5 be2 saN-kap to3-lai5.  Lang5 chiu7 long2 lai5 khoaN3, ia7 soa3 ka7 i kiong-hi2.  Hit e5 lau7-lang5 kong2, Chit e5 tai7-chi3 bo5 tek- khak; si7 chai-e7 ia7 kaN2.  Au7-lai5 i e5 kiaN2 siong5-siong5 ai3 khia5 hit chiah be2; u7 chit8 jit8 m7 tu2 ho2 khi3 hou7 poah8-loh2-lai5, kha-kut soa3 siang3 tng7-khi3.  Cheng3 lang5 iu7 lai5 tham3-bai7 i, soa3 ka7 i an-ui3.  Hit e5 lau7- lang5 kong2, Chit ho7 tai7-chi3 bo5 tek-khak; si7 hok-khi ia7 kaN2.  Koh keh chiaN5 ni5 ku2, Ou5-jin5 nia2 chin choe7 peng, kong-phah jip8 Sai3-chiuN7, kiN3-na7 siau3-lian5 lang5 long2 tioh8 kiah8 ke-si khi3 kap Ou5-jin5 saN-thai5.  Tng hit-si5 Sai3-chiuN7 e5 lang5, chap8 hun7 si2 kau2 hun7 khah ke khi3.  Chi2-u7 chit e5 pai2-kha e5 in pe7 kiaN2 tit-tioh8 po2-choan5 in e5 siN3- mia7.  
Chiau3 teng2-bin7 e5 khoan2 ka7 i khoaN3, lang5 ti7 chit se3-kan, tit-tioh8 hok-khi3, ia7 m7-bian2 hoaN-hi2, tu2-tioh8 chai-e7, ia7 m7-bian2 hoan5-lo2 : tioh8 ai3 chai hok-khi3 e5 lai7-bin7, ia7 u7 chai-e7, chai-e7 e5 tiong-kan, iu5-goan5 u7 hok-khi3.  Lang5 na7 oe7 beng5-pek8 chit e5 to7-li2, chiu7 put-lun7 ti7 sim2-mih8 sou2-chai7, ti7 sim2-mih8 si5, sim-koaN bo5 m7 peng5-an khoai3-lok8. 
Tui3 sio2-khoa2 oe7 chai toa7 hang7
Tiu7-ong5 u7 chit8 jit8 tit-tioh8 chit8 siang chhiuN7-ge5 e5 ti7, i e5 jin5-sin5  Ki5 Chu2 khoaN3-liau2 put-chi2 iu-bun7 kiaN-hiaN5.  Lang5 mng7 i kong2, Che  sng3 bo5 sim2-mih8 iau3-kin2 e5 su7, an3-chaiN2-iuN7 li2 ia7 kiaN kau3 an2-ni?  Ki5 Chu2  chiah kong2, In-ui7 lang5 na7 u7 chit ho7 ge5-ti7, chiu7 m7 koh eng7 chhou-hui5 e5 chiu2-poe, tek-khak tioh8 eng7 gek8-poe lai5 phoe3 i.  Kau3 u7 ge5-ti7 gek8-poe,  chiu7 m7 koh chiah8 hit ho7 chhou-chhai3 pian7-png7 lah; tek-khak oe7 beh chiah8 hiah e5 san-tin hai2-bi7.  Na7 chiah8 san-tin hai2-bi7, chiu7 m7 kheng2 koh chheng7 chit ho7 chhou-pou3 i-chiuN5, tioh8 hit ho7 leng5-lo5 phang2-si tiu5-toan7 chiah beh chheng7.  Na7 kau3 chiah8  chheng7 hiah ho2, chiu7 m7 kheng2 koh khia7 chit ho7  m7 chiaN5 chhu3, tek-khak tioh8 khia7 koaiN5 lau5 toa7 chhu3; an2-ni na2 khi3 na2 chhia-hoa5, m7 chai beh kau3 toh-loh8 ui5 chi2.  Au7-lai5 Tiu7-ong5  ko2-jian5 chin chhia-chhi2, long2 bo5 chiau3-kou3 peh-siN3, ti3-kau3 hou7 Chiu Bu2-ong5 biat8-khi3.     
 
 
Kou2 lang5 gian5 kong2, Ai3 chheng7 e5 ai3 io5, ai3 chiah8  e5 ai3 phiau5.  In-ui7 u7 lang5 ia7 khioh siok8-gu2 khi2-lai5 kong2, Sin-nih8 bo5 i, pi7 lang5 khi, khiok ia7 u7 iaN2; bo5 lun7 sim2-mih8 sou2-chai7, long2 si7 an2-ni.  Sou2-i2 tai7-ke na2 tau3 na2 chhia-hoa5.  Ki5-sit8 lan2 lang5 teh khia7-khi2 e5 sou2-chai7, kap chiah8 chheng7 e5 su7, chi3-ho2 si7 tioh8 choe5-chaN2 chheng-khi3 choe3 iau3-kin2; chhian-ban7 m7 thang him-sian7 pat8 lang5 e5 hoan5-hoa.  In-ui7 na7 u7 chit8  khoan2 e5 ho2 mih8, tek-khak tioh8 chhe7 pat8 hang7 ho2 mih8 lai5 phoe3 i; na7 bo5, to thin7 boe7 ke3.  Chhin-chhiuN7 goa2 beng5 khoaN3-kiN3 chit8 lang5, ui7-tioh8 chian2- hoat, ia7 te3 lang5 choe3 chit8 su poaN3-le2-hok8, khiok ia7 u7 bo7-a2, m7-ku2 iau2 khiam3 chit8 siang ho2 e5 phe5-oe5; kau3 chiaN geh8 e5 chhoe it, tai7-ke teh chng, chong2-si7 i iau2 khiam3 chit hang7 chiu7 boe7 eng7 tit, khah kan- khou2 ia7 tioh8 boe2 lai5 thiN.  Sou2-i2 u7 khun5-khiam7 ho2- tek e5 lang5, tek-khak tioh8 tui3 sio2-khoa2 e5 su7 lai5 jin7- chin.     
Chhe7 boe7 si2 e5 hong-hoat
Chai7-cha2 u7 chit8 e5 lang5, ka-ki7 kong2, i bat boe7 si2 e5 hong-hoat.  Ian ong5 thiaN- kiN3, sui5-si5 chhe lang5 khi3 mng7 i khoaN3 tioh2 eng7 sim2-mih8 hoat-tou7.  Kho2-sioh hit e5 su3- chia2 ti7 lou7-nih8 tam-koh, iau2-be7 kau3 te3, hit e5 kong2 u7 boe7 si2 e5 hong-hoat e5 lang5 i2-keng si2 khi3, soa3 boe7 thang tit-tioh8.  Ian ong5 put-chi2 siu7-khi3 hit e5 hong7 chhe e5 lang5, kong2 i ti7 lou7-nih8 ian5-chhian5, ti3-kau3 boe7 thang tit-tioh8 hit ho7 boe7 si2 e5 hong-hoat; chiu7 beh thai5 hit e5 hou7 i chhe e5 lang5. Au7-lai5 u7 chit8 e5 jin5-sin5 khou2-khng3 Ian ong5 kong2, Si2-sit si7 lang5 sou2 kiaN-hiaN5, siN3-mia7 si7 lang5 sou2 tui3-tiong7.  TaN hit e5 lang5 ka- ki7 to i2-keng si2-khi3-liau2, an3-chaiN2-iuN7 u7 hong-hoat thang hou7 Ong5 boe7 si2 leh?     
Tong-si5 ia7 u7 chit8 e5 lang5, mia5 kio3 Che5 Chu2, ia7 beh oh8 chit ho7 boe7 si2 e5 hong-hoat; thiaN-kiN3 hit e5 lang5 si2, chiu7 put-chi2 iu-bun7 hoan5-lo2.  Hu3 Chu2 thiaN-kiN3 chiu7 thi2- chhio3 i kong2, Li2 beh oh8 boe7 si2 e5 hong- hoat, iah8 hit e5 beh ka3 li2 e5 sian-siN i2-keng to si2-khi3 lah, li2 iau2-ku2 teh thoe3 i iu-bun7, m7 chai li2 si7 beh oh8 i sim2-mih8 leh?    
 
 
TaN hian7-si5 e5 lang5 sou2 teh hok8-sai7 it-khai3 e5 ngou2- siong7, ia7 kong2 si7 kou2-cha2 e5 tiong-sin5 hau3-chu2; chhin- chhiuN7 TiuN Sun5 choe3 Tou-thian Tai7-te3, TiuN Gi5 choe3 Giok8-hong5 Tai7-te3, Li JiN2 choe3 Thai3-siong7 Lo2-kun, Lau5 Tiong5-seng choe3 Chin-bu2 Tai7-te3, Tan5 Chu2-chhun choe3 Bun5-chhiong Te3-kun, Tio7 Kong-beng5 choe3 Chai5-sin5 Phou5-sat, Lim5 Bek2-a2- che2 choe3 Thian-siong7 Seng3-bu2, Koan U2 choe3 Hiap8-thian Tai7-te3, TiuN To7-leng5 choe3 Thian-su, Sek-khia-bou5-ni5 choe3 Put8-chou2; chhin-chhiuN7 chiah e5 kong2 boe7 tit liau2, m7 bian2 kong2 he si7 thou5-chhiok8 chha5 khek e5, bo5-leng5 bo5-siaN3, chiu7-si7 siat-su2 ko2-jian5 in hiah e5 lang5 long2 iau2 ti7 se3-kan, in ia7 boe7 oe7 siuN2- su3 lang5 e5 siN-si2 ho7-hok, in-ui7 in ka-ki7 e5 siN-si2 ho7- hok, siong7-chhiaN2 boe7 oe7 ka-ki7 choe3 chu2 tit, beh thai3 oe7 koan2 lang5 e5 siN-si2 ho7-hok leh?  Ho5-hong3 in i2-keng si2-khi3 kang2 chheng ni5 ku2, lian5-to7 si2-liau2 koh khah u7 chai5-leng5 pun2-su7 mah?  Tek-khak bo5 chit tiau5 li2, tek-khak bo5 chit tiau5 li2.  
M7 chai khin-tang7
Kou2-cha2 e5 si5, Ian kok u7 chit8 e5 chai5-tiau7 e5 lang5, mia5 kio3 Gak8 Ge7.  I lian5-hap8 Chin5, Chhou2, Han5, Tio7, Gui7, gou7 kok e5 peng, lai5 kong-phah Che5 kok.  Che5 ong5 beng7-leng7 Chhiok-chu2 khi3 ti2-tek8 in; hoan-hu3 Chhiok-chu2 kong2, Li2 tioh8 kap i kau- chian3, thai5 kau3 oe7 iaN5 tui3-tek8; na7 bo5, goa2 beh biat8 li2 e5 ke-koan3, kui chong-chok8  choe3 chit8-e7 thai5, lian5 lin2 chou2-kong e5 hun5-bong7 to beh kut8-khi2-lai5.   Chhiok-chu2 am3-chiN7 siuN7 kong2, Eng7 chit8 kok e5 peng, beh tu3 lak8  kok thai3 tong3 oe7 tiau5?  Na7 kiu5 boe7 thai5-su chiu7 ho2, nia2 kaN2 ng3-bang7  iaN5 in?  Kau3 liong2-peng5 chiap tin7 e5 si5, Chhiok-chu2 koaN2-kin2 chhut  beng7 the3 peng, in-ui7 kiaN-liau2 thai5-su.  Beh siaN2 chai lak8 kok e5 peng, chiong an2-ni choe3 chit8-e7 ham7 oa2-lai5.  Che5 peng toa7 pai7; Chhiok-chu2 tan-jin5 tok8-be2, chau2 kau3 put ti khi3 hiong3.  Hit-si5 iau2 u7 chit8 e5 chiong3, mia5 kio3 Tat8-chu2, chiong hiah e5 pai7 peng koh chip8 choe3 tui; in-ui7 kun-hiong3 put chiok, chhe lang5 khi3 tui3 Che5-ong5 nia2 gun5.  Che5-ong5 siu7-khi3 kong2, Chit ho7 bo5 lou7-eng7 e5 peng, iau2 teh ng3-bang7 goa2 hoat hiong3 hou7 in mah?  Bo5, bo5, bo5.  Au7-   lai5 Tat8-chu2 e5 peng, kap Gak8 Ge7 kau- chian3, kun-peng long2 bo5 thang chiah8, sim-koaN chiu7 loan7, sou2-i2 Che5 kok thai5 su; Tat8-chu2 soa3 tin7  
bong5.  Lak8 kok e5 peng than3 chit e5 se3, chiam3 chhit-chap8 goa7 e5 siaN5-ti5; lian5 Che5 kok e5 kiaN-siaN5 ia7 phoa3; kok khou3 e5 kim-gun5 chai5-po2, long2 hou7 in poaN liau2-liau2.  Che5 ong5 chau2-khi3 ti7 Ku2- siaN5 nih8; au7-lai5 ia7 hou7 lang5 chhi3-si2.   
KiN3-na7 hit ho7 khah gau5 eng7 lang5 e5 lang5, i chiu7 khoaN3 hit e5 lang5 e5 chai5-tiau7 kau3 tah-loh8, chiah eng7 i choe3 hit e5 su7, si7 kian3 ki ji5 chok, choe3 liau2 chiah oe7 seng5-kong.  Na7-si7 hit ho7 lang5 to choe3 boe7 lai5, beh kah i kiong5 choe3, tek-khak oe7 piN3 chhut m7 ho2 e5 su7 lai5.  Che5 ong5 beng7-leng7 Chhiok-chu2 nia2 chit8 kok e5 peng, beh kah i tek-khak tioh8 thai5-iaN5 in lak8 kok, che kiam2 m7 si7 eng7 chit8 e5 toa7 ui5-lan5 e5 su7, beh kiong5-kiong5 kah i choe3 mah?  Chhiok-chu2 oe7  to5 chau2, sit8-chai7 si7 Che5-ong5 pek i khi3 e5.  Koh  chhin-chhiuN7 Beng5-tiau5-be2 Chong5-cheng e5 si5, Li2 Chhoang3 cho7 hoan2, kok khou long2 khang-hu, ai3 tui3 kiaN-siaN5 lai7 e5 bun5-bu2 koaN toe5 tam7-poh8 lai5 choe3 kun- hiong3, thang peng5-tiaN7 chit e5 jiau2-loan7.  Hiah e5  koaN long2 kong2 bo5 chiN5, sim7-chi3 u7-e5 tiau5-kou3-i3 tah chit8 tiuN ji7 toa3 mng5-khau2 kong2, Chit keng chhu3 beh boe7,an2-ni lai5 moaN5-phian3 lang5 kong2 in teh bo5 chiN5.  Lian5 Kok-tiong7 (Hong5-te3 e5 tiuN7-lang5)ia7 si7 an2-ni.  Hong5-hou7 kheng5 i e5 sai-khia, kap hoe-hun2 chiN5, chha-put-to u7 chap8-ban7; kau-tai7 i e5 lau7-pe7, khi3 hoat hou7 siaN5-lai7 e5 kun-peng.  Hit e5 Kok-tiong7 ia7 ka7 i tau7 chhit ban7 khi2-lai5, chi2-u7 hoat saN ban7 na7- tiaN7.  Kau3 au7-lai5 Li2 Chhoang3 kong-phoa3 kiaN-siaN5, Hong5-te3 chu7-chin7, hiah e5 bun5-bu2 koaN long2 hou7 Li2 Chhoang3 liah8 khi3.  Chiu7 eng7 chit8 khoan2 e5 heng5-hoat8, chiong chit8 e5 thih-khou tui3 hiah e5 koaN-oan5 sui5-e5 thoa lai5 khou thau5-khak, chiah mng7 khoaN3 in e5 chiN5 chhang3 toa3 tah-loh8; na7 m7 kong2 chiu7 eng7 thih-thui5  ka7 i tiN5 khah loh8 khi3, tak8 e5 tong3 long2 boe7 tiau5, long2-kong2 chhut lai5.  Hit e5 Kok-tiong7 ia7 hou7 i chiN saN pah kui2 ban7 khi3; koh in-ui7 lang5 u7 khah lau7, boe7  siu7-tit hit khoan2 e5 heng5-hoat8, keh jit8 ia7 soa3 si2-khi3. Chhin-chhiuN7 chit khoan2 bo5 kou3 tai7-kiok8 e5 lang5, kap Che5 ong5 m7 kheng2 hoat hiong3-gun5, si7 siang7 chit8 khoan2 e5 gu5-gong7.  
Sun2 jin5 li7 ki2
U7 chit8-e5 bou2-mih8 lang5, in chhiuN5-a2-lai7 u7 chit8 chang5 gou5-tong5 chhiu7, u7 ki i2-keng ta- khi3; in chhu3-piN u7 chit8 e5 lau7-lang5 lai5 ka7 i kong2, Chit chang5 chhiu7 hoat toa3 chia, u7 hoan7-tioh8 chhu3-theh8, put-chi2 bo5 li7-ek lin2 ke-lai7 e5 lang5; thai3 m7 chho3-khi2-lai5? Hit e5 bou2 lang5 ia7 chin-chiaN3 thiaN i e5  chhui3; chiong hit chang5  
gou5-tong5 chhiu7 chho3-khi2-lai5.  Hit e5 lau7-lang5 chiu7 ke3-lai5, ka7 i tho2 hiah e5 ta e5 chhiu7 ki, kong2 si7 beh  choe3 chha5 hiaN5.  Hit e5 bou2 lang5 thiaN-liau2 chin m7 hoaN-hi2 kong2, Chit e5 lau7-lang5 in- ui7 beh tihN8 chha5, kio3 goa2 tioh8 chho3 chit chang5 chhiu7; na7 chhin-chhiuN7 chit khoan2 e5 chhu3-piN, sit8-chai7 hou7 lang5 thang kiaN.     
Hian7-si5 u7 chit8 chiong2 e5 lang5, lang5 sou2 choe3 e5 su7, i chiu7 eng7 chin choe7 oe7 lai5 chou2-tong3, kong2 chit hang7 m7 ho2, a2-si7 hit hang7 m7 ho2; i pun2-sin khiok sut-au7-phau3 khi3 choe3, lai5 chiam3 lang5 pan-gi5, che ia7 si7 kap hit e5 lau7-lang5 siang7 chit8 iuN7.   
Hoat-tou7 chai7 lang5 eng7
Song3 kok u7 chit8 e5 lang5 oe7 kap chit8 khoan2 e5 ioh8, boah-liau2 chhiu2 boe7 pit; kui2-na7 tai7 lang5 kho3 u7 chit e5 ioh8, long2 teh choe3 phio3-se e5 kang-ge7.  Au7-lai5 u7 chit8 e5 lang5-kheh lai5 chhe7 in, beh eng7 chit8 pah niu2 e5 gun5 ka7 in boe2 chit e5 ioh8-hng.  Hit e5 Song3 kok e5 lang5 chiu7 kap in chong- chok8 lai7 tai7-ke chham-siong5 kong2, Lan2 tak8 se3-tai7 choe3 chit e5 phio3-se e5 eng5-giap8, sou2 than3 bu5-ki-chiN5, taN chit8 si5 boe7 chit e5  ioh8-hng, u7 thang tit-tioh8 chit8 pah khou, thai3 oe7 m7 ho2 leh?  Chiu7 chiong ioh8-hng boe7 hou7 hit e5 lang5-kheh.  Lang5-kheh chiu7 khi3 kiN3 Gou5 ong5, kong2 i u7 chit khoan2 e5 ioh8-hng.  Tng hit-si5 Gou5 kok kap Oat8 kok teh saN-thai5.  Gou5 ong5 chiu7 beng7-leng7 chit e5 lang5-kheh nia2 chui2-kun, ti7 tang- thiN e5 si5, kap Oat8 kok chui2-chian3; in-ui7 chit peng5 e5 peng u7 chit ho7 ioh8, chhiu2 long2 bo5 pit, khah oe7 oah8-tang7, soa3 phah iaN5 Oat8 kok e5 lang5.  Au7-lai5 hit e5 lang5- kheh hong kau3 chin koaiN5 e5 koaN-chit.     
Koh u7 chit8 hang7, ti7 kui2 chap8 ni5 cheng5 Sio2 Liu5- khiu5 e5 kang2-khau2, in-ui7 kong3-phoa3 chit8 chiah chun5, Sio2 Liu5-khiu5 e5 lang5 u7 khioh-tioh8 chit8 toa7 kan e5 ioh8;  khoaN3-liau2 peh8-peh8 mi5-mi5, m7 chai sim2-mih8 lou7-eng7. Hia e5 lang5 long2 si7 teh tho2-hai2, koaN5-thiN e5 si5, chhiu2- nih8 boe7 bian2-tit oe7 pit; chiu7 eng7 chit ho7 ioh8 lai5 ka7 i soe2 khoaN3-mai7 teh.  He2, chin ho2 eng7, soe2-liau2 ia7 boe7 pit, ia7 boe7 thiaN3, iah8 na7 u7 pit e5 chhiu2, soe2-liau2 chin khoai3 ho2.  Kau3 au7-lai5 soe2 kau3 chhun bo5 chit8 tiam2-a2 na7-tiaN7, tu2-tioh8 chit8 e5 Eng-kok e5 bok8-su khi3, in chiu7 koaN7 chhut-lai5 mng7 i, khoaN3 che si7 sim2-mih8  ioh8.  Hit e5 bok8-su chit8 e7 khoaN3, to si7 kin-na2-hun2, chiu7 ka7  
in kong2, Che si7 ti7 koaN5-jiat8-piN7 te7 it ho2 e5 ioh8.  Hit8 si5 Sio2 Liu5-khiu5 chin choe7 chit ho7 piN7, tai7- ke put chit8-tiam2-a2 khi3 chiah8, long2 u7 tit-tioh8 ho2.     
TaN lan2 ia7 siong5 bat khoaN3-kiN3, siang7 chit8 keng oh8-tng5 e5 hak8-seng, siang7 thak8 chit8 khoan2 e5 chheh, sian-siN ia7 siang7 chit8 khoan2 teh ka3-si7 in; kau3 chut-giap8 liau2, u7-e5 khi3 choe3 koaN, choe3 kau3 chin toa7, chhut-chiong3 jip8-siong3; u7-e5 khi3 khui- hang5 che7 tiam3; u7-e5 jin7 lou7 than3 chiah8, taN-chhang boe7-chhai3; che iau2 si7 kui2-ku2 e5 lang5.  Iau2 u7 hit ho7 chi3-khi3 chin toa7, siuN7 beh choe3 seng3-hian5 e5 lang5, chhun5 sim beh kiu3 se3-kan e5 su7.  Ia7 u7 chit8 khoan2 khah bo5 lou7-eng7 e5 lang5, chiah8-pa2 to5 lau7, iu5-goan5 kap lang5 ke3 chit8-si3-lang5.  Koh u7 chit8 khoan2, ka- ki7 kam-goan7 choe3 hou7 ha7-chian7, lim-thin5 kong3-phah, m7 tho2 m7 than3, kaN2 chiah8 kaN2 khai, ai3 poah8 ai3 hoa7. Te7 it hai7 chiu7-si7 chiah8 a-phian3.  Siok8-gu2 u7 kong2, phian3 si7 thou5, chiah8-liau2 chiu7 hou5-tou5; a-phian3 chit8 e7 gian3, bo5 lun7 sim2-mih8 su7 to kaN2 choe3.  ThiN-e7 kan e5 lang5, bo5 tang3 sng3 khoan2, chiau3 chhin-chhiuN7 teng2-bin7 so2 kong2, chit kui2 khoan2 e5 lang5, sui-jian5 sou2 tit-tioh8 e5 hak8-bun7 kap ka3-si7 long2 siang7 chit8 iuN7, m7-ku2 chai5-tiau7 a2 ham-ban7, chun-kui3 a2 pi-chian7, si7 toa7-toa7 bo5 saN-tang5.  Sou2-i2 lang5 ti7 chit se3-kan, eng- kai tioh8 hun3-chi3 lai5 kiaN5 ho2 lou7; na7 bo5 chiu7 kou-hu7 pe7-bu2 iuN2-chhi7 e5 kong-lo5, kap sian-siN teh ka3-si7 e5 un-tek.  Chhin-chhiuN7 teng2-bin7 kong2 hit nng7 chan5 kou3-su7, tioh8 chiong lan2 e5 hak3-bun7 lai5 choe3 u7 lou7-eng7  e5 su7; m7-thang chhin-chhiuN7 in tit-tioh8 hit ho7 ho2 ioh8, kan-ta liah8 choe3 soe2 chhiu2 e5 lou7-eng7.    
Iu2 beng5 bu5 sit8
Song3 kok u7 chit8 e5 lang5, ti7 lou7.-nih8 teh kiaN5-iu5, hut-jian5 khoaN3-kiN3 lou7-tiong u7 chit8 pau mih8, chiu7 ka7 i khioh khi2 lai5, theh8 kau3 in tau; thau2 khui chit8 e7 khoaN3, goan5-lai5 si7 chhan5-hng5 e5 khoe3-kng3, tat8-tit kui2-na7 ban7 gun5.  Chiu7 hoaN-hi2 kau3 boe7  kou3-tit, eng7 chit8 e5 kui7-a2 toe2-khi2-lai5, siu toa3 bat8-chiat8 e5 sou2-chai7.  Chiu7 ka7 i e5 chhu3-piN chhin-chhek peng5-iu2 kong2, Goa2 sng3 si7 ho2-giah8 lang5, lin2 chai mah?     
Lun7 kau3 se3-kan lang5, phe-si2 chin7-lat8 teh keng3- cheng--e5, bo5 m7 si7 ui7-tioh8 mia5-siaN chai5-li7 chit nng7 hang7.  U7 lang5 tit-tioh8 chit8 e5 bo5 lou7 bo5 eng7 khang-hu e5 mia5-siaN, ka-ki7 chiu7 phin2-phong2 kau3 bo5 soah; si7 na2 chhin-chhiuN7 hit ho7 khioh-tioh8 khoe3-kng3, ka- ki7 kong2 si7 ho2-giah8 lang5 chit8-poaN-iuN7.  
Phong3-hong bo5 toe2
 Ian ong5 chin ai3 bi5-soe3 e5 ki5-kha2 mih8.  U7 chit8 e5 Oe7-kok e5 lang5 tui3 ong5 kong2, Goa2 oe7 eng7 chhi3-a2 e5 be2-liu, khek chiaN5 bu2 kau5 e5 heng5-chong7.  Ian ong5 toa7 hoaN- hi2, chiu7 eng7 chin choe7 e5 hong7-lok8 lai5 iuN2- chhi7 i.  Ong5 kong2, Goa2 ai3 khoaN3 li2 sou2 khek e5 bu2 kau5 siN choe3 chaiN2-iuN7.  Oe7 kok e5 lang5 kong2, Ong5 na7 beh khoaN3, tioh8 tai7-seng poaN3 ni5 ku2, m7 thang jip8 khi3 keng-lai7, m7 thang chiah8 chiu2, m7 thang chiah8 bah, ia7 tioh8 ti7 loh8 hou7 liau2 jit8 chhut e5 si5-chun7, ia7 m7 thang toa3 im3-ng2 e5 sou2- chai7, jian5-au7 chiah oe7 khoaN3-kiN3 goa2 khek hit ho7 bu2 kau5; na7 peng5-siong5 si5 si7 khoaN3 boe7 tioh8.  Ong5 thiaN-kiN3 chiah choe7 hang7 e5 ui5-lan5, chiu7 chiam7 chhiaN2 pang3 he7 teh.     
Keh bo5 loa7 ku2, u7 chit8 e5 Teng7 kok e5 Phah-thih sai-hu7 tui3 Ian ong5  kong2, Goa2 khoaN3-kiN3 na7 lang5 teh tiau-khek sim2-mih8 mih8-kiaN7, i sou2  eng7 e5 chhai5-liau7 tek-khak tioh8 ai3 pi2 sou2 beh khek e5 ke toa7 tam7-poh8, chiah  oe7 eng7 tit.  TaN hit e5 chhi3-a2 be2-liu sng3 si7 chiam-chiam lai7-lai7 e5 mih8, lang5  beh  tui3 tah-loh8 khi2 chhiu2 leh?  ChhiaN2 khoaN3 hit e5 Oe7 kok e5 lang5, si7 eng7 sim2-mih8 hong-hoat lai5 khek, chiu7 chai i oe7 hiau2-tit a2 boe7.  Ong5 kong2,  Ho2; chiu7 tui3 Oe7 kok e5 lang5 kong2, Goa2 ai3 khoaN3 li2 sou2 khek e5 si7 chaiN-iuN7.   Oe7 kok e5 lang5 kong2, ChhiaN2 theng3-hau7 goa2 to3 lai5 khi3 goan2 chhu3-nih8   theh8; chiu7 than3 chit e5 phang7, choe3 i to5-chau2 khi3 liau2.   
Hian7-si5 iau2 u7 choe7-choe7 be5-sin3 su7, na7 kong2 kau3 sin5-sian kui2-koai3, tak8 e5 chiN3 kau3 khia7-chin khia7-hian7.  Na7 tau5 he7 liau2 chhau3-kham2 u7 than3 in e5 i3-su3, chiu7 kong2 put-chi2 hian2-hek leng5-siaN3; ia7  na7 he7 liau2 bo5 eng3-giam7, ia7 m7-kaN2 kong2 si7 put8 bo5 leng5-siaN3,  chiu7 siN-chhut chin choe7 thoe3 put8 jia-kham3 e5  oe7.  Siok8-gu2 kong2,  Put8 che7 iN5, kong-ma2 che7 piN2.  Ki5-sit8 chha5-kho2 khi2 lai5, toe7-bin7-chiuN7  beh thai3 u7 sin5 sian leh; put-ko3 si7 lang5 liap-cho7--e5, lai5 teh phian3 lang5 na7-tiaN7.  Si7  
tu2-tu2 chhin-chhiuN7 hit e5 Oe7 kok e5 lang5, kong2 i oe7 toa3 chhi3-a2  be2-liu khek bu2-kau5 e5 heng5 chit8-poaN-iuN7. 
Tioh8 chiau3-kou3 sin-the2
Gak8-cheng3 Chu2-chhun beh loh8 in tiaN5- nih8 e5 gim5-kiN5-a2, tah8 m7 tu2 ho2, sit-gou7 siong- tioh8 ka-ki7 e5 kha-kut.  Kau3 i2-keng i-ho2 kui2-na7 jit8 lah, iau2 bo5 chhut-khi3 kiaN5; bin7- nih8 u7 chin m7 hoaN-hi2 e5 khoan2.  I e5 hak8- seng chiu7 mng7 i kong2, Sian-siN in-ui7 sit- gou7 siong-tioh8 kha, taN i2-keng ho2 chiah ku2 lah, iau2 m7 bat chhut mng5, koh chin hoan5-lo2 e5 khoan2, m7 chai si7 sim2-mih8 ian5- kou3?  Gak8-cheng3 Chu2-chhun in3 i kong2, Lin2 an2-ni mng7 kai3 ho2; na7 m7 bat tioh8 ka7 in kong2.  In-ui7 goa2 bat thiaN-kiN3 Cheng- chu2 teh kong2, kong2 i siu7 Khong2-chu2 e5 ka3-si7, seh-tioh pe7-bu2 hou7 lan2 oan5-choan5 e5 sin-the2, lan2 ia7 tioh8 oan5-choan5 lai5 heng5 i, m7 thang siong-hai7-tioh8 seng-khu, ia7 m7 thang sun2-sit heng5-hai5, chiah thang kio3 choe3 si7 hau3-chu2.  Kun-chu2 e5 lang5 m7 kaN2 chit8 bak8-nih ku2 pang3 boe7 ki3-tit chit ku3 e5 ka3-si7; sou2-i2 goa2 chiah chin hoan5-lo2.  An2- ni kho2-kian3 sin-the2 m7 si7 lan2 sai-khia e5, sng3 si7 pe7-bu2 e5.     
TaN siN lan2 e5 sin-the2 kap iuN2 chhi7 lan2 e5, sng3 si7 pe7- bu2; siuN2-su3 lan2 e5 leng5-hun5 e5, chiu7-si7 thiN Pe7.  Sin- the2 pi2-pheng7 leng5-hun5, chu7-jiang5 si7 leng5-hun5 khah tui3-tiong7; pe7-bu2 pi2-pheng7 thiN Pe7, chu7 jian5 si7 thiN Pe7 khah chun-kui3.  Seng3-keng u7 kong2, Lang3 e5 sin-the2 si7 Siong7-te3 e5 tian7, lang3 na7 sun2-hai7 sin the2, chiu7-si7 sun2-hai7 Siong7-te3 e5 tian7, hit e5 choe7 chu7-jian5 koh khah tang7.  M7 ku2 se3-kan lang5 u7 e5 ai3 khai, ai3 hoa7, chiah8 a phian3, heng3 poah8 kiau2, lai5 sng2-hai7 in  e5 sin-the2 kap cheng-sin5, sim-chi3 choe3 chhut phaiN2 tai7, lai5 hoan7-tioh8 kok hoat, chiong sin the2 khi3 siu7 heng5-hoat8.  M7-na7 leng5 jiok8 tioh8 pe7-bu2 hou7 lan2 e5 sin-the2, boe7 chheng-choe3 u7-hau3 tit, ia7 sun2-hai7- tioh8 Siong7-te3 e5 tian7, hit ho7 choe7 koh khah chhim,  koh khah tang7.  Chiau3 an2-ni khoaN3, lan2 se3-kan lang5 thai2 thang khoaN3-khi n lan2 e5 seng3-khu leh?     
Ke3-sit tioh8 kin2 koe2
Beng7-chu2 e5 chheh kong2.  Bat u7 chit e5 lang5, in chhu3-piN e5 koe na7 lai5 in tau, i chiu7 ka7 i liah8-khi2-lai5 thai5.  Na7 tak8 jit8 khoaN3-kiN3, i ia7 tak8 jit8 ka7 i liah8-khi2-lai5.  bo5 koh pang3 hou7 i chhut-khi3.  Au7-lai5 u7 lang5 ka7 i kong2, Peng5-iu2 ah, li2 tak8 jit8 liah8 lin2 chhu3-piN e5 koe, sit8-chai7 si7 boe7 eng7 tit, chhiaN2 li2 tioh8 kin2-kin2 kai2-ko3.  Hit e5 lang5 in3 kong2, Liah8 lang5 e5 koe, goa2 ku2-ku2 chiu7 chai si7 boe7 an2-ni choe3 tit.  TaN i2-keng siu7 li2 e5 ho2 ka3-si7, kam-goan7 tui3 taN kai2-ko3, au7 ke3 chit8 geh8-jit8 chiah liah8 chit8 chiah chiu7 ho2; tan2-hau7 me5-ni5 khi2, chiah long2 boh8- tit liah8.     
Hian7-si5 ia7 u7 chin choe7 lang5, i2-keng chai chiah8 a-phian3 ai3 lim-chu2, i2-kip8 phiau5 tou2 hit ho7 tai7-chi3, long2 si7 bo5 chiau3 to7-li2.  Na7 tu2-tioh8 u7 lang5 khou2- khng3 in, in chiu7 in3 kong2, Goa2 khoaN-a2-si7 to beh  koe2.  Ia7 u7 kong2, Goa2 au7-geh8 chiu7 beh koe2, u7 e5 kong2, me2 ni5 goa2 chiu7 beh ka7 i tu5-khi3.  Che chin- chiaN3 si7 ka-ki7 phian3 ka-ki7; ki3-jian5 chai si7 bo5 chiau3 to7-li2, chiu7 tioh8 liam5-piN koe2-piN3; beh thai3 tioh8 theng3-hau7 me5-ni5 a2 si7 ti7-si7 leh?  Khong2-chu2 kong2, U7 ke3-sit chiu7 m7-thang pin5-toaN7 koe2, chiu7-si7 teh kong2 chit khoan2 e5 lang5.      
Hou5-hun7 bong2 ke3
Che5 soan-ong5 ai3 thiaN u5 e5 gak8-khi, (chhin-chhiuN7 tong7-siau), tak8-pai2 teh pun5 e5 si5-chun7, tioh8 saN pah lang5 choe3 chit8-e7 lai5 pun5.  Tong-si5 u7 chit8 e5 Lam5-kok e5 sian- siN lai5 kiN3soan-ong5, chheng2 beh jip8 chit e5 pun5 u5 e5 chit-hun7. soan-ong5 put-chi2 hoaN-hi2, tak8 geh8-jit8 ia7 su3 chin choe7 e5 hong7-lok2, kau3-giah8 thang iuN2-chhi7 kui2-na7 pah lang5.  Au7-lai5 soan-ong5 si2-khi3, Bin2- ong5 chiap-khi2-lai5 che7 ui7; ia7 iu5-goan5 chin ai3 thiaN u5 e5 gak8-khi3.  Chong2-si7 Bin2-ong5 m7 ai3 hiah choe7 lang5 saN-kap pun5, i ai3 sui5 lang5 chit8-e5 chit8-e5 pun5 hou7 i thiaN.  Hit e5 Lam5-kok sian-siN thiaN-kiN3 chit ho7 siau-sit, chiu7 than3 cha2 choe3 i to5-chau2 khi3 liau2.   
Chiau3 an2-ni khoaN3, chit e5 Lam5-kok sian-siN, goan5-pun2 si7 chit2-tiam2-a2 pun5 u5 e5 pun2-su7 to bo5.  In- ui7 khoaN3-kiN3 Soan-ong5 hoaN-hi2 thiaN saN pah lang5 choe3 chit8 choe5 pun5, liah8 choe3 che si7 chin ho2 e5 ki- hoe7, oe7-thang ka2-mou7 kap in hou5-hun7 chai7-lai7; ka-ki7 pun5 liau2 ho2 thiaN a2 si7 m7 ho2 thiaN, phah-sng3 Soan-ong5 ia7 thiaN boe7 chhut.  Au7-lai5 Bin2-ong5 iu7 ai3 beh sui5 lang5 chit8-e5 chit8-e5 lai5 pun5, an2-ni chiu7 chit8-tiam2-a2 kian3-siau3 to boe7 kham3-tit, boe7 bian2-tit tioh8 tng- bin7 lau3-khui3; sou2-i2 put-tek-put tioh8 tai7-seng to2- chau2.  Kho2-sioh se3-kan chhin-chhiuN7 chit e5 Lam5- kok sian-siN e5 lang5 si7 chin choe7; bo5 lun7 si7 choe3 koaN, a2-si7 ka3 oh8, i2-kip8 choe3 thoan5-to7 e5, eng2-eng2 u7 chit teng2 ho7 e5 lang5; chi2-u7 chai hou5-hun7 lai5 that- giah8, choe3 tai7-chi3 lo2-lo2 chho2-chho2 chiu7 ka7 i ke3 khi3, siuN7 thang tou5-bou5 hit si5 e5 hong7-lok8, tek-khak bo5 siuN7 ka-ki7 e5 pun2-su7 chaiN2-iuN7, ia7 bo5 siuN7-kau3 tai7 chi3 e5 seng3-pai7 si7 chai2-iuN7; lai5 ti3-kau3 siong thian hai7 li2, gou7 lang5 e5 toa7 su7.  Long2 bo5 siuN7 kau3 au7-lai5 tek- khak u7 chit8 e5 jit8-ki5, chiong tak8 lang5 sou2 choe3 e5 kang, ia7 beh chit8-e5 chit8-e5 tng bin7 ka7 i chhi3, lai5 tiaN7- tioh8 in e5 siuN2-hoat8.  Kau3 hit si5 khiok bo5 sou2-chai7 thang khi3 to5-siam2, m7-si7 chhin-chhiuN7 hit e5 Lam5- kok sian-siN, chau2-li7 chiu7 oe7 soah tit.   
M7 thang long7 hiam2
 Chong-chu2 u7 kong2, U7 chit8 e5 song3- hiong lang5, kan-ta kho3 chit chhioh8-a2 teh tou7 oah8.  U7 chit8 jit8 i e5 kiaN2 chhang3 chui2 bi7 jip8 hai2 toe2 chin chhim, tit-tioh8 chit8 liap8 chin-chu, tat8 u7 kang2 chheng gun5 e5 ke3-chiN5.  In lau7-pe7 chit8-e7 khoaN3-kiN3, kiaN- liau2 i e5 kiaN2 tham-sim koh khi3 chhe7, chiu7 theh8 chioh8-thau5 ka7 i tok hou7 phoa3; chiah  kong2, Che tat8 kang2 chheng gun5 e5 chu, un2-tang3 si7 chin chhim e5 hai2-toe2, le5-leng5 am7-kun2-e7 e5; li2 tit-tioh8 chit e5 chu, liong7- pit si7 in-ui7 le5-leng5 teh khun3; na7-si7 cheng-sin5 e5 si5, tek-khak si7 bo5 siN3-mia7.     
Lun7 kau3 se3-kan chiu2 sek chai5 khi3, bo5 kong2 chit8 pai2 chiu7 oe7 hai7 lang3.  Siok8-gu2 kong2, Chiu2 put chui3 jin5, jin5 chu7 chui3; sek put be5 jin5, jin5 chu7 be5.  Chhin-chhiuN7 chiah8 a-phian3, bo5 kong2 chit8 poaN3 pai2 chiu7 oe7  tiau5; tai7-seng chiah8-liau2 chhu3-bi7 chhu3-bi7, u7 chiah8 ia7 an2-ni, bo5 chiah8 ia7 an2-ni.  Na2 chiah8 na2  
ku2, o2 ho3! bo5 chiah8 boe7-eng7-tit lah.  Ia7 na7 an2-ni chai thang  kiu-kha, koaN2-kin2 lai5 koe2 ia7 ho2; m7 ku2 long2 si7 ju2 chiah8 ju2 toa7, na2 ku2 gian3 na2 tang7, chio2-chio2 oe7 chhin-chhiuN7 hit e5 lau7 lang5 e5 koat-sim.     
Ia7 koh chhin-chhiuN7 poah8-kiau2 lang5, ia7 si7 an2-ni. U7 si5 tiau5-kou3-i3 tau3 lang5 lai5 choe3 kiau2-be5, tai7-seng poah8 sio2 khoa2 e5 si5, tiau5-ti5 pang3 ho7 i iaN5; i chiu7 liah8 choe3 ka-ki7 chin gau5 poah8, sim-koaN na2 toa7, siuN7 beh iaN5 khah choe7.
