Hit si5 in chiu7 eng7 hoat-tou7 lai5 ka7 i; iah8 chit8-e7 su, tit8-tit8 siuN7 beh phiN5, na2 phiN5 na2 gia5 iN5.  Sim kong5 so3 jiat8, cheng3-keng su7 pang3-sak liau2-liau2; mi5-jit8 chim3-chu3 teh poah8; bu2-long7 kau3 kheng-ka tong7 san2, lian5 siN3-mia7 u7 si5 soa3 bo5-khi3. TaN chit e5 lau7 lang5 e5 sou2 choe3, si7 kiaN i e5 hau7-siN, chit8 pai2 u7 choan2-chiah8; au7 ke3 koh khi3 choe3, tioh8 piN3 kau3 bo5 pan-gi5 chiah soah be2.  Sou2-i2 chiong hit  liap8 chu tok hou7 phoa3, hou7 i e5 kiaN2 oe7 si2 sim, boe7 koh khi3 choe3.   
Sin5 ia7 u7 kok.
Che5 kok eng7 peng kong-phah Lou2 kok, ai3 beh tit-tioh8 Lou2 kok e5 gim5-tiaN2.  Lou2 kok e5 peng tong3 boe7 tiau5, chiu7 kah lang5 chu3 chit8 e5 ke2 e5 tiaN2, sang3 khi3 Che5 kok. Che5 hou5 khoaN3-liau2 giau5-gi5, kiaN-liau2 m7 si7 chin e5 gim5-tiaN2, chiu7 chhe  lang5 sang3 to3-tng2 khi3 Lou2 kok, ia7 ka7 Lou2 hou5 kong2, Na7 si7 Liu2-ha7 Hui7  kong2 che si7 chin e5 gim5-tiaN2, goan2 Che5 kok e5 jin5-kun chiu7 beh  seng5-siu7 i.  Lou2 hou5 chiu7 khi3 thau3 Liu2-ha7 Hui7 b h lai5 kan-cheng3 chit e5 tiaN2.  Liu2-ha7 Hui7 kong2, Kun eng7 gim5-tiaN2 hian3 hou7 Che5 kok, si7 ui7-tioh8 beh po2-choan5 kun e5 kok,Chong2-si7 sin5 ia7 u7 kok, chiu7-si7 sin5 e5 sin3-sit8.   Hian7-chai7 kun beh pho3-hoai7 sin5 e5 kok, lai5 po2-choan5 kun e5 kok, chit ho7 tai7-chi3 beh thai3 oe7 eng7 tit?   Lou2 hou5 bo5 hoat-tou7, chiu7 eng7 chin e5 gim5-tiaN2 sang khi3 hou7 Che5 kok.     
Lun7 kau3 lang5 oah8 ti7 se3-kan, bo5 lun7 si7 choe3 koaN choe3 sai3, a2 si7 khui hang5 che7 tiam3, boe2-boe7 than3 chiah8, bo5 lun7 si7 tui3 goa7-kok, a2 si7 pun2-toe7 sou2-chai7 e5 lang5, lai5-ong2 kau-chiap, long2 tioh8 eng7 sin3-sit8 choe3 kau-che3 e5 so2-si5.  Na7 si7 bo5 sin3-sit8, si7 chhin-chhiuN7 toa7 tiuN chhia bo5 chhia-taN, soe3 tiuN chhia bo5 chhia piN5; khoaN3 beh thai3 oe7 kiaN5 oe7 tin2-tang7 leh?  Hian7-si5 u7 chit8 khoan2 e5 lang5, chi2-u7 oe7 hiau2-tit kong2 peh8-chhat8, bo5 iaN2 bo5 chiah, siN kau3 u7 ki u7 hioh8, kong2 kau3 kui-nng5 tho3, lai5 moa5-phian3 lang5; bo5 siuN7 kau3 phah phaiN2 mia5-siaN, pi2 hit e5 sit kok koh  
khah iau3-kin2.  Sim7-chi3 u7 e5 beng5 chai si7 hoan7-tioh8 cha3-khi, oe7 liah8 khi3 pan7 choe7, in ia7 si7 tiau5-kou3-i3 beh choe3; chin-chiaN3 si7 thang siong-sim e5 su7.     Siong7-te3 chap tiau5 kai3 u7 kong2, M7 thang lam7-sam2 choe3 kan-cheng3. Khong2-chu2 ia7 u7 kong2, Beh liau7-li2 kok, tioh8 kiong- keng3 in e5 tai7-chi3, koh tioh8 sin3-sit8.  Ia7 kong2, Choe3 gin2-na2 iau3-kin2 tioh8 soe3 ji7, koh sin3-sit8.  Chhin- chhiuN7 chit ho7 oe7, u7 choe7-choe7 khoan2 e5 ka3-si7;kho2- kiau3 sin3-sit8 si7 te7-it po2-poe3, te7-it tioh8 tui3-tiong7 lah.   
Ut8 pang7 siong chhi5.
Chian3 kok e5 si5, Sou Chin5 tui3 Ian ong5 kong2, U7 chit8 jit8 ho5-nih8 chit8 liap8 pang7 (hun2-gio5 e5 khoan2)chhut-lai5 ti7 hoaN7-teng2, chiong khak thi2-khui teh hou7 phak8 jit8. Hut-jian5 u7 chit8 chiah ut8 (chiau2-a2 e5 mia5, siong5-siong5 ti7 chui2-nih8 tho2 chiah8)khoaN3- kiN3, chiu7 tui3 hit e5 pang7 e5 bah ka7 i tok  teh; hit liap8 pang7 ia7 chiong khak hap8 oa2 lai5, tui3 ut8 e5 chhui3 ka7 ngoeh8-teh.  Ut2 chiu7 kong2, Kin-a2-jit8 bo5 loh8 hou7, bin5-a2-chai3 bo5 loh8 hou7, chiu7 u7 pang7 bah thang chiah8. Pang7 ia7 kong2, Kin-a2-jit8 bo5 chhut jit8, bin5- a2-chai3 koh bo5 chhut jit8, tek-khak u7 si2 ut8. An2-ni liong2 peng5 khiu2-teh m7 pang3.  Chin tu2 ho2, u7 chit8 e5 tho2-hi5 lang5 tui3 hia ke3, khoaN3-kiN3 chit8 chiah ut8 kap chit8 liap8 pang7, tiN5-tiN5 ka2-ka2 choe3 chit8 tui, m7 kheng2 saN-niu7; i chiu7 choe3 chit8-e7 ka7 i liah8-khi3. Siok8-gu2 kong2, Ut2 pang7 siong chhi5, gu5-jin5 tek li7, chiu7-si7 chit e5 kou2-tian2.     
Koh iau2 chit8 hang7, ti7 oa2 saN-chap8 ni5 cheng5, Lak8-ku-li2 hit si3 e5 lang5, iau2-be7 siu7 bun5-beng5 e5 kau3-hoa3, ti3-sek be7 khui, boe2- boe7 e5 su7 long2 bo5 kap lang5 ke3-kau3.  Bat u7 chit8 pai2, nng7 e5 hit sou2-chai7 e5 lang5 khi3 phah-lah8; kau3 jit8 beh am3 e5 si5, nng7 e5 lang5 u7 phah saN chiah lok8, chiu7 gia5 chhut lai5 ti7 lou7-piN the pun.  Chit8 lang5 pun chit8 chiah, m7 ku2 iau2 u7 chit8 chiah.  Na7 chit e5 thoa-ke3-lai5, hit-e5 chiu7 kong2, An2-ni li2 khah ke.  Iah8 hit-e5 thoa-ke3-khi3, chit-e5 iu7 kong2, An2-ni li2 khah choe7.  Boe7 hiau2- tit phoa3 peng5 lai5 pun, kan-ta kui chiah thoa-lai5 thoa-khi3.  Teh pun boe7 piN5,ia7 chhau3-khiau2 tu2-tioh8 chit8 e5 boe7 chap8-he3 e5 tui3 hia ke3, khoaN3-kiN3 in an2-ni teh  pun, pun long2 boe7 piN5, i chiu7 oa2 khi3, chit8 lang5 pun chit8 chiah hou7 in, ia7 ka-ki7  
thoa chit8 chiah lai5 bin7-thau5-cheng5, mng7 in kong2, Chit8 lang5 chit8 chiah an2-ni u7 piN5 bo5?  Hit nng7 e5 lang5 khoaN3-liau2 toa7  hoaN-hi2 kong2, Li2 chin kong-to7, chin gau5 pun; thai3 m7 khah cha2 lai5 teh, hou7 goan2 chin ku2 teh pun boe7 piN5?     
Lun7 kau3 se3-kan lang5, choe7-choe7 si7 in-ui7 chit8 e5  sio2-khoa2 e5 tai7-chi3, m7 kheng2 saN niu7.  Li2 kang7 goa2 chit8 e7, goa2 ia7 beh kang7 li2 chit8 e7 , lai5 tho2 phiN5.  Li2 me7 goa2 chit8 siaN, goa2 chiu7 me7 li2 kui2-na7 siaN, thang  khah-iaN5 i, long2 si7 beh chiam3 pan gi5.  U7 si5 in ui7  chit8 e5 sio2-sio2 khoa2-khoa2 e5 tai7-chi3, ia7 long7 kau3 saN ko3 kui2-na7 ni5.  Lang5 na7 khou2-khng3 in, in kong2 si7 cheng khi3 put cheng chai5; chit peng5 m7 kheng2 jin7 su, hit peng5 m7 kheng2 jin7 chbo3, chiong chiN5 thoa teh ia7, cheng3-keng tai7-chi3 pang3-sak liau2 liau2.  Kau3 chai thang hoan2-hoe2 e5 si5,liong2 peng5 to long2 kheng-ka tong7-san2; chi2-u7 ui7-tioh8 beh thau2 chit8 tiam2 khui3, hoan2-tng2 chiah8 chit8 e5 toa7 khek-khui.  Sou2-i2 lang5 oe7 jim2-nai7, oe7 ho5-sun7, si7 te7 it iau3 kin2.  Chiu7- si7 hit e5 Lak8-ku-li2 lang5, in-ui7 khah tiau5-tit8, sou2-i2 liau2 sio2-khoa2; na7 beh eng7 kiong5-e5 lai5 saN chiN, kiaN-hau2 soa3 bo5 thang pun poaN3 chiah.     
Tioh8 chiau3 kong-to7
Liat8-kok e5 si5, Chin3 To7-kong mng7 Ki5 Hong5-iong5 kong2, Hian7-si5 Lam5-iong5 iau2- be7 u7 koaiN7-koaN, m7 chai sim2-mih8 lang5 oe7 kham-tit tng chit e5 chit-jim7.  Ki5 Hong5- iong5 kong2, Kai2 Hou5 oe7 eng7 tit.  Chin3 To7-kong kong2, Kai2 Hou5 kiam2  m7 si7 kap li2 u7 oan-siu5 e5 lang5 mah?  Ki5 Hong5-iong5 in3 kong2, Kun si7 mng7 goa2 khoaN3 sim2-mih8 lang5 oe7 kham-tit tng chit e5 chit-jim7, to m7 si7 mng7 goa2 e5 siu5-jin5.   Chin3 To7-kong kong2, Ho2; chiu7 eng7 i.  Kok-lai7 e5 lang5 ko2-jian5 long2 o-lo2 i ho2.  Ke3 bo5 joa7 ku2, Chin3 To7-kong koh mng7 Ki5  Hong5-iong5 kong2, Kok-nih8 bo5 u7 nia2 peng e5 koaN, m7 chai sim2-mih8 lang5 oe7 kham-tit tng chit e5 chit-jim7.  Ki5 Hong5-iong5 kong2, Ngou2-a2 oe7 eng7 tit.  Chin3 To7-kong kong2, Ngou2-a2 kiam2 m7 si7 li2 e5 hau7-siN mah?  Ki5 Hong5-iong5 kong2, Kun si7 mng7 goa2 khoaN3 sim2-mih8 lang5 oe7 kham-tit tng chit e5 chit-jim7, to m7 si7 mng7 goa2 e5 hau7-siN ah.  To7-kong kong2, Ho2; chiu7 chhai2 eng7 i.  Kok-lai7 e5 lang5 ia7 si7 o-lo2 eng7 chit e5 lang5 chin tioh8 chin ho2. Khong2-chu2 thiaN-kiN3 an2-ni chiu7 kong2, Ki5 Hong5-iong5 sou2 kong2 e5 oe7, chin-chiaN3 si7 bo5 chho3.  I tui3 ti7 goa7-bin7 e5 teh ku2-chian3, bo5 khioh oan3-hun7, kong2 che si7 lan2 e5  
oan- siu5.  Tui3 ti7 lai7-bin7 e5 teh ku2-chian3, bo5 pi7 hiam5-gi5, kong2 che si7 lan2 e5 hau7-siN.  Che chin-chiaN3 si7 kong-to7 e5 lang5 ah.     
Lun7-kau3 hian7-kim e5 lang5, toa7-poaN3 si7 liah8 jin5- cheng5 khoaN3 khah tui3-tiong7, bo5 lun7 hit e5 lang5 e5 pun2-su7 si7 chaiN2-iuN7.  Siat-su2 goa2 e5 siu5-jin5, tek-khak si7 kong2 in m7 ho2; ia7 na7 si7 goa2 e5 chhin-chhek, chiu7 eng7 hiah e5 ho2 oe7 lai5 o-lo2 in; long2 m7 kheng2 kong2 kong-to7 e5 oe7.  Bu2 Sam3-su bat kong2, Kap  goa2 ho2 e5, chiu7-si7 ho2 lang5; kap goa2 phaiN2 e5, chiu7-si7 phaiN2 lang5; sit8-chai7 chin-chiaN3 si7 u7 iaN2.  Chong2-si7 lan2 kau3-hoe7 lai7 e5 lang5 iau3-kin2 m7 thang chhin-chhiuN7 an2-ni; tioh8 oh8 Ki5 Hong5-iong5 chiau3 kong-to7 chiah ho2.  U7 si5 in2-chin3 lang5 lai5 jip8 seng3-kau3, a2 si7 ku2- chian3 lang5 lai5 thak8 Toa7-oh8, long2 tioh8 chiau3 hit e5 lang5 e5 phin2-heng7 chim-chiok lai5 kong2; m7 thang u7 chit8-tiam2-a2 phian-than2 e5 sim.  In-ui7 lan2 sou2 in2-chin3 ku2-chian3 e5 lang5, na7 choe3-liau2 u7 ho2 bou5-iuN7, chiu7 lan2 ia7 u7 eng5-kng.  Siat-su2 sou2 chian3 e5 lang5, in e5 sou2 choe3 long2 bo5 chiau3 lan2 ku2-chian3 hit si5 e5 oe7, a2-si7 kau3 poaN3-tiong-tng5 chiah taN2-chha3, chiu7 lan2 ku2-chian3 e5 lang5 ia7 chin phaiN2 se3-bin7; boe7 bian2-tit hou7 lang5 kong2 lan2 si7 bo5 chiau3 kong-to7, a2-si7 kong2 lan2 boe7 bat lang5.  Sou2-i2 kou2-cha2 e5 hoat-tou7, na7 ku2-chian3-tioh8 gau5 lang5, ko2-jian5 u7 li7-ek ti7 kok-ka, chiu7 po2-ku2 e5 lang5 ia7 tit-tioh8 siuN2-su3; iah8 na7 chian3 m7 tioh8 lang5, choe3- liau2 m7 ho2 u7 hoan7-choe7, hit e5 po2-ku2 e5 lang5 ia7 tioh8 lian5-cho7.  Chhin-chhiuN7 chit-tiap8 e5 po2-cheng3-jin5 tioh8 lian5-tai3 in e5 chek-seng5 hit khoan2.  Kho2-kian3 teh chian3 lang5 e5 koan-he7 si7 chin toa7, m7-thang sui5- pian7 hut-liok8 i .     
Chha5 koe u7 oan5-choan5 e5 tek-heng7
Ki2 Seng2-chu2 teh ka7 Chiu Soan-ong5 chhi7 hit ho7 sio-phah koe;  i2-keng ka3 kech3ap jit8 ku2, Soan-ong5 mng7 kong2, Chitchiah koe oe7  eng7 tit hou7 i sio phah tit a2 boe7?  Ki2 Seng2-chu2 kong2, Chit chiah koe  iau2-koh si7 chin kiau-ngou7, gau5 sai2 seng3-te7, boe7 oe7 eng7 tit hou7 i kap  pat8 chiah sio-phah tit.  Au7-lai5 koh ke3 chap8-jit8, Soan-ong5 koh mng7  i kong2, Chit chiah koe oe7 hou7 i sio phah tit a2 boe7?  Ki2 Seng2-chu2 kong2,  Chit chiah koe iau2-ku2 si7 na7 thiaN-kiN3 sim2-mih8 hiang2, i chiu7 thi5, a2-si7 khoaN3-tioh8 sim2-mih8 iaN2, i chiu7 jip; iau2-be7 thang kap pat8 chiah sio- phah tit.  Iu7-koh ke3 chap8 jit, Soan-ong5 iu5-goan5 teh  mng7, Ki2 Seng2-chu2  kong2,  
Iau2 si7 boe7 eng7 tit, in-ui7 na7 teh khoaN3 sim2-mih8, iu5-goan5 chin chhiN-kong5, ia7 gau5 siu7-khi3; sou2-i2 boe7 eng7 tit.  Bak8-chit8-nih iu7 ke3 chap8 jit8,  Soan-ong5 iu7 koh chiau3 cheng5 an2-ni mng7, Ki2 Seng-chu2 chiah kong2, Chha-put-to oe7 eng7-tit hou7 i khi3 sio-phah tit lah.  Sui-jian5 u7 pat8 chiah  koe teh thi5, i khiok na2-chun2 bo5 thiaN-kiN3, chu7-chu7 chai7-chai7, put-tong7 seng-sek, khoaN3-liau2 chhin-chhiuN7 chha5 e5 koe; sou2-i2 tek-heng7 sng3 si7 chiau5-pi7, pat8 chiah e5 koe khoaN3-tioh8 i, boe7 bian2-tit ka-ki7 to3-the3 tui3  au7-bin7 khi3 liau2.     
Chi-na2 Tiong5-kang hit si3, na7 kong2 lang5 e5 pun2- su7 bo5 cheng-kong, u7 chit8 ku3 siok8-gu2 kong2, PoaN3 pan5 chhou3.  Tai7-khai3 si7 kong2, Chhou3 toe2 poaN3-pan5 na7-tiaN7, sio2-khoa2 chit8-e7 io5 chiu7 u7 siaN; na7 toe2 kau3 tiN7 lai5 ka7 i io5, chiu7 bo5 thiaN-kiN3.  Chhin-chhiuN7 hit ho7 bat chit8-hang7 poaN3-hang7, sio2-khoa2 u7 to7-hak8 e5 lang5, i chiu7 chin kiau-ngou7 chu7-ko, na7 kap lang5 choe3 tui, chiu7 phin2 i e5 pun2-su7.  Siat-su2 si7 chin-chiaN3 to7- hak8 khah koaiN5, tek-heng7 chin ho2, hak8-bun7 ia7 chhim hit khoan2 e5 lang5, in chiu7 hoan2-tng2 chin  khiam-pi.  Leng7-goa7 u7 chit8 khoan2, beng5-beng5 si7 u7, khoaN3-liau2 na2 chhin-chhiuN7 bo5, beng5-beng5 si7 chat8- chat8, khoaN3-liau2 na2-chun2 khang-khang e5 heng5- chong7.  Siok8-gu2-u7 kong2, Chin chiong-kun put- chai7 ti7 jiong5 chong.  Ia7 kong2, U7--e5 m7 kong2, bo5--e5 teh phin2-phong2, chiu7-si7 chit e5 i3-su3.  
M7 chai ka-ki7 u7 piN7
 Pian2 Chhiok si7 Tiong-kok kou2-cha2 e5 si5, choe3 u7 mia5-siaN e5 i-seng.   U7 chit8 jit8 tui3 Che5-kok keng-ke3, jip8-khi3 kiN3 Che5 Hoan5-kong, Pian2  Chhiok chiu7 ka7 Hoan5-kong kong2, Kun-hou5 e5 phe5-hu hian7-si5 u7 piN7 teh;  na7 bo5 i-ti7, chiu7 oe7 ju2 chhim.  Hoan5-kong kong2, Goa2 to bo5 piN7.  Ke3 gou7  jit8 au7, Pian2 Chhiok koh kiN3-tioh8 Hoan5-kong, iu7 ka7 i kong2, Kun-hou5 e5 piN7 i2-keng kau3 ti7 tng5 ui7 e5 sou2-chai7; na7 m7 i-ti7, oe7 ti3 khah chhim.  Hoan5-kong  ia7 bo5 in3 i.  Kau3 Pian2 Chhiok chhut khi3, Hoan5-kong put-chi2 m7 hoaN-hi2,  tui3 kun-sui5 i e5 lang5 kong2, He2, choe3 i-seng e5 lang5, ai3 than3 lang5 e5 chiN5,  beh tian2 in e5 pun2-su7; goa2 beng5-beng5 to bo5 sim2-mih8 m7 ho2, i ia7 kong2  goa2 u7 piN7.  Koh ke3 gou7 jit8, Pian2 Chhiok iu7 lai5 kiN3 Hoan5-kong, chit8-e7 khoaN3-tioh8, chiu7 oat8-tng2-sin choe3 i chhut-khi3.  Hoan5-kong chiu7 kio3  lang5 khi3 mng7 i, khoaN3 si7 chaiN-iuN7.  Pian2 Chhiok chiu7 kong2, PiN7 ti7  phe5-hu, eng7 ioh8 lai5 soe2, a2 si7 eng7 he2 lai5 ku3, chiu7 oe7 i tit.  PiN7 ti7 huih-meh8,  eng7 chu3-sia7 ia7 oe7 i tit.   
Na7 piN7 ti7 tng5-ui7 e5 sou2-chai7, eng7 ka, eng7 chiu2 e5 ioh8-lui7  ia7 koan2 oe7 tioh8.  PiN7 kau3 ti7 kut-chhe2, sui-jian5 si7 chip-chiang2 siN-si2 e5 koan5-peng3, ia7 bo5 hoat-tou7 liau2.  Hian7-si5 kun e5 piN7 i2-keng jip8 ti7 kut-chhe2;  goa2 sou2-i2 m7 kaN2 koh kong2 sim2-mih8.  Au7-lai5 koh ke3 gou7 jit8, Che5 Hoan5-kong hut-jian5 khi2 piN7, kio3 lang5 khi3 tiau3 Pian2 Chhiok; Pian2 Chhiok i2-keng choe3 i to5-siam2.  Ke3 bo5 joa7 ku2, Hoan5-kong chiu7 piN7 si2.     
Hian7-si5 choe7-choe7 hit khoan2 ui5-hui chok-tai2 e5 lang5, peng5-sou3 ia7 u7 hit ho7 ho2 e5 chhin-chiaN5 peng5- iu2 khou2-khng3 in, in khiok long2 m7 thiaN; kau3 au7-lai5 hou7 koaN-hu2 liah8 khi3 heng5-hoat8 teng7 choe7, chiah chai thang siuN7-tioh8 bou2 lang5 sou2 kong2 e5 oe7 si7 tioh8, chong2-si7 i2-keng bo5 lou7-eng liau2.  Koh chhin-chhiuN7 chit-tiap8 e5 Thoan5-tou7 sian-siN teh kong2 to7-li2, kin-a2-jit8 kio3 lang5 hoan2-hoe2 koe2-piN3, bin5-a2-chai3 ia7 si7 kio3 lang5 hoan2-hoe2 koe2-piN3, m7 ku2 se3-siok8 lang5 long2 m7 kheng2 hoan2-hoe2 koe2-piN3, koh m7 sin3 ka-ki7 u7 choe7. Kau3 au7-lai5 u7 chit8 jit8 khia7 ti7 sim2-phoaN3 tai5 cheng5, Siong7-te3 mng7 choe7 e5 si5-chun7, hit-tiap8 beh hoan2-hoe2, khiok si7 siuN ban7 lah.  
KiaN2 kan-cheng3 pe7 choe3 chhat8
Chhou2 kok u7 chit8 e5 tiau5-tit8 e5 lang5, in lau7-pe7 thau-khan lang5 e5 iuN5, i chau2-khi3 kong-tng5 chhut siu3.  KoaN-hu2 liah8 in lau7- pe7 lai5, in-ui7 i e5 kiaN2 choe3 kan-cheng3, bo5 oe7 thang chiN3, chiu7 teng7-choe7  beh thai5 i. Chit e5 tiau5-tit8 e5 lang5 iu7 chhiaN2 koaN-hu2 pang3 i e5 lau7-pe7, i kam-goan7 thoe3 i e5 lau7-pe7 si2.  Au7-lai5 kau3 teh-beh thai5 e5 si5-chun7, chit e5  lang5 tui3 hiah e5 ge5-iah8 kong2, Goan2 lau7-pe7 thau-khan lang5 e5 iuN5, goa2  khi3 tng koaN chhut siu3, an2-ni goa2 kiam2 m7 si7 chit8 e5 tiau5-tit8 koh sin3-sit8  e5 lang5 mah?  Goan2 lau7-pe7 hoan7-choe7 tioh8 thai5, goa2 kam-goan7 thoe3 i si2,  an2-ni goa2 kiam2 m7 si7 chit8 e5 hau3-chu2 mah?  Chhin-chhiuN7 goa2 chit  khoan2 e5 sin3-sit8 koh u7 hau3 e5 lang5, keng3-jian5 tioh8 hou7 lang5 thai5, chit kok  lai7 iau2 u7 sim2-mih8 lang5 m7 tioh8 thai5 leh?  Chhou2 ong5 thiaN-kiN chiah e5 oe7,  chiu7 sia3-bian2 hit e5 lang5 bo5 thai5.  Khong2-chu2 thiaN-kiN3 chiah kong2, Chin ki5-koai3 ah, u7 chit khoan2 e5 tiau5-tit8 lang5, sng3 choe3 si7 u7 sin3-sit8, keng3- jian5 eng7 in lau7-pe7 lai5 boe2 ho2 mia5-siaN hou7 lang5 o-lo2, chin-chiaN3 si7 ki5-koai3.     
 
Na7 lun7 se3-kan, eng2-eng2 u7 chit8 khoan2 e5 lang5, peng5-siong5-si5 mih8-iuN7 kan-khiau2 to u7, eng7 pah poaN khui2-khiat e5 ke3-bou5; na7 khoaN3-kiN3 bou2-mih8 lang5 khah gu5-chhun2, chiu7 beh khi3 khi-hu7 i, khoaN3-kiN3 sim2-mih8 lang5 khah loan2-jiok8, chiu7 beh khi3 hai7 i, long2 bo5 chit8 tiam2-a2 jin5-ai3 e5 sim-chiaN5, ia7 bo5 chit8 tiam2-a2 lin5-bin2 e5 cheng5-i3.  Kip8-chi3 kau3 au7-lai5, khi- hu7 lang5 ia7 khi-hu7 kau3 chiok lah, hai7 lang5 ia7 hai7 kau3 chin7 liau2, put-gi7 e5 chiN5-chai5 ia7 eng7 long2 boe7 liau2.  Hit-si5 khiok siuN7 beh chhe7 chit8 e5 ho2 lang5 e5 mia5 lai5 choe3;  chiu7 khi3 siu-li2 chit8 tiau5 kio5, a2 si7 khi3 cheng2-li2 chit8 keng bio7, sang3 lang5 kui2 nia2 mi5-hiu5, a2-si7 hoat tam7-poh8 bi2 hou7 song3-hiong lang5, chiu7 giam2-jian5 ka-ki7 liah8 choe3 ho2 lang5 teh choe3 ho2 su7. Chiau3 an2-ni khoaN3, in na7 beh chhin-chhiuN7 chit khoan2 e5 teh kiu5 ho2 lang5 e5 mia5-siaN, put-ju5 cha2-jit8 boh8-tit choe3 hit ho7 hai7 lang5 e5 tai7-chi3 kiam2 m7 si7 koh khah ho2 mah?       
Hoan2-hoe2 jin7 choe7
Chhit kok e5 si5, Lin7 Siong-ju5 sng3 si7 ho2 khau2-chai5, koh u7 tam2-lek8 e5 lang5, i u7 oan5- choan5 hit te3 po2-gek8 to3-lai5 Tio7-kok, ia7 ti7 Bin2-ti5 e5 sou2-chai7, bo5 leng5-jiok8-tioh8 i e5 kun-ong5.  Sou2-i2 Tio7-ong5 hong i choe3 siong7-kheng.  Chit-ui7 tian-to3 pi2 Liam5 Pho2 khah koaiN5.  Liam5 Pho2 chit8-e7 siuN7, Goa2 tui3 siau3-lian5 kau3 taN, keng-ke3 kang2 pah pai2 e5 cheng-chian3, chiah choe3 chiong- kun e5 chit; Lin7 Siong-ju5 put-ko3 kho3 i e5 khau2-chai5, hoan2-tng2 pi2 goa2 koaN choe3 khah koaiN5.  Chiu7 tui3 lang5 kong2.  Goa2 na7 tu2-tioh8 Siong-ju5 e5 si5, tek-khak beh leng5- jiok8 i.  Siong-ju5 thiaN-kiN3 chit ho7 oe7, mui2 pai2 chhut-lai5 e5 si5-chun7, na7 khoaN3-kiN3 Liam5 Pho2, chiu7 koaN2-kin2 siam2  tui3 piN-a2 khi3.  I sou2 eng7 e5 lang5 khoaN3-kiN3 in chu2-lang5 chit ho7 khoan2, chiu7 liah8-choe3 toa7-toa7 e5 kian3-siau3; tai7-ke lai5 tui3 Siong-ju5 saN-si5, beh khi3  pat8 ui7.  Siong-ju5 chiah ka7 in kong2, Hian7-si5 te7-it kiong5 te7-it toa7 e5 chiu7 si7 Chin5-kok.  Chong2-si7 goa2 ti7 i tian7-teng2, siong7-chhiaN2 kaN2 toa7 siaN hoah lai5 chek-pi7 i Chin5 ong5, ho5-hong3 Liam5 Chiong-kun, goa2 kiam2 chin-chiaN3 si7 teh kiaN mah?  Put-ko3 chit-tiap8 Chin5-kok m7 kaN2 lai5 phah Tio7-kok, chiu7-si7 in-ui7 u7 goan2 nng7 lang5, na7 kau-chiap ong2-lai5 e5 su7, goa2 oe7 siat-hoat,  m7-ku2 cheng-chian3 e5 tai7-chi3, iu5-goan5 tioh8 kho3 Liam5 Chiong-kun.  Siat- su2 goan2 nng7 e5 put-ho5, si7 chhin-chhiuN7 nng7 chiah hou2 teh saN-chiN, hit e5 se3-bin7 oh-tit long2 oah8; sou2-i2 goa2 na7  
kiN3-tioh8 i, chiu7 tai7-seng siam2-pi7.  In-ui7 goa2  si7 liah8 kok-ka e5 tai7-chi3 choe3 khah iau3-kin2, i tui3 goa2 sng3 si7 ko3-jin5 e5  hiap8-hiam5 na7-tiaN7, sou2-i2 bo5 beh kap i ke3-kau3 lah.  I sou2 eng7 e5 lang5, thiaN-liau2 put-chi2 u7 cheng5-li2, ia7 chiu7 oh8 in chu2-lang5 e5 khoan2,  tu2-tioh8 Liam5 Pho2 e5 kun-lang5, ia7 long2 khah niu7 i.  Liam5 Pho2 hit peng5  e5 lang5, chiu7 na2 kiau-ngou7 khi2 lai5, liah8 choe3 Siong-ju5 chin-chiaN3 kiaN i.   Au7-lai5 u7 chit8 lang5 mia5 kio3 Gu5 Kheng, lai5 chhe7 Liam5 Pho2, chiong Lin7 Siong-ju5 e5 i3-su3 thiah beng5 hou7 i thiaN.  Liam5 Pho2 chiah chhiN2-gou7 hoan2-hoe2, chiu7 thng3-pak-theh pe7 chit8 ki tek-poe, lai5 Siong-ju5 in tau jin7 choe7, chhiaN2 Siong-ju5 eng7 tek-poe chek-hoat8 i.  Siong-ju5 chin hoaN-hi2 khan i e5 chhiu2, chhiaN2 i jip8-khi3 lai7-bin7, ho2 le2 khoan2-thai7 i; nng7 lang5 soa3 kiat choe3 siN-si2 e5 kau-poe5.   
Lun7-kau3 put-ho5 e5 tai7-chi3, m7 na7 kok-nih8 u7 an2-ni, ke-lai7 ia7 si7 u7 an2-ni.  Chiu7-si7 Ia5-sou e5 kau3-hoe7, ia7 boe7 kong2 tit chiu7 bo5 an2-ni.  Bat khoaN3-kiN3 u7 si5 chit peng5 e5 kau3-hoe7 khoaN3-khin hit peng5 e5 kau3- hoe7, a2 si7 hit peng5 e5 hoe7-iu2 khoaN3-khin chit peng5 e5 hoe7-iu2.  U7 si5 kong2 bou2 lang5 si7 kiu5 piaN2 tit-tioh8 piaN2, a2 si7 kong2 bou2 lang5 si7 oa2-kho3 se3-lek8, ia7 bat kong2 bou2- mih8 lang5 to bo5 hak8-bun7, hoan2-tng2 teh choe3 chip- su7, a2 si7 kong2 bou2 mih8 lang5 to bo5 jiat8-sim, chaiN2-iuN7 teh choe3 thoan5-to7.  An2-ni tai7-ke phoe-pheng5; kong2-liau2 to long2 u7 in e5 li2-khi3.  Su7-put-ti Mou5-kui2 i2-keng than3 chit e5 ki-hoe7, hou7 li2 li7-khui cheng3-keng e5 lou7, lai5 jip8 ti7 i e5 khoau5-tho3 lah.  Ia7 chiu7-si7 se3- siok8 lang5, in-ui7 khoaN3-kiN3 lan2 e5 hoe7-iu2 ka-ki7 put- bok8, bo5 saN-thiaN3 e5 sim, oe7 soa3 kiaN kau3 m7 kaN2 lai5; an2-ni kau3-hoe7 thai3 oe7 heng-ong7 nih?  Sou2-i2 chhim- chhim ng3-bang7 kau3-hoe7 lai7 e5 peng5-iu2, na7 u7 chit ho7, chiu7 koaN2-kin2 koe2; na7 bo5, ia7 tioh8 kin2-sin7 m7 thang hoan7-tioh8, boh8-tit u7 phang7 thang hou7 Mou5-kui2 jip8- khi3.     
Iah8 koh chit8 hang7, Siong-ju5 kap Liam5 Pho2 sng3- si7 siang7 chit8 tian7 e5 jin5-sin5, Liam5 Pho2 e5 sim u7 hou7 hit e5 kong-beng5 mia5-siaN be5-khi3, chiu7 kap Siong-ju5 m7-ho2.  Siong-ju5 ia7 khoan-iong5 i, kau3 i chai thang hoan2-hoe2 jin7-choe7, chiu7 hoaN-hi2 koh chiap-lap8 i, kap i kau-poe5; che sng3-si7 chit8 lang5 tui3 chit8 lang5, peng5- iu2 ong2-lai5 e5 su7 na7-tiaN7.  Iau2 u7 chit8 hang7 khah toa7 iau3-kin2, chiu7-si7 se3-kan lang5 kiaN5 m7 tioh8 lou7, poe7-biu7 to7-li2, Siong7-te3 ia7 chhut-chai7 in khi3 choe3, kau3 i chai  
thang hoan2-hoe2 jin7-choe7, chiu7 beh koh chiap-lap8 i choe3 kiaN2; chit ho7 sng3-si7 siN lan2 e5 leng5-hun5, pe7-kiaN2 e5 chi3-chhin, chu7-jian5 koh khah iau3-kin2.  I u7 chhe- khian2 Kiu3-chu2 Ia5-sou loh8-lai5 se3-kan, hou7 lang5 sin3 lai5 tit-tioh8 koh kap Siong7-te3 chhin-kun7.  Ia2-sou lai5 se3- kan thoan5 Siong7-te3 kok e5 hok-im, hou7 lang5 chhiN2-gou7 chai choe7, si7 chhin-chhiuN7 Gu5 Kheng thiah-beng5 Siong-ju5 e5 i3-su3.  TaN lan2 long2 tioh8 oh8 Liam5 Pho2, chai thang chhiN2-gou7 jin7-choe7, bian2-tit au7-lai5 beh hoan2-hoe2 e5 si5, chiah chai i2-keng ti5 lah.  
Gau5 ti7-li2 peh-siN3
Ku3 Pek-giok8 choe3 Oe7-kok e5 chaiN2-siong3, hit si5 kok-lai7 toa7 peng5-tiaN7.  Chu2-kong3 khi3 mng7 i kong2, M7 chai lin2 kok-lai7 eng7 sim2-mih8 hoat-tou7 teh ti7-li2.  Ku3 Pek-giok8 kong2, Goa2 si7 eng7 m7 bian2 ti7-li2 e5 hoat-tou7 lai5 teh ti7 kok.  Tng hit-si5 Chin3-kok Tio7 Kan2-chu2 siuN7 beh khi3  kong-phah Oe7-kok, tai7-seng chhe Su2 Am2 khi3 Oe7-kok tham3-thiaN cheng5-heng5.  Su2 Am2 to3-lai5 he5-hok kong2, Ku3 Pek-giok8 teh choe3  chaiN2-siong3, m7 thang khi3 kong phah i.    
Beng7-chu2 u7 kong2, Teh siu2 kok, m7 si7 kho3 soaN- khiN e5 gui5-hiam2 choe3 kian-kou3 lah.  Koan2 peh-siN3 boe7 oe7 liah8 siu7 hong e5 toe7-hng choe3 che3-han7 tit. Sou2-i2 Ko Iau5 sui-jian5 si7 toa7-chih8 koh teng5-ku3, i ti7 Sun3-te3 hit si5 teh choe3 koan2 hoat-lut8 e5 koaN, liau7-li2 peh-siN3 heng5-hoat8 e5 su7, long2 bo5 chit2 tiam2-a2 oan- ong2; khiok pi2 hit ho7 u7 khau2-chai5 gau5 kong2 oe7 e5 khah ho2.  Su Khong3 sui-jian5 si7 chhiN-mi5 e5 lang5, i choe3 Chin3-kok Thai3-chaiN2 e5 si5-chun7, kok-lai7 e5 cheng3-su7 long2 bo5 chit8-tiam2-a2 hun7-chap8; khiok pi2 hit ho7 u7 bak8-chiu thang khoaN3 khah ho2.  An2-ni kho2-kian3 bo5 lun7 sim2-mih8 tai7-chi3, long2 tioh8 kiu5 hit e5 sit8-chai7, m7-thang chng-thaN7 hit e5 goa7-phe5, si7 khah iau3-kin2.      
Koh che ia7 kap Lo5-ma2 jin5-su te7 6, te7 7 chiuN sou2 ki3-chai3 chiaN5-seng3 e5 to7-li2 chha-put-to saN-tang5.  In- ui7 Kiu3-chu2 kio3 I e5 peh-siN3 lai5 kiaN5 ho2, m7 si7 eng7 lut8- hoat giam5-giam5 iok-sok in, chiu7-si7 eng7 I e5 Seng3-sin5 kam2-hoa3 in e5 sim, hou7 in chu7-jian5 kiaN5 ho2 su7.   
 
Su7 hong5 kah si5
Lou2-kok u7 chit8 e5 siN3 Si e5 lang5, siN nng7 e5 kiaN2, chit8-e5 ai3 oh8 bun5 e5, chit8-e5 ai3 oh8 bu2 e5.  Hit e5 ai3 oh2 bun5 e5 khi3 Che5 kok, beh ba7 khoaN3 u7 koaN thang choe3 bo5.  Che5 hou5 khoaN3 i e5 hak8-bun7 chin ho2, chiu7 chhiaN2 i choe3 in hiah e5 kong-chu2 e5 sian-siN.  Hit e5 ai3 oh8 bu2 e5 khi3 Chhou2 kok kiN3 Chhou2 ong5. Chhou2 ong5 ia7 chin hoaN-hi2, ku2-khi2 i choe3 kun-cheng3-si.  An2-ni nng7 e5 hiaN-ti7-a2, chit bun5 chit8 bu2, long2 teh choe3 toa7 koaN, sng3 si7 hian2-chou2 eng5-chong, ka-teng5 chin u7 kong-chhai2 e5 su7.  Lang5-lang5 put-chi2 him- soan7 in.  Ia7 chin chhau3-khiau2, in hit chhu3-piN u7 chit8 e5 siN3 Beng7 e5, iu5-goan5 nng7 e5 kiaN2, sou2 hak8-sip8 e5 ia7 siang7 chit8 iuN7. Chong2-si7 long2 iau2 teh lok8-phek, kan-khou2 kau3 boe7 kham tit.  In-ui7 an2-ni, chiu7 lai5 mng7-khi2, khoaN3 in an3-chaiN2-iuN7 oe7 kau3 chiah hian2-tat8; siN3 Si e5 eng7 sit8-chai7 ka7 in kong2.  Hit e5 siN3 Beng7 e5 chiu7 kah hit e5 oh8 bun5 e5 toa7 kiaN2 khi3 Chin5 kok,  beh ba7 khoaN3 u7 koaN thang choe3 bo5.  Chin5 ong5 thiaN i hiah e5 to7-tek e5 oe7 chiu7 kong2, Hian7-chai7 si7 thiN-kha-e7 toa7  jiau2-loan7 e5 si5, long2 tioh8 oa2-kho3 peng e5 khui3-lat8 choe3 iau3-kin2; na7 eng7  jin5-gi7 lai5 liau7-li2 kok, si7 beh hai7 goa2 e5 kok hou7 biat8 bo5.  Chiu7 chiong in  hit e5 toa7 kiaN2 eng7 kek8 kan-khou2 e5 heng5-hoat8, hou7 i piN3-chiaN5 hoe3-jin5,  chiah pang3 i khi3.  Ia7 hit e5 soe3-han3 e5 khi3 Oe7 kok, tui3 Oe7 hou5 kong2-khi2 tioh8 chaiN2-iuN7 lai5 kang2-sip8 bu2 e5 su7.  Oe7 hou5  kong2, Hian7-si5 goa2 e5 kok sng3 si7 put-chi2 loan2-jiok8, koh kap chiah e5 toa7 kok sio keh-kai3.  Sou2-i2 na7 tui3 toa7 kok, eng-kai tioh8 sio2-sim kin2- sin7 lai5 hok8-sai7 i; na7 tui3 sio2 kok, ia7 chi3 ho2 si7 eng7 an-bu2 e5 hoat-tou7; an2-ni chiah sng3 si7 kiu5 kok-lai7 peng5-an e5 hong-hoat.  Siat- su2 eng7 peng-koan5, chiu7-si7 teh chhe7 biat8- bo5 e5 lou7.  Na7 pang3 chit e5 lang5 oan5-choan5 to3-khi3, chiong-lai5 tek-khak oe7 hai7 goa2 e5 kok.  Chiu7 chiong kha ka7 i cham7-khi2-lai5, chiah pang3 i to3-khi3 Lou2 kok.  Hit e5 siN3 Beng7 e5 khoaN3-kiN3 nng7 e5 kiaN8 m7-na7 bo5 koaN thang choe3, hoan2-tng2 long2 piN3 hoe3-jin5, chiu7 khi3 kau3 beh si2, soa3 khi3 siN3 Si e5 in lai7-bin7 ka7 i chhau2-nau7.   Hit e5 siN3  
Si e5 chiu7 kong2, Hoan7-su7 na7 tu2-tioh8 si5-ki chiu7 heng-ong7,  sit-loh8 si5-ki chiu7 choe3 pai7-hoai7. Lin2 e5 hak8-bun7 kap goan2 siang7 chit8 iuN7,  m7-ku2 hit e5 si5-ki si7 bo5 saN-tang5.     
Chiau3 an2-ni khoaN3, thiN-kha-e7 e5 li2-khi3, boe7 oe7 kong2-tit siong5-siong5 si7 tioh8, tai7-chi3 ia7 boe7 oe7 kong2 tit chhiang5-chai7 m7-tioh8 tit.  U7 e5 chit khoan2 e5 tai7- chi3, chai7-cha2 sng3 choe3 u7 li2-khi3, choe3-liau2 si7 tioh8; kau3 hian7-chai7 khiok boe7 oe7 sng3-tit u7 li2-khi3.  U7 e5 chit hang7 mih8 hian7-chai7 si7 bo5 lou7-eng7, kau3 au7-lai5 m7-ku2 piN3 choe3 chin u7 lou7-eng7.  Sou2-i2 u7 li2-khi3, a2 si7 bo5 li2-khi3, u7 lou7-eng7 a2 si7 bo5 lou7-eng7, khiok boe7 oe7 it-teng7 lai5 siu2 tit,long2 tioh8 khoaN3 si7 sim2-mih8 si5-chun7.  Tai7- pit8, Sou2-lo5-bun5, Giau5, Sun3, in e5 chun-kui3 choe3 jin5- kun, ia7 boe7 kong2 tit in u7 siuN ke3-thau5. Liap8-sat-lou7, Gan5 Hoe5, in song3-hiong kau3 choe3 khit-chiah8, khia7- khi2 hit phian-phiah oeh8-toeh8 e5 hang7-a2-lai7, ia7 si7 boe7 eng7 tit kong2 in si7 thai3 pi-chian7.  In-ui7 kok lang5 e5 sou2 choe3, Siong7-te3 long2 u7 tiaN7-tioh8 e5 si5 hou7 in, m7 si7 lang5 sou2 oe7 bian2-kiong2 tit.  Beng7-chu2 u7 kong2, Su2 seng iu2 beng7, hu3-kui3 chai7 thian.  Sou2-i2 lang5 long2 tioh8 siu2 pun2-hun7, jin7 mia7, theng3-hau7 si5, chhut-chai7 thiN chu2-i3, m7 thang kiong5-kiong5 choe3.  Siok8-gu2 u7 kong2, Su7 hong5 kah si5; siat-su2 tai7-chi3 bo5 tu2-tioh8 hah8 hit e5 si5, sui-jian5 khah gau5 ke3-bou5, choe3 kau3  chin chiu-chi3, ia7 bo5 tek-khak oe7 tit thang seng5-kong.  
To gi5 oe7 hai7 su7
Hoai5-lam5 chu2 e5 chheh kong2, U7 chit8 e5 cha-bou2 gin2-na2 beh chhut ke3 e5 si5, in chhu3-piN e5 lang5 ka7 i e5 pe7-bu2 kong2, Lin2 cha-bou2-kiaN2 ke3-khi3 lang5 tau, au7-lai5 oe7 siN kiaN2 a2 boe7, si7 boe7 liau7 tit; na7 boe7 siN, kiam2 m7 si7 hoan7-tioh8 chhit- chhut e5 tiau5-le7 mah?  Leng5-khou2 tioh8 chiau3-kou3 li2 e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2, kah i na7 u7 li7-pian7 e5 si5, tioh8 chiong in ang hit thau5 e5 saN-a2-khou3 kap chap8-chhui3 e5 mih8, thau- theh8 koa2 to3-lai5 lin2 chhu3; ban7-it au7-lai5 bo5 ka7 lang5 siN kiaN2, hou7 lang5 li5 to3-lai5, ia7 chiah u7 thang tou7 oah3.  In e5 pe7-bu2 liah8 choe3 an2-ni si7 chin tioh8, chiu7 kap in cha-bou2-kiaN2 tau3, chiong in ang hit peng5 e5 mih8-kiaN7, thau- theh8 to3-lai5 in tau.  Ke3 u7 hiah ku2, in e5 ta-ke-koaN chai kio3 i e5 sim-pu7 tiaN7-tiaN7 thau-theh8 mih8 khi3 in goa7-ke chhu3,  
chiu7 kong2, Goan2 chit e5 sim-pu7, sim-koaN i2-keng ng3 ti7 goa7-bin7, si7 boe7  eng7-tit koh lau5 i toa3 teh, put-ju5 liong7-cha2 hou7 i khi3; chiu7 ka7 i li5 to3-khi3 in goa7-ke hia.  In e5 pe7-bu2 m7 chai hit e5 hou7 lang5 li5 e5 ian5-kou3,  hoan2-tng2 chin kam2-kek chhu3-piN hit e5 lang5, kong2 i ka3-si7 in, hou7 in chai thang than3 cha2 pi7-pan7.   
Na7 lun7 pun2-to2 kap Tiong-kok e5 lang5, ia7 choe7-choe7 u7 chit ho7 mau5- peng7, mui2 siong5 choe3 chit8 hang tai7-chi3, chiu7 giau5-gi5 kiaN-liau2 boe7  chiaN5; chiu7-si7 i2-keng choe3 chiaN5, ia7 giau5-gi5 kiaN-liau2 tu3 bo5 ku2.  Ti3- kau3 u7 hit ho7 eng-kai tioh8 chin7-lat8 e5, m7 kheng2 khi3 chin7 lat8, eng-kai  tioh8 pan7 e5 su7, ia7 m7 kheng2 khi3 pan7; kan-ta kiaN oe7 peh8 liau2 kang, a2 si7  oe7 liau2 pun2, an2-ni long2 m7 kheng2 khi3 choe3.  Koh u7 chit8 khoan2,  hit ho7 tai7-chi3 taN-chiah chhong3 lip8, ia7 m7 kheng2 he7 pun2 chhut-lat8 loh8 khi3 choe3, hoan2-tng2 si3-koe3 khau- khek; na7 u7 thang than3 tam7-poh8 jip8 chhiu2, ka-ki7 chiu7 liah8 choe3 kau3-giah8; iah8 hit ho7 tai7-chi3 e5 seng5- kong a2 si7 pai7-hoai7, long2 bo5 beh khi3 koan2.  Put-lun7 chhong3 sim2-mih8 tai7-chi3, tai7-khai3 si7 u7 thau5 bo5 be2, poan3 tou5 ji5 hoe3 e5 khah choe7; bo5 u7 hit ho7 kian-kou3 koat-toan3 e5 sim; sou2-i2 choe3 long2 boe7 oe7 seng5-kong. 
Hit khoan2 e5 lang5, m7 na7 choe3 tai7-chi3 si7 an2-ni, chiu7-si7 than3 to7-li2 hok8-sai7 Siong7-te3, ia7 bo5 m7 si7 an2- ni.  Phi3-lun7 chhin-chhiuN7 chit e5 lang5, peng5-sou3 chin ai3 kong2 peh8-chhat8 lai5 phian3 lang5, au7-lai5 in-ui7 chai choe3 tai7-chi3 na7 u7 hah8 ti7 Siong7-te3 e5 chi2-i3, Siong7-te3 chu7- jian5 siuN2-su3 hok-khi3 hou7 i, iu7 koh lam7-sam2 kong2 peh8-chhat8, si7 hoan7-tioh8 Siong7-te3 kap lang5 long2 siu7- khi3 e5 choe7.  An2-ni chiu7 lai5 chun-than3 Siong7-te3 e5 chi2-i3, ng3-bang7 Siong7-te3 siuN2-su3 hok-khi3 hou7 in.  M7- ku2 ke3 be7 joa7 ku2, hut-jian5 iu7 giau5-gi5 Siong7-te3 siuN2-su3 e5 hok-khi3, si7 bong5-bong5 biau2-biau2, boe7 pin5-chun2 tit, m7 thang choan-choan oa2-kho3 chit hang7; put- ju5 it-bian7 eng7 tam7-poh8 peh8-chhat8 oe7 lai5 phian3 lang5, ia7 it-bian7 lai5 chun-than3 to7-li2, kiam2 m7 si7 nng7 thau5 long2 u7 thang oa2-kho3 mah?  Kho2-sioh chhin-chhiuN7 chit khoan2 e5 lang5, it-seng long2 boe7 oe7 tit-tioh8 hok- khi3 e5 po3-siuN2, hoan2-tng2 kong2 chin Sin5 bo5 u7 leng5- siaN3.  Kiam2 chin-chiaN3 chin Sin5 bo5 u7 leng5-siaN3 mah? Siok8-gu2 kong2, Gi5 su7 bu5 kong; na7 si7 giau5-gi5 e5 tai7- chi3, choe3 liau2 boe7 seng5-kong, chiu7-si7 chit e5 i3-su3.    
 
Kin phang bo ho se
Beng-chu u kong, Song kok u7 chit8 e5 lang5, hoan5-lo2 i chhan5-nih e5  tiu7-a2 long2 bo5 sim2-mih8 toa7, i chiu7 chit8 bou5 chit8 bou5, eng7 chhiu2 ka7 i puih8, hou7 phu5 khah koaiN5-khi2-lai5; tit8-tit8 chau2 to3-lai5 in tau ka7 lang5 kong2, Kin-a2-jit8 goa2 khoaN3-kiN3 chhan5-nih e5 tiu7-a2 long2 m7 toa7, put-chi2 hoan5-lo2;  goa2 khiok u7 siuN7-tioh8 chit8 e5 hoat-tou7, thang pang-chan7 i toa7 chang5.  In hau7-siN thiaN-kiN3 an2-ni, chiu7 koaN2-kin2 chau2 khi3 khoaN3; o2-ho3, hiah e5  hou7 i puih8 e5 tiu7-a2, to long2 ta-ta-khi3 lah.  
Lun7-gu2 chheh u7 kong2, Ai3 koaN2-kin2 chiu7 choe3 boe7 tit thang kau3.  Ia7 Tiong7-iong5 e5 u7 kong2, Phi3- ju7 chiuN7 koaiN5, tioh8 tui3 ke7-ke7 lai5 peh; phi3-ju7 kiaN5 hng7, tioh8 tui3 kun7 lai5 kiaN5 khi2.  An2-ni thang chai bo5 lun7 choe3 sim2-mih8 su7, long2 tioh8 chiau3 chhu3-su7 lai5 kiaN5, chiah oe7 tit choe3 kau3 seng5-kong.  Na7 si7 chhut-chai7 in ka-ki7 e5 kin2 seng3-te7, boe7 oe7 kiaN5 i chiu7 beh oh8 phau2, an2-ni beh thai3 oe7 po2 tit i boe7 poah8- to2 leh?  Chhin-chhiuN7 Ma2-kho2 si3 chiuN7 ji7 chap8 lak8 chat u7 kong2, Siong7-te3  e5 kok chhin-chhiuN7 lang5 ia7 cheng2-chi2 ti7 toe7-nih2, mi5-si5 khun3, cha2-khi2 si5 khi2-lai5, hit e5 cheng2-chi2 chiu7 hoat-ge5, chiam7-chiam7 toa7-khi2- lai5, lang5 ia7 boe7 hiau2-tit an2-choaN2-iuN7 oe7 an2-ni.  In-ui7 toe7 teh siN gou7-kak, si7 chhut ti7 chu7-jian5 e5, tai7-seng si7 ng, au7-lai5 toa7 chang5 chiaN5 sui7, kau3 be2 sui7-nih8 chiu7 kiat kui liap8, ia7 hiah e5 liap8 seng5-sek8 liau2, chiu7 eng7 liam5-lek8-a2 khi3 koah, in-ui7 siu-seng5 e5 si5-chun7 kau3 lah.  Chiau3 an2-ni chiah u7 chhut ti7 chu7-jian5; na7 chhin-chhiuN7 hit e5 Song3 kok e5 lang5 sou2 teh choe3, m7-na7 boe7 pang-chan7 i toa7, si7 tian-to3 hou7 i khau si2 liau2-liau2.  Sou2-i2 siok8-gu2 koh teh kong2, Kin2 phang2 bo5 ho2 se, kin2 choe3 bo5 ho2 ta-ke; chiu7 si7 kah lang5 tioh8 chiau3 chhu3-su7 lai5 kiaN5.         
Cheng2 ti2 oa
Chong-chu2 bat kong2, U7 chit8 jit8 chiN2-lai7 e5 sui2-koe tui3 Tang-hai2 e5 pih kong2, Goa2 put-chi2 ai3 kap li2 saN-kap thit-tho5, khoaN3 si7 beh toa3 chiN2-noa5-teng2, thiau3-lai5 thiau3- khi3, a2-si7 beh toa3 chiN2-lai7 e5 piah-khang, hioh-khun3 lai5 tam5-lun7;  hek8-si7 toa3 chui2-bin7 pang3 teh hou7 i phu5, a2-si7 tiam3-bi7 chhang3-loh8 lai5 thou5-soa toe2, long2  
chin ho2 thit-tho5; bo5 lun7 si7 am7-mui5,  a2-si7 tou7-un2, to m7 tat8-tioh8 goa2.  TaN tit-tioh8 chit khut e5 chui2, koh u7 chiah-nih8 toa7, chiah-nih8 khoah e5 chiN2, ia7 sng3 si7 kek8 lok8  e5 se3-kai3 lah.  Pih Sian-siN, li2 chaiN2-iuN7 m7 khah siong5 lai5 goan2 chit ho7  ho2 sou2-chai7 thit-tho5 leh?  Tang-hai2 e5 pih chiu7 siuN7 beh loh8-khi3, to3- kha chhng  iau2-be7 jip8-khi3, chiaN3-kha to i2-keng khi3 khe5-teh lah, chiu7  toa3 chiN2-teng2 seh8 kui2-na7 choa7; soa3 tui3 hit chiah sui2-koe kong2, Li2 boe7  hiau2-tit tang-hai2 e5 toa7 mah?  Kang2 chheng li2 e5 hng7, iau2-be7 kau3-giah8  thang pi2 i e5 khoah; kang2 chheng tng7 e5 koaiN5, iau2-be7 kau3-giah8 thang  pi2-tit i e5 chhim.  U2-te3 e5 si5, kau2 ni5 e5 chui2-chai, chit e5 hai2 bo5 khoaN3-kiN3 ke- thiN khah koaiN5.  Thong-ong5 hit-tiap8, chhit ni5 e5 khong3-han7, chit e5 hai2  ia7 bo5 khoaN3-kiN3 kiam2-chio2 khah ke7; bo5 kong2 in-ui7 ku2 chiam7-si5 pian3-keng, a-si7 u7 choe7 chio2 e5 chin3-the3.  Che si7 goan2 tang-hai2 kek8 lok8 e5 sou2-chai7.  Hit chiah chiN2-lai7 e5 sui2-koe thiaN-kiN3 chiah e5 oe7, tai7-seng chhiN-chin koh gong5-ngiah8; au7-lai5 siuN7 liau8 kian3-siau3, tiam7-tiam7 long2 bo5 i3-su3.     
Lun7-kau3 se3-kan lang5, chi2-u7 chai eng5-hoa5 hu3-kui3, ai3 choe3 toa7-koaN, than3 toa7 chiN5, hak ho2 e5 chhan5, chhoa7 sui2 e5 bou2,  u7 choe7-choe7 kim-gun5 chai5-po2, an2-ni chiu liah8-choe3 chun-kui3; ia7 m7  chai ehiah e5 i2-goa7, iau2 u7 pi2 chit ho7 khah chun-kui3 e5 tai7-chi3. Chhin-chhiuN7 Po2-lo5 m7 goan7 choe3 Iu5-thai3 lang5 e5 koaN, lai5 kun-te3 Ia5-sou.  Mou5-se m7 kheng2 hiong2-siu7 Ai-kip8 ong5-kiong e5 hok-khi3, kam-goan7 kap I-sek- liat8 lang5 phun-pho ti khong3-ia2.  Gan5 Hoe5 khia7 toa3 hit ho7 m7 chiaN5 sou2-chai7, si7 tng3 teh chiah8 chit8 kheng-a2 png7, chit8 khok-a2 thng; chong2-si7 i liah2- choe3 chin khoai3-lok8.  Liap8-sat-lou7 song3-hiong kau3 bo5 thang chiah8, tiam3 ho2-giah8 lang5 e5 mng5-khau2, theng3-hau7 pun tam7-poh8 e5 lau5-san mih8 lai5 chi2-ki, i ia7 long2 bo5 hoan5-lo2.  Chhin-chhiuN7 chit kui2 lang5, kiam2 m7-si7 kap lan2  siang7 chit8 khoan2 e5 seng-khu, saN tang5 chit8 khoan2 e5 seng3-cheng5; chaiN2- iuN7 m7 chai chiah8 ho2 chheng7 ho2 si7 lang5 sou2 him-sian7 mah? ChaiN2-iuN7 i thian-thian-a2 m7, hoan2-tng2 si5 ho2 giah8, kam-goan7 hou7 song3-hiong; bo5 him sian7 chun-kui3, kam-sim choe3 pi-chian7, bo5 hiam5 kan-khou2, put-lun7 tu2-tioh8 sim2-mih8 chhi3-lian7, ia7 bo5 koe2-oaN7 in e5 sim- chi3?  Che kiam2 m7 si7 piau2-beng5 in sim-lai7 kap bak8- chiu e5 tiong-kan, leng7-goa7 u7 chit8 khoan2 e5 keng2-gu7, khah-iaN5 ti7 se3-kan e5 eng5-hoa5 hu3-kui3, kap hiah e5 chun-kui3 ho2-giah8 kim-gun5 chai5-po2 mah?  Iah8 hiah e5 mi5-jit8 tu-tu siuN7 chit ho7 e5 lang5 kap chit e5 cheng2- ti2-oa, u7 sim2-mih8 hun-piat leh? 
 
Koh chit8 hang7, lan2 chia e5 lang5 khah choe7 long m7 bat chhut-goa7, hou7  i kek8 kiaN5 si7 ti7 in pun2 hiuN-sia7, a2-si7 kun7-hu7 e5 pou-thau5, in chiu7 phin2  kau3 i khi3 sim2-mih8 sou2-chai7 thit-tho5, joa7 ho2 kong-keng2; in iah8 m7 chai pat8-ui7 e5 siaN5-chhi7 u7 joa7 toa7, lang5 u7 joa7 choe7. Na7 thiaN-kiN3 chit8 hang7 khah ki5-koai3 e5 su7, in chiu7 liah8-choe3 si7 kong2 peh8-chhat8 teh phian3 i.  Ia7 na7 hit ho7 m7 eng-kai sin3, bo5-iaN2 bo5 chiah,  liap chit8 e5 kui2-sin5 e5 mia5 lai5 phian3 lang5, in chiu7 sin3 tauh-tauh, na7 pat8 lang5 m7 sin3, in chiu7 ke-thiN kui2-ku3 lai5 kan-cheng3 kau3 khia7-chin kiha7-hian7, che long2 si7 tui3 ti7 bo5 iat-lek8 e5 sou2-ti3.  Koh  m7-na7 chit8-poaN3-lang5 si7 an2-ni, kui kok e5 lang5 ia7 u7 chit ho7 mau5-peng7.  Chhin-chhiuN7 Tiong-kok ti7 kui2-chap8 ni5 cheng5, boe7 kap goa7-kok kau-thong ong2-lai5 boe2-boe7 e5 si5, ka-ki7 liah8 choe3 pun2- kok si7 chin toa7, koh chin gau5, khoaN3 goa7-kok long2 bo5 chiuN7 bak8, kong2 in si7 hoan-a2 sou2-chai7, bo5 siuN7- tioh8 Seng3-jin5 e5 ka3-si7, tek-khak si7 bo5 sim2-mih8 kho2- chhu2; an2-ni ka-ki7 khoa-khau2 chu7-toa7.  Su7-put-ti goa7-kok hiah-nih8 bun5-beng2, kho-hak8 ia7 chin hoat- tat8, bo5 lun7 thian-bun5 te7-li2, lai5-be7-lai5 khi3-be7-khi3 e5 su7, long2 u7 gian2-kiu3 khah chiau5-kau3.  Kun7-lai5 khah u7 lang5 kap kok kok teh lai5 ong2, chiah chai kau3 goa7-kok e5 bun5-beng5  tak8 hang7 hiah nih8 chiau5-pi7, m7-ku2 che sng3 si7 u7 ke3-khi3 goa7-kok iu5-lek8,  a2-si7 pun2-sin bat keng-ke3 e5, chiah oe7 chai kau3 an2-ni.  Ia7 na7 hit ho7 siu2-kiu7-phai3 m7 ai3 kong2 i5-sin e5 oe7 hit ho7 lang5, na7 thiaN-kiN3 khah sin-ki5 e5 oe7, ia7 bo5 koh-iuN hit ho7 cheng2-ti2-oa teh thiaN Tang-hai2 toa7-pih e5 oe7 lah.     
Chin7 choe3 lang5 e5 pun2-hun7
Cho2-toan7 e5 chheh u7 kong2, Teng7-kok e5 tai7-hu koaN, Pi5 Cho3, ka7 in  kok-nih8 e5 chaiN2-siong3 Chu2-san2 kong2, Goa2 khoaN3 koh bo5 joa7-ku2 Teng7- kok oe7 u7 he2-chai; chhiaN2 li2 tioh8 choe3 chio3 lai5 ki5-to2, ng3-bang7 khoaN3 oe7 bian2- tit u7 chit e5 chai-e7.  Chu2-san2 m7 thiaN Keh bo5 kui2-jit8, ko2-jian5 u7 toa7 he2-chai.  Pi5 Cho3 koh ka7 i kong2, Na7 m7 thiaN goa2 e5 chhui3, m7-bian2 joa7-ku2, iau2-ku2 u7 he2-chai.  Chu2-san2 in3 i kong2, ThiN e5 choe3 tai7, hou7 lang5 thai3 oe7 hiau2-tit?   Au7-lai7 e5 su7, lang5 nia2 oe7 chai?  Put-ko3 tioh8 chin7 lang5 e5 pun2-hun7 lai5  choe3, khah iau3-kin2.  Au7-lai5 Teng7-kok kau3 be2 to ia7 peng5-an bo5 tai7-chi3;  ia7 bo5 koh u7 he2-chai.  
 
Tai5-oan5 kap Tiong-kok eng2 u7 chit8 khoan2 hit ho7 lang5, choan-bun5 kong2 ke2 sian-ti e5 oe7, u7-si5 kong2, Koh joa7-ku2 oe7 u7 he2-chai, a2 si7 chui2-chai; u7-si5 kong2, Bou2-mih8 si5 oe7 oe7 tu2-tioh8 un-ek8 e5 kan-khou2; long tioh8 than3 cha2 chhiaN2 koa2 he5-siuN7 a2-si7 to7-su7, lai5 choe3 chio3, thang  kai2 tu5 chit khoan2 e5 chai-e7.  An2-ni sit8-chai7 kan-ta lam7-sam2 liau2 chiN5  na7-tiaN7, long2 bo5 chit8-tiam2-a2 u7 lou7-eng7.  Iah8-keng e5 chheh kong2, Chek- chu7 ho2 e5 ke-lai7, in e5 hok-khi3 tek-khak u7 chhun; chek-chu7 phaiN2 e5 ke-lai7, in e5 chai-e7 tek-kak chhiong-chiok.  Su-keng-nih8 ia7 kong2, Choe3 ho2 e5 chiu7 eng7 pah hang7 hok-khi3 siuN2-su3 i; choe3  m7 ho2 e5  chiu7 chiong pah-hang7 chai-e7 kang3 hou7 i.  An2-ni-siN khoaN3, lang5 tioh8 chiau3 to7-li2 lai5 kiaN5, oh8 choe3 ho2 lang5, chiu7 thang siam2-pi7 tak8 iuN7 e5 chai-lan7.  Ho5-hong3 chui2, he2, un-ek8, chit ho7 chai-e7, si7 tui3 lang5 m7 sio2-sim lai5 tu2-tioh8.  Siat-su2 oe7 chiong khiN-kau khui hou7 thau3, hoaN7-chah8 khi2 hou7 kian-kou3, beh thai3 oe7 u7 chui2-chai leh?   Iah8 na7 cha2-am3 he2-chek oe7 hiau2 soe3-ji7, tak8 pai2 tai7-seng ti5-hong5, beh thai3  oe7 u7 he2-chai leh?  Koh lim-chiah8 na7 oe7 hiau2-tit tioh8  chheng-khi3, khia7- khi2 e5 sou2-chai7 kap sin-chheng7 oe7 kin2-sin7, iah8 beh thai3 oe7 u7 un-ek8 leh?  M7-ku2 lang5 long2 m7 tui3 hit e5 sit8-chai7 e5 su7 lai5 kang2-kiu3, kan-ta sin3 hit ho7 he5-siuN7  to7-su7 e5 liam7-keng pai3-chham3, choe3-chio3 sio-hiuN, chhong3-long3 hiah e5 bo5 li7-ek e5 su7; ho5 e5 lou7 chhut-chai7 i that-teh, bo5 beh khui; hou7-hoaN7 ku3-chai7 i to2-hoai7, bo5 beh siu-li2; koe-lou7 oeh8 chiN-chiN, chhu3-theh8 chat8 thong2-thong2, si3-koe3 kiaN-si2 lo5-lang5; khia7-khi2 e5 sou2-chai7, ia7 ak-ak chak-chak; chiah8  chheng7 e5 mih8, ia7 boe7 hiau2-tit tioh8 chheng-khi3 soe3-ji7, chiau3 oe7-seng e5 hoat-tou7 lai5 kiaN5, kan-ta beh kho3 hiah e5 put8-a2, eng7 choe3-chio3 ngia5  lau7-jiat8, lai5 ng3-bang7 in po2-pi3, hou7 lan2 peng5-an bo5 tai7-chi3. An2-ni beh thai3 oe7 kho3 tit leh¡H     
M7 thang kho3-se3
Tan5 Chin2 ti7 Gui7-kok e5 si5, choe3 chin toa7 e5 koaN, Hui7-chu2 tui3  Tan5 Chin2 kong2, Li2 tioh8 ai3 soe3-ji7 hok8-sai7 ong5 cho2-iu7 e5 lang5.  Li2 khoaN3 iong5-liu2 si7 kai3 khoai3 oah8, kai3 khoai3 toa7 e5 chhiu7.  Na7 than2-hoaiN5  ka7 i chai, i ia7 tian-to3 siN-khi2-lai5; at-tng7 ka7 i chai, i ia7 si7 oe7 oah8.  M7 ku2 u7 chit8 chan5, sui-jian5 u7 chap lang5 chai i, na7 u7 chit8 lang5  teh ka7 i puih8, i chiu7 boe7 oah8, boe7 toa7 chang5.  An2-ni khoaN3, eng7 chap8   
lang5 teh chai, he chin chian7 chin khoai3 oah8 e5 chhiu7; iau2 si7 boe7 tu3-tit chit8 e5 lang5 lai5 teh puih8 i.  Che si7 sim2-mih8 ian5-kou3 leh?  In-ui7 chai e5  khah oh, puih8 e5 khah khoai3.  Li2 sui-jian5 tit-tioh8 ong5 chin toa7 chai-poe5, m7-ku2 kiaN-liau2 beh puih8 li2 e5 lang5 ia7 chin choe7.  Sou2-i2 li2 tioh8 kin2-sin7 kap lang5 saN-ho5, m7-thang kho3-se3, liah8- choe3 ong5 hou7 li2 kho3 chiu7 kau3 giah8.  Na7 an2-ni, chiah m7 bian2 u7 gui5-hiam2.     
Hian7-si5 e5 lang5, siat-su2 u7 se3 thang kho3, beh kah  i boh8-tit gia5-chhut lai5 eng7, si7 chin ui5-lan5.  Khah choe7 si7 hit ho7 chin7 lat8 thiam2-mi7 koaN-hu2, ng3-bang7 i e5 se3 lai5 hou7 lan2 kho3, chiah khi3 chin7-lat8 kiau-ngou7 pat2 lang5; an2-ni liah8 choe3 chin the2-bian7.  Beh chhe7 hit ho7 bo5 kek-khui3 e5 lang5, si7 chin chio2.  Chai7-cha2 Chi-na2 chhit-kok e5 si5, Siong Iong3 choe3 Chin5 kok e5 chaiN2-siong3, i choan kho3 Chin5 Hau3-kong chit8 e5 lang5 na7-tiaN7; ki5-u5 lian5 thai3-chu2 kong2 oe7 lioh8-a2 m7 tioh8, ia7 chiong thai3-chu2 e5 sian-siN bin7-nih8 ka7 i chhiah ji7, phiN7 ka7 i koah khi2-lai5.  Kau3 Hau3-kong si2, thai3-chu2 chiap ui7, bo5 joa7-ku2 soa3 liah8-khi3, ngou2-ma2 hun-si. An2-ni kho2-kian3 se3-lek8 si7 long2 boe7 kho3 tit.  Lang5 kong2 bou2-tan-hoe sui-jian5 si7 ho2, ia7 tioh8 ai3 u5 lek8- hioh8 lai5 saN hu5-chhi5.  Na7-si7 kan-ta kho3 i oe7 pa- kiat hiah e5 lo2-tia tai7-jin5, ia7 kap pat8 lang5 long2 boe7 ho5, kiaN-liau2 i sou2 oa2-kho3 e5 lo2-tia kap tai7-jin5 ia7 hou7 i kho3 boe7 tiau5.  In-ui7 lang5 e5 siN-si2 heng-soe si7 bo5 tek-khak.  Lun7-kau3 sou2 oe7 kho3 tit, tok8-tok8 chit8 e5 na7-tiaN7, chiu7-si7 lan2 e5 Kiu3-chu2 Ia5-sou; ia7 lan2 sou2 kho3 I, m7 si7 ai3 tit-tioh8 se3-kan hit ho7 khang-hu e5 hoa5- bun5-hian2, si7 ui7-tioh8 leng5-hun5 eng2-oah8 e5 ian5-kou3. Koh lan2 sou2 kho3 I, m7 si7 kho3 I e5 se3-thau5, si7 kho3 I e5 jin5-ai3 kap un-tian2.  I e5 jin5-ai3 bo5 lun7 lang5 e5 phaiN2 kau3 toh-loh8, na7 hoan2-hoe2 jin7-choe7 sin3 lai5 kho3 I,  chiu7 oe7 tit-tioh8 kiu3.  In-ui7 lang5 e5 sou2 kiaN5, long2 than3 in e5 su-iok8, boe7  bian2-tit hoan7-tioh8 Siong7-te3 e5 kai3-beng7, chiau3 kong-gi7 lai5 phoaN3-toan3, long2 tioh8  siu7 eng2-oan2 e5 heng5-hoat8.  M7-ku2 Siong7-te3 put-jim2 ki5 sim, chiah eng7 chhut chit ho7 siok8-choe7 e5 hoat- to7.  Kong2 siok8-choe7, m7 si7 chhin-chhiuN7 se3-kan eng7 chiN5-gun5 lai5 mai2-chiok, kiu5-kiam2 in e5 choe7-koa3, si7 eng7 thoe3-oaN7 e5 hong-hoat, chiu7-si7 Siong7-te3 khoaN3 lang5 hoan7-tioh8 eng2-oan2 tim5-lun5 e5 choe7, chiu7 chiong i e5 KiaN2 thoat-chhut, loh8-lai5 se3-kan chhut-si3 chhin- chhiuN7 lang5, lai5 thoan5 Thian-kok e5 hok-im, kio3 lang3 tioh8 sin3; kau3 saN chap8 lian5 he3, soa3 hou7 lang5 liah8 khi3 teng3 si2 ti7 sip8-ji7-ke3.  TaN na7 chiau3 lang5 teh siuN7, Ia5-sou ki3-jian5 si7 Pe7 Siong7-te3 thoat-chhut  
lai5, se3- kan lang5 thai3 u7 koan5-leng5 thang liah8 I, koh ka7 I hai7 si2 leh?  M7 ku2 che chiu7-si7 Siong7-te3 eng7 chhut siok8 choe7 e5 hong-hoat, kio3 Ia5-sou thoe3 si2, eng7 I  e5 po2-huih soe2 lang5 e5 choe7.  Chong2-si7 si2 au7 saN jit8 Siong7-te3 u7 hou7 I koh oah8, soa3 pek8-jit8 seng thian, beng7-leng7 I e5 hak8-seng, khi3 phou2 thiN-e7 thoan5 hok- im.  Lang5 na5 sin3 I, chiu7 tit-tioh8 kiu3, m7 sin3 e5 kau3- be2 tioh8 teng7 choe7.  Sou2-i2 kong2 oe7 kho3 tit e5 chi2-u7 Ia5-sou na7-tiaN7, ki5-u5 long2 boe7 kho3 tit liau2-liau2.  
Put ti put choe7
 Chhan5 Su3 bu2-ban7 Chou-kok e5 jin5-kun, Chou-kun beh thai5 i. Chhan5 Su3 chhiN- kiaN, chiu7 khi3 kiN3 Hui7-chu2, kiu5 thoe3 i seh- cheng5.  Hui7-chu2 chiu7 khi3 kiN3 Chou-kun, mng7 i kong2, Siat-su2 chim2-ma2 u7 chit8 e5 lang5 lai5 kiN3 li2, i tiau5-kou3-i3 eng7 chit8 bak8 chhauh8-chhauh2 nih ka7 li2 khoaN3, m7 chai li2 beh chaiN2-iuN7 khoan2-thai7 i.  Chou-kun kong2, I an2-ni hi3-lang7 goa2, goa2 tek-khak thai5 i.  Hui7-chu2 koh kong2, Na7-si7 lai5 e5 lang5 si7 chhiN-mi5 e5, he beh chaiN2-iuN7? Chou-kun kong2, He goa2 bo5 kang7 i; in-ui7 ki3-jian5 si7 chhiN-mi5 e5 lang5, i bak8-chiu to bo5 khoaN3-kiN3, boe7 bian2-tit oe7 chhauh8- chhauh8 nih; lang5 kong2 put ti put choe7, i ka-ki7 to m7-chai an2-ni si7 sit-le2, sou2-i2 bo5 beh pan7 i e5 choe7.  Hui7-chu2 chiu7 koh kong2, Na7 an2-ni chit e5 Chhan5 Su3 e5 teh choe3 lang5, ti7 tang-peng5 e5 si5, bu5-ban7-tioh8 Che5-hou5, ti7 lam5-si3 e5 si5, ia7 leng5-jiok2-tioh8 Chhou2-ong5, i ti7 chit e5 lam7-sam2 khi-bio5 lang5 e5 tai7-chi3, sng3 si7  pe7-bu2 siN-chiaN5 e5 chhiN-mi5 e5, li2 mih-sai2 oan3-hun7 i leh? Chou-kun thiaN-liau2 chiu7 soah-khi3, bo5 khi3 pan7 Chhan5 Su3 e5 choe7.  
Lun7-kau3 se3-kan e5 lang5, eng2-eng2 u7 hit ho7 ai3 kap siau2-jin5 e5 lang5 lai5-ong2, kau3 au7-lai5 hou7 i lui7-tioh8, siu7 khek-khui, ka-ki7 iau2 m7 jin7 m7 bat lang5, hoan2-tng2 khi3 oan3-hun7 hit e5 siau2-jin5, che kiam2 u7 koh-iuN7 chhin-chhiuN7 kap chhiN-mi5 e5 teh cheng-lun7 hit e5 bak8-chiu chhauh8-chhauh8 nih mah?  Iah8 chiu7-si7 kau3-hoe7-lai7 e5 lang5, tui3 se3-siok8 lang5 teh kau-chiap u7 si5 in-ui7 cheng-lun7 to7-li2, pian7-pok kau3 beh saN-me7.  Lan2 ia7 bo5 siuN7, in to iau2-be7 tit-tioh8 to7-li2, sim-koaN be7 siu7 Sin5 e5 kam2-hoa3, bak8-chiu chhin-chhiuN7 be7 khui leh; an2-ni chiu7 m7 thang kap in teh chhia-poaN5.       
 
 
Chu7-siong mau5-tun2
Chhou2-kok u7 chit8 e5 lang5 teh boe7 tun2, (chiu7-si7 tin5-pai5), ia7 teh boe7 mau5, (chiu7-si7 chhiuN), ka-ki7 o-lo2 i e5 tin5-pai5 chaiN2-iuN7 e5 kian-kou3, bo5 lun7 sim2-mih8 mih8, long2 chhak8 boe7 thau3 ke3 khi3.  Koh ke3 bo5 joa7-ku2, iu7- koh ka-ki7 o-lo2 i e5 chhiuN si7 chin lai7, chin ho2 kng3; bo5 lun7 sim2-mih8 mih8 chhak8-liau2 chiu7 thau3 ke3-khi3.  Tng hit-si5 u7 chit8 e5 lang5 mng7 i kong2, Li2 an2-ni  ka-ki7 tian2-li2 e5 mau5 si7 joa7 lai7, tun2 si7 joa7 kian-kou3, taN m7 chai toh-loh8 chit8 hang7 khah sit8-chai7;  thai3 m7 eng7 li2 e5 mau5 lai5 chhak8 li2 e5 tun2 khoaN3-bai7-teh?  Hit e5 Chhou2-kok  e5 lang5 soa3 bo5 poaN3 ku3 oe7 thang in3.     
Hian7-si5 u7 chit8 ku3 siok8-gu2 teh kong2, Chu7-siong mau5-tun2, a2-si7 kong2, Ka-ki7 mau5-tun2, chiu7-si7 chit e5 tian2-kou3.  Si7 teh chi2 hit-ho7 chit8 chhui3 tau3 siang chih8, tai7-seng kong2 e5 oe7 kap au7-bin7 long2 bo5 ho5 e5. Sou2-i2 bo5 lun7 choe3 tai7-chi3, i2-kip8 teh kong2 oe7, long2 tioh8 siuN7-lai5 khi3-to3, m7-thang sui5-pian7 lam7-sam2 kong2, chiah boe7 u7 chit khoan2 chu7-siong mau5-tun2 e5 su7.    
Bo5 li7-ek lang5
Che5-kok u7 chit8 e5 chhut-mia5 e5 thak8- chheh lang5, mia5 kio3 Chhan5 Tiong7.  I m7 ai3 choe3 koaN, kam-goan7 un2-ku san-lim5, choe3 kang tou7 pa2, khoaN3-phoa3 se3-kan beng5-li7 chit nng7 ji7.  Au7-lai5 u7 chit8 e5 Song3- kok e5 lang5, mia5 kio3 Khut Kok, lai5 kiN3 i, ka7 i kong2, Goa2 ku2-ku2 chiu7  thiaN-kiN3 sian-siN li2 e5 ho2 mia5-siaN, kong2 li2 peng5-seng koat-toan3 m7  kheng2 kho3 lang5 chiah8 png7.  TaN goa2 u7 chit8 khoan2 chai pu5-a2 e5 hoat-tou7 beh hian3 hou7 li2, oe7 hou7 sou2 chai e5 pu5-a2 teng7 khok-khok, na2 chhin-chhiuN7 chioh8- thau5 e5 khoan2, koh chin kau7, ia7 bo5 khang bo5 phang7.  Chhan5 Tiong7 thiaN-liau2 chiu7 kong2, Chai pu5-a2 e5 lou7-eng7, si7 beh chiong i lai5 toe2 tang toe2 sai.  Na7 si7 teng7 kau3 chhin-chhiuN7 chioh8-thau5, kau7-kau7 koh bo5 khang bo5 phang7, an2-ni chiu7 boe7 eng7 tit thang phoa3-khui khi2-lai5 toe2 mih8 tit. Che beh kap lang5 sng3 choe3 sim2-mih8 pu5- a2 leh?  Khut Kok chiu7 in3 i kong2, Na7 an2-ni goa2  
chiu7 beh chiong chit e5 hoat-tou7 pang3 hiat kak8 liau2.  Chong2-si7 chhin-chhiuN7 Sian-siN chit khoan2 e5 m7 kheng2 kho3 lang5 chiah8 png7, tek-khak ia7 si7 bo5 li7- ek ti7 lang5; kiaN-liau2 sian-siN ia7 si7 kap chit khoan2 teng7 khok-khok e5 pu5-a2 sio siang7 leh.     
Lang5 kap khim5-siu3 hit e5 toa7 hun-piat e5 sou2-chai7, chiu7-si7 lang5 oe7 chai-kio3 hok8-sai7 Siong7-te3 kap hok8- sai7 lang5.  Na7 kan-ta chai u7 i ka-ki7, ia7 long2 m7 chai u7 pat8 lang5, koh m7 chai thang kong2 u7 chit8 ui7 chin-sit8 bo5 lam7-sam2 eng2-oan2 oah8 ti7-teh e5 Chu2-chaiN2, an2- ni chiu7 sit-loh8 choe3 lang5 e5 chu-keh.  Sou2-i2 Seng3- keng u7 kong2, Lin2 e5 kng tioh8 chio3 ti7 lang5 e5 bin7- cheng5, hou7 in khoaN3-kiN3 lin2 e5 ho2 sou2 kiaN5, lai5 kui eng5- kng hou7 lin2 ti7 thiN-nih8 e5 Pe7.  Chiau3 an2-ni khoaN3 lang5 na7 chhin-chhiuN7 hit ho7 siu-to7-jin5 khi3 un2-ku san-lim5, kan-ta beh kiu3 ka-ki7 e5 leng5-hun5, kiam2 m7 si7 sit-loh8 choe3 lang5 e5 pun2-hun7?    
Kou3-chip put-thong
 Teng7-kok u7 chit8 e5 lang5 beh chhut khi3 boe2 chit8 siang oe5, tai7-seng ti7 in chhu3-nih8, chiu7 chiong i e5 kha, niu5 khoaN3 joa7 tng5 joa7 toa7, pi2-kau3 chit8 e5 iuN7 chham kha-nih8 ho5-ho5, chiu7 chhiaN2 he7 ti7 toh-teng2.  Au7- lai5 khi3 kau3 ti7 koe-nih8, chiah siuN7-tioh2 boe7 ki3-tit theh8 hit e5 pan7 lai5.  Ti7 koe-chhi7 nih8 sui-jian5 u7 chin choe7 e5 oe5, khiok m7-kheng2 boe2, kong2 i boe7 ki3-tit theh8 hit e5 iuN7 lai5 pi2 khoaN3-bai7-teh.  Kau3 theng3-hau7 i to3-khi3 in chhu3, theh8 hit e5 iuN7 lai5 e5 si5, to i2-keng soaN3 chhi7, tiam3 long2 koaiN liau2-liau2 lah. In-ui7 an2-ni soa3 boe2 bo5 oe5.  U7 lang5 ka7 i kong2, Li2 thai3 m7 eng7 li2 e5 kha loh8-khi3 pi2, chheng7 kau3 oe7 ho5-ho5 tu2 ho2 mih-sai2 tioh8 koh to3-khi3 theh8 hit e5 pan7.   I chiu7 in3 kong2, Leng5-khou2 tioh2 sin3 hit e5 pan7, m7 thang sin3 chit siang kha.     
Na7 lun7 se3-kan, ia7 u7 chit khoan2 hit ho7 lang5, choan-choan si7 sin3 kou2-cha2 e5 hoat-to7, m7 sin3 sin e5 hoat-tou7, m7 chai kau3 kou2-cha2 e5 hoat-tou7, long2 si7 hah8 ti7 hit e5 si5-ki teh eng7.  Na7 si7 kan-ta chai hit e5 kou2- cha2 e5 hoat-tou7, ia7 long2 boe7 hiau2-tit i5-si5 che3-gi5, an2- ni chiu7 tek-khak oe7 gou7 toa7-su7.    
 
Oh8 m7 tioh8 iuN7
Teng7-koaiN7 e5 sou2-chai7, u7 chit8 e5 lang5 kah in bou2 ka7 i choe3 chit8 nia8 khou3.  In bou2 mng7 i kong2, Beh choe3 sim2-mih8 khoan2? Hit e5 lang5 kong2, Chiau3 chhin-chhiuN7 goa2 ku7 e5 khou3 hit khoan2.  In bou2 chiu7 chiong hit te3 sin e5 pou3, hui2-hoai7 hou7 phaiN2, chiah choe3 chit8 nia2 kap i e5 ku7 e5 saN-tang5.     
Koh u7 chit8 hang7; ti7 kui2-chap8 ni5 cheng5, Hiong-kang2 taN-chiah koah kui Eng-kok, chiu7 u7 chin choe7 Eng-kok lang5 lai5 tiam3 ti7 hia, kaN2 si7 in-ui7 iau2-be7 u7 choe3 chhai5- hong5 e5 sai-hu7 lai5, sou2-i2 hiah e5 Eng-kok lang5, u7 khi3 chhiaN3 hia e5 pun2-toe7 lang5 ka7 in choe3 iuN5-hok8.  Hia e5 pun2-toe7 chhai5- hong5 pou7-pin5 m7 bat khoaN3-kiN3 hit khoan2 e5 saN-a2-khou3, khoaN3-liau2 hoan ki3-ka3, chia ia7 chit8 e5 te7-a2, hia ia7 chit8 e5 te7-a2, kui nia2 ui kau3 choan khang.  Chiu7 koh mng7 in kong2, Beh chaiN2-iuN7 choe3?  Hit e5 Eng-kok lang5 kong2, Chiau3 goa2  ku7 e5 hit khoan2 an2-ni choe3.  Hit e5 chhai5-hong5 chiu7 chiau3 in ku7 e5 pan7, ka7 i ka loh8 khi3 choe3, lian5 hit ho7 kiN phoa3 khang koh thiN7 e5, i ia7 chiau3 hit e5 kiN phoa3 e5 se3-bin7,  ka7 i ka hou7 khui, chiah koh thiN7.  Kau3 au7-lai5 choe3 ho2, hiahN khi3 hou7 hit e5 Eng-kok lang5, thi2-khui khi2-lai5 chit8-e7 khoaN3,  thai3 oe7 kui nia2 ka kau3 chia ia7 chit8 khang, hia ia7 chit8 khang, chiah koh pou2 kau3 hoe lok8-lok8?  Chiu7 ham i khau-chhau2, m7  na7 m7 kang-chiN5 hou7 i, tian-to3 beh ka7 i tho2 pou3-sin e5 gun5.  Liong2-peng5 cheng-lun7 boe7 soah; au7-lai5 u7 lang5 chhut-lai5 ka7 in chhu2, chiah tiau5-tit8.  
Lun7-kau3 tak8 kok e5 hoat-tou7 kap hong-siok8, to long2 u7 ho2 ia7 u7 phaiN2; m7 ku2 beh than3 hit e5 ho2 e5 khah oh, beh oh8 phaiN2 e5 si7 khah khoai3.  Na7 beh kan- ta chai hit-e5 phaiN2 e5 sou2-chai7, ia7 m7 chai thang oh8 ho2 e5, an2-ni kap hit e5 Teng7-kok e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 teh choe3 khou3, chham hit e5 Hiong-kang2 chhai5-hong3 e5 teh  choe3 iuN5-hok8, u7 sim2-mih8 koh-iuN7 leh?       
 
Sia2-seng chhu2-gi7
Tong-iong5 Tiong5-pan2-pho Tio7 Chu2-liong5 kiu3 A-tau2, hit-si5 Lau5 Pi7 kap Cho5 Chho3 kau-chian3, Lau5 Pi7 thai5-su, i e5 chiong3 kap ke-koan3 long2 si3-soaN3 liau2-liau2. I u7 chit8-e5 tai7-chiong3 mia5 kio3 Tio7 Chu2-liong5, ti7 pah-ban7 kun-tiong beh chhe7 in e5 chu2-bu2 kap sio2 chu2-lang5, jip kau3 Tiong5-pan2-pho e5 lam5-peng5, chiah khoaN3-kiN3 hu-jin5 pho7 tau2 ti7 chit8 e5 phoa3 chhiuN5-a2 e7 chiN2-noa5- teng2 teh che7, bak8-sai2 si3-lam5-sui5.  Chu2- liong5 siuN7-khi2 Lau5 Pi7 tok8-tok8 chit8 e5 kiaN2 na7-tiaN7, na7 bo5 kiu3 i chiu7 Han3-tiau5 soa3 choat8-su5, chiu7 koaN2-kin2 chhiaN2 Bi2 Hu-jin5 chiuN7 be2, thang saN-kap to5-mia7.  Hu-jin5 kong2, Goa2 si2 si7 bo5 iau3-kin2, chong2-si7 in lau7-pe7 chi2-u7 chit8 e5 kiaN2 na7-tiaN7, choan- choan oa2-kho3 chiong-kun po2-hou7 i, m7- thang in-ui7 goa2 lai5 lian5-lui7 li2.  Kong2-liau2 chiu7 chiong A-tau2 pho7 hou7 i, soa3 thiau3 loh8 kou2-chiN2--nih8 si2.  Chu2-liong5 chiu7 chiong tau2 pak8 toa3 seng-khu--nih8 phe siN3-mia7 phah chhut ban7-teng5-ui5, chiong A-tau2 lai5 heng5 Lau5 Pi7.  Au7-lai5 ti7 Se-siok8 chiap-ui7 choe3 hong5-te3.  Che sit8-chai7 si7 choan kho3 Chu2-liong5 e5 iong2-beng2.     
Lan2 thak8 chit khoan2 e5 kou3-tian2, siuN7 khi2 Bi2 Hu- jin5 pang3-sak siN3-mia7, Chu2-liong5 phe-mia7 kau-chian3, an2-ni lai5 kiu3 A-tau2, si7 in-ui7 A-tau2 e5 si2 oah8 chiu7-si7 koan-he7 Han3-tiau5 e5 chun5 bong5, sou2-i2 khoaN3 choe3 bo5 ke3 e5 po2-poe3; pang3-sak siN3-mia7 lai5 kiu3 i, chiau3 li2- khi3 khiok eng-kai tioh8 an2-ni.     
TaN se3-kan lang5 sou2 po2-poe3--e5 chiu7-si7 siN3-mia7, na7- si7 iau2 u7 pi2 siN3-mia7 koh khah iau3-kin2 e5, chiu7-si7 boe7 si2-sit, boe7 biat8-bo5 e5 leng5-hun5.  Ki-tok kang3-lim5 lai5 se3-kan, pang3-sak siN3-mia7 ti7 sip8-ji7-ke3, che tiau5-kou3-i3 si7 beh lai5 kiu3 se3-kan lang5 e5 leng5-hun5.  Seng3-keng u7 kong2, Jin5-chu2 kau3, si7 beh kiu3 sit-loh8 e5 lang5 (Thai3.  18: 11). 
 
Kui2-koai3 e5 pun2-su7
Chai7-cha2 u7 chit8 e5 lang5 teh ka7 Che5-ong5 ui7 ji7-ui7, Che5-ong5 mng7  i kong2, Ui7 sim2-mih8 te7-it ui5-lan5?  Hit e5 ui7-kang kong2,  Kau2 be2 choe3  ui5-lan5.  Che5-ong5 koh mng7 kong2, Ui7 sim2-mih8 te7 it khoai3?   Ui7-kang koh in3 i kong2, Kui2-koai3 iau-chiN choe3 khoai3 ui7.  In-ui7  kau2 be2 si7 lang5 cha2-am3 siong5-siong5 teh khoaN3, na7 ui7 chit8-tiam2-a2 bo5 tu2-ho2 hah8, lang5 chiu7 liam5-piN khoaN3 oe7 chhut; sou2-i2 khah oh-tit  ui7.  Iau-chiN kui2-koai3 sng3-si7 bo5 heng5 bo5 iaN2, ia7 bou5 lang5 bat khoaN3-kiN3; put-lun7 ui7 sim2-mih8 khoan2, lang5 long2 boe7 hiau2-tit hun-piat, sou2-i2 u7 khoai3 ui7.     
Se3-kan eng2 u7 chit cheng2 lang5, chin gau5 chng-ki5 choe3-koai3, piN3 hiah e5 ki5-koai3 e5 tai7-chi3, ka-ki7 liah8 choe3 si7 chin gau5, ki5-sit8 long2 si7 hiah e5 ui7 kui2-koai3 e5 pun2-su7, lai5 teh phian3 lang5 na7-tiaN7.  Che ia7 thang pi2-pheng7 chhin-chhiuN7 lang5 kong2 in u7 hoat-tou7 thang phoa3 te7-gek8 khui thian-tong5, che khiok khah khoai3 kong2, in-ui7 oh-tit thang kap in pian7-pok.  Chong2- si7 lang5 na7 kong2 in u7 hoat-tou7 thang kiu3 lang5 chhut in e5 phaiN2, piN3 choe3 ho2 lang5, che khah oh-tit kong2, in-ui7 u7 iaN2 bo5 iaN2 lang5 liam5-piN chai.  Ia7 chhin- chhiuN7 Ma2-kho22: 9 sou2 ki3-chai3 Ia5-sou mng7 cheng3 lang5 kong2, Ka7 pian3-sui7 e5 kong2, Li2 e5 choe7 sia3 lah, a2-si7 kong2, Khi2-lai5, gia5 li2 e5 phou-a2 lai5 kiaN5, toh-loh8 chit8 hang7 khah khoai3?  Chiu7 tng cheng3 lang5 e5 bin7-cheng5 i-ho2 hit e5 lang5, hou7 lang5 chai Jin5-chu2 ti7 toe7--nih8 u7 koan5 thang sia3 choe7.  Lan2 e5 Seng3-kau3 na7 u7 kong-hau7 thang kiu3 phaiN2 lang5 piN3 choe3 ho2 lang5, hou7 lang5 khoaN3, peh-siN3 chiu7 khah khoai3 sin3 lan2 sou2 kong2 boe7 khoaN3-kiN3 e5 su7.  
Bat lang5 khah-ho2 bat chiN5
Lou2-kok e5 chaiN2-siang3 Beng7 Hian3-chu2, khi3 Chin3-kok tiau5-pheng3.  Chin3-kok e5 chaiN2-siong3, Han5 Soan-chu2, siat ian5-siah8 khoan2-thai7 i; oaN7 saN-ui7 e5 kheh thiaN, long2 pai5 kau3 chin sui2, chin chiau5-pi7, koh chin ho2 khoaN3.  Hian3-chu2 kong2, Chin- chiaN3 si7 pu3 kau3-kek8 liau2.  Soan-chu2 kong2, Lin2 chhu3 pi2 goan2 chia an2-chaiN2-iuN7? Hian3-chu2 kong2, Goan2 chhu3 song3 kau3 m7 ho2 kong2.  Chi2-u7 nng7 e5 thak8-chheh lang5, chit8-e5 mia5 kio3 Gan5 Hoe5, chit8-e5 mia5 kio3 Chu Bu5-leng5, hou7 goa2 tit-tioh8 kok--nih8 oe7 peng5-tiaN7, peh-siN3 oe7 an-un2; goa2 sou2 u7 e5, chin7 chai7 an2-ni na7-tiaN7.  Kau3 Hian3-chu2 chhut-khi3, Soan-chu2 chiah kong2, I si7 kun-chu2 e5 lang5, liah8 hit ho7 poe5-iuN2 gau5-lang5 choe3 ho2-giah8.  Goa2 si7  siau2-jin5 e5 lang5, chiah liah8 chiah e5 kim-gun5 chu-gek8 choe3 ho2-giah2.  Goa2 ka-ki7 siuN7 sit8-chai7 chin kian3-siau3.     
Siok8-gu2 kong2, Bat lang5 khah ho2 bat chiN5, sit8-chai7 chin u7-iaN2.  M7-ku2  se3-kan lang5, m7 tan7-na7 peng5-iu2, in-ui7 chi5 N-chai5 lai5 choat8-kau,  chiu7-si7 hiaN-ti7, pe7-bu2, bou2-kiaN2, i2-kip8 chhin-chhek e5 teh kau-chiap,  to tioh8 chit hang7 chiN5 choe3 thau5-cheng5.  An2-ni kho2-kian3 chiN5 e5 khui3- lat8 si7 chin toa7, chin gau5 pe2-pak8 lang5, na7 m7 si7 hit ho7 kam-goan7 hou7 i song3-hiong hoaN-hi2 khoai3-lok8 lai5 siu2 to7-li2 e5 lang5, chiu7 bo5 hiah khoai3 oe7 thoat-li7 chit hang7 e5 pe2-pak8.  Ma2-kho2 10: 23, Ia5-sou tui3 I e5 hak8-seng kong2, Pu3 lang5 beh jip8 Siong7-te3 e5 kok si7 chin oh.  Che si7 in-ui7 u7 chit8 e5 ho2-giah8 lang5 lai5 kiN3 Ia5-sou, kui7-teh kiu5 khoaN3 tioh8 chaiN2-iuN7 choe3, chiah oe7 tit-tioh8 eng2-oan2 oah8.  Ia5- sou kio3 i tioh8 khi3 pian3 boe7 i e5 ke-giap8, lai5 chin2-che3 song3-hiong lang5, chiu7 chiN5-chai5 chek-chu7 ti7 thiN- nih8; chong2-si7 hit e5 lang5 thiaN-kiN3 chit ho7 oe7, bin7 sui5- si5 pian3-sek, u7 iu-chhiu2 e5 khoan2, ia7 soa3 choe3 i khi3. An2-ni kho2-kian3 chiN5-chai5 e5 khui3-lat8 teh pak8 lang5 si7 chin toa7.  Ai3 tit thoat-li7 chit khoan2 e5 pe2-pak8, tek-khak tioh8 khoaN3 oe7 phoa3 chiah e5 se3-kan2 e5 eng5- hian2; m7 thang chhin-chhiuN7 Han5 Soan-chu2, kan-ta oe7 hiau2-tit chng-thaN7 goa7-bin7 e5 ho2 khoaN3. 
Chai7 Chin5 ui7 Chin5
 Han3-tiau5 e5 si5 u7 chit8 e5 lang5 mia5 kio3 Koai2 Thong, si7 choe3 Han5 Sin3 e5 chham- bou5.  Kau3 Han5 Sin3 khi3 phoa3 Che5-kok liau2-au7, Koai2 Thong u7 kio3 Han5 Sin3 tioh8  poan7 Han3, chiong Che5-kok tok8-lip8 khi2- lai5 koan2.  Han5 Sin3 put-jim2 ki5 sim, m7 thiaN i e5 chhui3.  Au7-lai5 Han5 Sin3 hou7 Han3 Ko-chou2 thai5-khi3.  Koai2 Thong ia7 hou7 liah8 lai5.  Han3 Ko-chou2 mng7 i kong2, Li2 bat kah Han5 Sin3 cho7 hoan2 mah?   Koai2 Thong in3 i kong2, To7-chek (kou2-cha2 e5 phaiN2 lang5)e5 kau2, khoaN3-kiN3 Giau5-te3 (kou2-cha2 e5 seng3-ong5)chiu7 toa7 pui7, chong2-si7 Giau5-te3 m7-si7  put-jin5 e5 jin5-kun, kau2  
khoaN3-kiN3 m7 si7 i e5 chu2-lang5, khiok si7 boe7 bian2-tit bo5 pui7.  Tong-si5 goa2 chai-kio3 u7 Han5 Sin3, khiok boe7 hiau2-tit u7 Pe3-ha7. Han3 Ko-chou2 thiaN-liau2 soa3 sia3-bian2 i e5 choe7.     
Lang5 kong2, Chai7 Chin5 ui7 Chin5, chai7 Chhou2 ui7 Chhou2, sng3 si7 kah lang5 tioh8 chin7-tiong, tioh8 chin7 pun2-hun7.  Chong2-si7 ia7 ai3 khoaN3 si7 sim2-mih8 khoan2 e5 chin7-tiong.  U7 chit8 cheng2 hit ho7 pai7-ka chu2-te7, chham hiah-e5  Ong5--ko Liu2--ko khi3 oang, long2 bo5 beh kou3 lai7-thau5, sim7-chi3 tau3 hiah e5 lai5 khi-hu7 in e5 chhin hiaN-ti7.  Ia7 u7 chit8-chiong2 hit-ho7 choan-bun5 teh pang-chan7 tui3-tek8, lai5 siong-hai7 pun2-sin e5 bu2- kok, i ia7 hia-hia pai-pai, ka-ki7 kong2 si7 cheng3-tit8 bo5 phian-su, si7 chin7-tiong7 teh po3 kok, m7 chai an2-ni tui3 sim2-mih8 lang5 teh chin7-tiong, ia7 teh po3 sim2-mih8 lang5 e5 kok.  Hai3-ah¡I  Chhin-chhiuN7 chit khoan2 e5 chin7-tiong, chit khoan2 e5 sim-koaN, soa3 khah-su hit ho7 kau2 e5 lui7, ia7 soa3 m7 chai thang hun-piat ho2 phaiN.      
PoaN chhu3 boe7 ki3-tit poaN bou2
Lou2 Ai-kong mng7 Khong2-chu2 kong2, Goa2 thiaN-kiN3 lang5 teh kong2,  hit ho7 chin gau5 boe7 ki3-tit tai7-chi3 e5 lang5, teh poaN chhu3 e5 si5, lian5 in bou2 ia7 boe7 ki3-tit poaN khi3.  Khong2-chu2 kong2, Che iau2  m7 si7 gau5 boe7 ki3-tit e5 lang5; hit ho7 chin gau5 boe7 ki3-tit e5 lang5, lian5 i  pun2-sin ia7 soa3 boe7 ki3-tit. Ai-kong mng7 kong2, An3-chaiN2-iuN7 pun2-sin ia7 soa3 boe7 ki3-tit?  Khong2-chu2 kong2, Kou2-cha2 e5 si5 u7 chit8 e5 Ha7 Kiat8-ong5,  i e5 chun-kui3 choe3 kau3 hong5-te3, i e5 ho2-giah8 koan2 kau3 thong kok.  M7 ku2 m7 than3 sian- ong5 e5 to7-li2, chhia-chhi2 ian3-lok8, be5 ti7 chiu2- sek; au7-lai5 kok phoa3 ka bong5, soa3 hou7 Thong-ong5 thai5-khi3, che kiam2  m7 si7 soa3 boe7 ki3-tit i pun2-sin mah?     
Se3-kan hit ho7 boe7 ki3-tit pun2-sin e5 lang5, kiam2 kan-ta Ha7 Kiat8 na7-tiaN7?  Se3-kan boe7 ki3-tit pun2-sin e5 su7, ia7 m7 tan7-na7 chiu2-sek na7-tiaN7.  Hoan7-na7 lang5  
choe3 chit8 hang7 bo5 chiau3 li2-khi3 e5 tai7-chi3, a2 si7 kong2 chit8 ku3 bo5 li2 e5 oe7, i2-kip8 chun5 chit8 hang7 bo5 to7-li2 e5 liam7-thau5, chiu7 long2 kau3-giah8 thang hai7- tioh8 in e5 seng-khu kap sim-koaN.  Sou2-i2 kou2-cha2 kun- chu2 e5 lang5, tui3 ka-ki7 chit8 e5, ia7 tioh8 chun5 kin2-sin7 keng2-kai3 e5 sim.  
Bo5 sin3 pin5, oe7 gou7 su7
 Chiu-tiau5 e5 si5, u7 chit8 e5 jin5-kun, mia5 kio3 Hiu-ong5, i che7 ui7 te7 saN ni5, chiu7 chhoa7 Po Su7 choe3 phian-hui, ong5 put- chi2 tek-thiong2.  Ia7 siN chit8 e5 kiaN2, mia5 kio3 Pek-hok8.  Keh nng7 ni5 ku2 liau2-au7, chiu7 chiong i e5 chiaN3-bou2 Sin-hou7 kap  thai3-chu2 Gi5-kiu7 hoe3-khi3, lip8 Po Su7 choe3 chiaN3-keng hong5-hou7, ia7 lip8 Pek-hok8 choe3 thai3-chu2.  Chong2-si7 chit e5 Po Su7 sui-jian5 hou7 Hiu-ong5 put-chi2 thiaN3-thang3, iau2-ku2 m7 bat khoaN3 i u7 hoaN-hi2 khui chhui3 lai5 chhio3 e5 bin7-iong5.  Hiu-ong5 ai8-tit i hoaN- hi2, eng7 chin choe7 hoat-tou7, ia7 lang7 i boe7 chhio; chiu7 mng7 i pun2-sin, khoaN3 i ai3 an3- chaiN2-iuN7 khah sim-sek.  Po Su7 kong2, Goa2 choe3 cha-bou2 gin2-na2 e5 si5,  ti7 goan2 chhu3-nih8 teh choe3 in-chiuN5, oe7 ki3-tit thiah-khui hit e5 tiu5-toan7 e5  si5, hit ho7 siaN put-chi2 ho2 thiaN.  Hiu-ong5 chiu7 kong2, An2-ni khah khoai3.   Chiu7 kio3 lang5 thoan5 chi2-i3 chhut-khi3 kau-tai7 Hou7-pou7, (koan2 chiN5-gun5 e5 koaN), mui2-jit8 tioh8 phoe3 chit8 pah phit e5 tiu5-tian7 jip8-lai5 keng-lai7, ia7 chiu7 thoan5 hiah e5 khah u7 lat8 e5 thai3- kam3, chit8 lang5 khia7 chit3 peng5, chiong hit  e5 tiu5-toan7, tui3 thau5-a2 sio2-khoa2 ka khui, chit8 lang5 khiu2 chit8 peng5, chhut-lat8 li3 khi3, li3 kau3 kih8-kih8 kiuh8-kiuh8.  Po Su7 thiaN-liau2 put-chi2 hoaN-hi2; m7-ku2 ke3  bo5 kui2 jit8, na2 thiaN na2 koaiN3-si3, m7 na7 bo5 sim2-mih8 chhu3-bi7, soa3 na2 chhin-chhiuN7 chin kiau2-jiau2, ia7 chiu7 m7 ai3 chhio3, m7 ai3 koh thiaN lah.     
Hiu-ong5 siuN7-liau2 bo5 hoat-tou7, chiu7 chhoa7 i chiuN7-khi3 ong5-kiong lai7 e5 tai5-teng2 nih8, chiah kio3 lang5 khi3 pang3 ian-tun. (lan-tun si7 chhin-chhiuN7 ian5-tang5 e5 khoan2-sit, chai7-cha2 bo5 tian7-po3 kap tian7- oe7 thang thong-ti siau-sit, ho7 pat ui7 chai, chiah eng7 chit ho7, tui3 kiaN-siaN5 khi2, li7 chit8 phou3 lou7, a2 si7 gou7-li2 lou7  chiu7 chhai7 chit8 ki, tit8-tit8 soa3, tit8-tit8 chhut-khi3; siat-su2 hong5-te3 tu2-tioh8 sim2-mih8 iau3-kin2 e5 su7, a2-si7 chhat8-be2 lai5 chhim-hoan7 tioh8, chiu7 chiong ian-tun pang3-khi2-lai5, jit8-si5 u7 khoaN3-kiN3 ian, mi5-si5 u7 khoaN3-kiN3  he2, ia7 thau5 chit8 ki na7 pang3, te7 ji7 ki khoaN3-kiN3,  
ia7 chiu7 pang3-khi2-lai5; an2-ni bo5 joa7-ku2 chiu7 si3-koe3 liam5-piN chai ong5 u7 hoan7-lan7, kun7-hu7 e5 chu-hou5 chiu7 khi2 peng lai5 kiu3 ka3).  Tng teh beh pang3 e5 si5, u7 i e5 jin5-sin5 chhut chau3 kong2, Che sng3 si7 Pe7-ha7 kap liat8-kok e5 chu-hou5 u7 iok, na7 m7-si7 hoan7-tioh8 toa7 iau3-kin2 e5 su7, tek-khak  boe7 eng7-tit pang3 chit e5 ian-tun tit.  Siat-su2 chim2-ma2 na7 pang3, au7-lai5 u7 su7, liat8-kok chu-hou5 chiu7 m7-sin3.  Hiu-ong5 kong2, Bo5 iau3-kin2, u7 tai7-chi3 goa2 chiah tam-tng.  Hian7-si5 thiN-e7 thai3-peng5, thai3 u7 sim2-mih8 su7?  Chiu7 kio3 lang5 khi3 pang3.  Ko2-jian5 keh bo5 joa7-ku2, moa2-thiN choan5 si7  he2-ian, kun7 kiaN-siaN5 e5 chu-hou5 khoaN3-kiN3, sui5-si5 nia2 peng beh lai5 kiu3 ka3; tiap-a2-ku2 tang-sai lam5-pak kun7-hu7 e5 chu-hou5 long2 toa3  peng kau3 lah.  Hiah e5 chu-hou5 tak8-e5 lai5 ti7 tai5-kha, mng7-khoaN3 ong5 u7 peng5-an a2 bo5, si7 u7 sim2-mih8 kin2-kip e5 tai7-chi3.  Hiu-ong5 kah lang5 ka7 in kong2, Kai-chai3 bo5 sim2-mih8 tai7-chi3, si7 in-ui7 kap Hong5-hou7 teh chhit-tho5, pang3-khi2-lai5 khoaN3-bai7 teh.  TaN chhiaN2 liat2-ui7  to3-khi3 siu2 lin2-e5 pun2-kok.  Hiah e5 chu-hou5 thiaN-liau2, li2 khoaN3 goa2, goa2 khoaN3 li2, long2 bo5 oe7 thang  kong2, chiu7 koh nia2 peng to3-khi3.  Po Su7 ti7 hit tai5-teng2, khoaN3-kiN3 hiah-nih8 choe7 e5 peng-be2, chau2 kau3  phihN-phihN chhoan2, kiah8 chhiuN kiah8 kiam3, kang2 kui2-na7 ban7 lang5, tak8-e5 hiong5 kai3- kai3, long2 si7 phah-sng3 beh sio thai5, bo5 siuN7 lai5 kau3 te3 ia7 bo5 siaN2 bou5 su7, tai7-ke bo5 i3 bo5 su3 koh to3-khi3, siuN7-liau2 chiu7 toa7 chhio3 khi2-lai5.  Hiu-ong5 khoaN3-liau2 put-chi2 hoaN- hi2.  Bo5 siuN7 koh keh gou7 lak8 ni5, hut-jian5 u7 Khian2-jiong5 e5 peng kong phah lai5. Hiu-ong5 kio3 lang5 koaN2-kin2 pang3 ian-tun, thang tiau3 kok ui7 e5 chu-hou5 nia2 peng lai5 kiu3 eng3.  Chai7 hiah e5 chu-hou5, tak8-e5 phah-sng3 si7 Hiu-ong5 kap Po Su7 teh kun2- chhio3, soa3 bo5 poaN3 lang5 beh nia2 peng lai5. Keh nng7 jit8 kiaN-siaN5 phoa3, Hiu-ong5 kap  Po Su7 chau2 kau3 Le5-soaN-kha, hou7 Khian2-jiong5 e5 ong5 jip-tioh8, soa3 hou7 chhi3--si2.     
Lun7-kau3 lang5 ti7 chit se3-kan, teh lai5-ong2 kau-poe5, long2 tioh8 u7 hit e5 lau2-sit8 sin3-iong7 khah iau3-kin2.   Chit8 ku3 hoan5 chit8 ku3, nng7 ku3 si7 chit8 siang.  Kou2 lang5 gian5 kong2, It gian5 hong3 chhut, su3-ma2 lan5 tui; chiu7-si7 kio3 lang5 tioh8 chiau3 i sou2 kong2 e5 oe7 lai5 kiaN5, m7-thang sit-loh8 sin3-iong7.  Siat-su2 na7 kap  lang5 chih-chiap tai7-chi3, sim-lai7 ia7 bo5 siuN7, chhin3-chhai2 lam7-sam2 kong2, hi-hi ha-ha, peh8-chhat8 peh8-koat, bo5 beh kong2 sit8-chai7 e5 oe7, au7-lai5 na7 tu2-tioh8 u7 cheng3-keng tai7-chi3, sui-jian5 kong2 kau3 lau2-lau2 sit8-sit8, lang5 ia7 m7 kheng2 siong-sin3.  Chhin-chhiu7 Chiu Hiu-ong5 chiah chit8 pai2 e5 choe3 m7 tioh8, chiu7 ti3-kau3 kok phoa3, lian5 ka-ki7 e5 siN3-mia7 ia7 bo5 khi3.  Khong2-chu2 kong2, Lang5 na7 bo5 sin3-sit8, m7 chai an2-choaN2-iuN7 thai3 oe7 eng7 tit; chit ho7 oe7 sit8-chai7 chin bo5 chhou3.  
Po2-sioh kong-im
Khong2-chu2 bat u7 chit8 jit8 chhut-goa7 e5 si5, thiaN-kiN3 u7 lang5 e5 siaN hau2 kau3 put- chi2 chham2-chhoeh.  I chiu7 kio3 sak- chhia--e5 kiaN5 khah kin2 teh, thang lai5 ka7 khoaN3 bai7.  Kau3 e5 si5, khoaN3-kiN3 si7 Ko Gu5 ti7 lou7-piN nih8 teh toa7 khau3.  Khong2- chu2 chiu7 loh8 chhia lai5 mng7 i kong2, Sian- siN u7 sim2-mih8 tai7-chi3 chiah-nih8 siong-sim, khau3 kau3 chiah-nih8 ai-chham2?  Ko Gu5 kong2, Goa2 u7 saN hang7 tai7-chi3, choe3-liau2 chin m7 tioh2.  Siau3-lian5 e5 si5, ai3 khi3 si3-koe3 liu5-hak8, boe7 oe7 hok2-sai7 goa2 e5 si7-toa7-lang5, si7 chit8 hang7 e5 m7 tioh8.  Sim-koaN siuN7 toa7, chi3 khi3 khah koaiN5, boe7 hiau2-tit hok8-sai7 goa2 e5 jin5-kun, si7 nng7 hang7 e5 m7 tioh8. Chham peng5-iu2 kau-poe5 put-chi2 ho2, in-ui7 sio2-khoa2 su7 chiu7 choat8- kau, si7 saN hang e5 m7 tioh8.  Chin-chiaN3 si7 chhiu7 ai3 peng5- cheng7, m7-ku2 hong m7 kheng2 soah.  KiaN8 beh chin7 hau3, si7-toa7-lang5  boe7 theng3-hau7 tit.  Ke3-khi3 boe7-tit koh-chai3 lai5 e5, si7 ni5-he3, bo5--khi3 boe7  tit koh khoaN3-kiN3 e5, si7 pe7-bu2.  TaN goa2 hian7-chai7 si7 teh theng3-hau7 si2 na7-tiaN7.  Khong2-chu2-thiaN liau2, chiu7 tui3 i e5 hak8-seng kong2, Lin2 tai7- ke tioh8 oe7 ki3-tit chiah e5 oe7.  Tng hit si5, u7 si7-toa7-lang5 ti7-teh e5 chap8-saN  lang5, kap Khong2-chu2 saN-si5, tng2-khi3 in chhu3-nih8 hok8-sai7 in e5 pe7-bu2.     
Siok8-gu2 kong2, Pe7-bu2 thiaN3 kiaN2, si7 tng5 lau5 chui2, kiaN2 thiaN3 pe7-bu2, chhiu7 be2 io5 hong.  In-ui7 choe3 kiaN2 e5 lang5, chhut-si3 chiu7 siu7 pe7-bu2 e5 iuN2-chhi7, tit8-tit8 liap8, tit8-tit8 kou3, kau3 ti7 oe7 pe5 oh8 kiaN5 e5 si5-chun7, choe3 pe7-bu2 e5 lang5, poaN3 pou7 ia7 m7 kaN2 pang3-li7.  Lioh8-a2 khah toa7 han3, chiu7 ke3-kau3 beh hou7 i thak8-chheh, ng3-bang7 au7-lai5 than3 chiah8 khah khoaN3-oah8.  Kau3 chiaN5-lang5 oe7 chu7-lip2 e5 si5, u7-e5 pe7-bu2 to i2-keng lau7- khi3 lah.  Sou2-i2 tioh8 than3-cha2 lai5 heng5 hau3-to7, ia7 tioh8 po2-sioh kong-im.  In-ui7 pe7-bu2 si7 pi2 lan2 khah lau7, boe7 oe7 siong5-siong5 kap lan2 ti7-teh.  Koh m7 tan7-na7 hok8-sai7 pe7-bu2 tioh8 an2-ni; bo5 lun7 sim-mih8 tai7-chi3, long2 tioh8 hian7 choe3 hou7 chiaN5 si7 khah ho2. Na7 si7 beh theng3-hau7 kau3 bin5-a2-chai3, kiaN-liau2 bin5-a2-chai3 u7  
bin5-chai3 e5 su7 thang pan7, boe7 oe7 iong5-un2 li2 koh choe3 kin-a2-jit8 e5 su7.  Lan2 lang5 ti7 chit se3-kan te7 it tioh8 po2-sioh e5, chiu7-si7 kong-im, put-ko3 hian7-chai7 na7-tiaN7.  In-ui7 cheng5 e5 kong-im i2-keng ke3-khi3, ban7-kou2 chhian-chhiu boe7 tit koh lai5.  I-au7 e5 kong- im,ia7 bo5 thang siok8 ti7 goa2, bong5-bong5 biau2-biau2, siN-si2 hou7 lang5 boe7 phah-sng3 tit.  Siat-su2 na7 m7 chai thang liah8 kong-im choe3 tui3-tiong7, chhut-chai7 i chit8-jit8 ke3 chit8 jit8, chit8 ni5 ke3 chit8 ni5, tek-khak boe7 bian2-tit u7 au7-lai5 e5 hoan2-hoe2 lah.  
Boe7 chip-koat-tit
Lou2 Ai-kong mng7 Khong2-chu2 kong2, KiaN2 than3 pe7 e5 beng7-leng7 si7 u7 hau3 mah?  Sin5 than3 kun e5 beng7-leng7 si7 chin7-tiong mah?  An2-ni lian5-lian5 nng7  saN pai2, Khong2-chu2 long2 bo5 in3 i.  Au7-lai5 Khong2-chu2 chhut-lai5 tui3 Chu2- kong3 teh kong2, Tu2-chiah Lou2-kun teh mng7 goa2, khoaN3 kiaN2 than3 pe7 e5 beng7-leng7, si7 u7 hau3 a2 m7 si7, sin5 than3 kun e5 beng7-leng7 si7 chin7-tiong a2 m7 si7, goa2 khiok bo5 in3 i, m7 chai li2 phah-sng3 chaiN2-iuN7?  Chu2-kong3 kong2, KiaN2 than3  pe7 e5 beng7-leng7 chu7-jian5 si7 hau3; sin5 than kun e5 beng7-leng7 chu7-jian5 si7 tiong; thai3 u7 sim2-mih8 thang koh in3 i?  Khong2-chu2 kong2, Chu2-kong3 li2 chin-chiaN3 si7 siau2-jin5 e5 lang5.  Kiam2 m7 bat thiaN-kiN3 kong2, Kou2-cha2 e5 si5 u7 chit8 ban7 tiuN chian3- chhia e5 kok, chiu7 u7 si3 e5 kaN2 ho2-taN2 lai5 kan3-cheng3 e5 jin5-sin5,  i e5 kok chiah boe7 hou7 lang5 koah-khi3; u7 chit8 chheng tiuN chian3-chhia e5 kok, tioh8 u7 saN e5 kaN2 kan3-cheng3 e5 jin5-sin5, i e5 sia7-chek chiah bo5  gui5-hiam2; ia7 u7 chit8 pah tiuN chian3-chhia e5 ke, ia7 tioh8 u7 nng7 e5 kaN2 kan3-cheng3 e5 lang5, i e5 chong-biau7 chiah boe7 hui2 khi3.  Choe3 kiaN2 e5  lang5, u7 cheng5-li2 thang kap in lau7-pe7 saN-chiN, boe7 kong2 tit si7 bo5  le2-sou3, choe3 peng5-iu2 e5 lang5, oe7 chiau3 li2-khi3 lai5 saN-chiN, boe7 kong2 tit si7 bo5 chiau3 kong-gi7.  Sou2-i2 kiaN2 than3 pe7 e5 beng7-leng7, be7 kau3-giah8 thang kong2 si7 u7 hau3, sin5 than3 kun e5 beng7-leng7, be7 kau3-giah8 thang kong2 si7 chin7-tiong; eng-kai tioh8 chim-chiok, khoaN3 i sou2 choe3 si7 tioh8 a2 m7 tioh8, thang than3 a2 m7 thang; si7 boe7 chip-koat tit.  An2-ni chiah oe7 chheng-hou tit choe3 u7 hau3, a2-si7 chheng- hou choe3 chin7-tiong tit.     
 
Hian7-si5 u7 chit8 khoan2 e5 lang5, na7 tu2-tioh8 lang5 khng3 i tioh8 sin3 Ia5-sou lai5 jip2 Seng3-kau3, i chiu7 ke2 kau3 chhin-chhiuN7 chin than3 in lau7-pe7 e5 beng7-leng7 e5 khoan2, chiu7 the-si5 kong2, Goan2 lau7-pe7 m7 chun2, a2 si7 kong2, Goan2 lau7-bu2 m7 kheng2.  Ki5-sit8 chit e5 than3 kau3 e5 su7, si7 chhut ti7 lang5 e5 liong5-sim.  Siat-su2 lan2 siuN7 tek-khak si7 ho2 chiu7 thah3 i.  Na7 phah- sng3 si7 m7 tioh8 lan2 chiu7 li7-khui i.  Mih-sai2 ke2-iaN3 thoa pe7-bu2 lai5 teh the-si5 leh.
Lau7 be2 oe7 jin7 lou7
Koan2 Tiong7 kap Che5 Hoan5-kong the3 Ian-kok khi3 cheng-hoat8  Kou-tiok kok, phah jip8 khi3 chin hng7.  Kou-tiok e5 peng tong3 long2 boe7 tiau5, chiu7 siuN7 chit8 e5 tok8 pou7, eng7 tam7-poh8 peng cha3 pai7,  in2-iu2 Che5-kok e5 peng, tui3 Ban7-li2 Sa-bok8 e5 sou2-chai7 khi3.  Hit te3 si7  Tiong-kok pak hng, kap Ngou5-lo5 kau-kai3 e5 sou2-chai7; kou2-cha2 e5 si5 lang5 long2 m7 bat khi3 hia, sou2-i2 choan5 si7 ia2-siu3 kap tok8 choa5; koh  si3-koe3 long bo5 chui2 thang chiah8, na7 khi2 hong, chiu7 bin7-tui3-bin7 to bo5 khoaN3-kiN3 lang5, beh chhut-lai5 iu7 m7 chai lou7.  Au7-lai5 Koan2 Tiong7 chiah  siuN7 kong2, Chian3-be2 khah choe7 si7 tui3 pak peng5 e5 sou2-chai7 khi3 e5; koh na7 si7 lau7 be2, i e5 lou7 ia7 kiaN5 khah choe7, u7 khah chai-iaN2.  Chiu7 keng2  chit8 chiah lau7 be2, chiong ka7-kiuN ka7 thau2-khi2-lai5, pang3 hou7 i ka-ki7 kiaN5, chiah beng7-leng7 kun-peng tai7-ke te3 chit chiah be2 lai5 kiaN5.  Au7-lai5 ko2-jian5 chhe7-tioh8 hit tiau5 toa7-lou7 thang chhut-lai5.     
Na7 lun7-kau3 Koan2 Tiong7, sng3 si7 kou2-cha2 chin chhut-mia5, toa7 chai5-tiau7 e5 lang5, i e5 ti3-sek chhong- beng5 ia7 sng3 chin chiok, i iau2 kam-goan7 kho3 hit chiah lau7-be2 lai5 in2-chhoa7 i e5 lou7, na2 chhin-chhiuN7 jin7 i choe3 sian-siN.  Ho5-hong3 lan2 e5 peng5-siong5 lang5, thai3 thang ka-ki7 chu7-chiok chu7-ko, m7 kheng2 kiu5 lang5 ka3-si7 leh? 
Chhak8 ke5 ka-ki7 gia5
Song3 ong5 mng7 i e5 chaiN2-siong3 Tng5 Iong3 kong2, Goa2 sou2 thai5 e5 lang5, ia7 sng3 si7 chin choe7; chong2-si7 chiah e5 cheng3 jin5-sin5 thai3 long2 iau2-ku2 si7 m7 kiaN goa2, che si7 sim2-mih8 ian5-ko3?  Tng5 Iong3 kong2, Ong5 sou2 thai5 e5, put-ko3 si7 hiah e5 phaiN2 lang5. Ong5 thai5 hiah e5 phaiN2 lang5, sou2-i2 ho2 lang5 na2 m7 kiaN.  Ong5 na7 ai3 cheng3 jin5-sin5 tak8  
e5 kiaN li2, put-ju5 m7 bian2 hun-piat ho2 phaiN2, liah8 lai5 chiu7 ka7 i thai5; an2-ni cheng3 jin5- sin5 tek-khak oe7 kiaN lah.  Ke3 bo5 kui2 jit8, Song3 ong5 chiu7 chiong Tng5 Iong3 ka7 i thai5 khi3.  Siok8-gu2 kong2, Choe3 bak8-chhiuN7 chhak8 ke5 ka-ki7 gia5; ia7 kong2, Lim5 Tou7-khian5 chu3 chheng3 phah ka- ki7.  In-ui7 Lim5-Tou7-khian5, (chai7-cha2 Tai5-oan5 e5 hai2- chhat8), u7 chu3 chit8 khoan2 e5 chheng3 lai5 eng7; bo5 siuN7 au7-lai5 ke3 bo5 joa7-ku2, ka-ki7 hou7 hit khoan2 e5 chheng3 phah si2.  Chhin-chhiuN7 chit khoan2 e5 chu7-chok chu7- siu7, chiaN3 tu2-ho2 kap Tng5 Iong3 e5 su7 saN-tang5. 
Long2 tioh8 jin7 chit
Chong5-a2 kap Kok-a2 nng7 lang5 saN-kap khi3 chhi7 iuN5, ia7 nng7 lang5 e5 iuN5 long2 u7 phah-m7-kiN3.  U7 lang5 mng7 Chong5-a2 khoaN3 si7 an3-chaiN2-iuN7 thai3 oe7 phah-m7-kiN3 iuN5. Chong5-a2 kong2, Goa2 si7 in-ui7 chhi7-iuN5 e5 si5 teh khoaN3 chheh.  Iah8 mng7 Kok-a2 khoaN3 si7 ui7 siaN2-su7 sit-loh8 iuN5.  Kok-a2 kong2, Si7 in-ui7 khoaN3-iuN5 e5 si5-che7 teh poah8-kiau2. An2-ni in nng7 lang5 sou2 choe3 e5 su7 sui-jian5 si7 bo5 saN tang5, phah-m7-kiN3 iuN5 khiok si7 siang7 chit8 khoan.     
Se3-kan lang5 bo5 lun7 choe3 sim2-mih8 tai7-chi3, long2 tioh8 ai3 u7 choan-sim, chu7-jian5 kian3 choe3 kian3 seng5- kong,kiN3 pan7 kiN3 ho2-se3.  Ia7 na7 beh chhiu2 teh choe3 chit hang7, sim-koaN teh siuN7 hit hang7, lang5 khia7 ti7 chit peng5 soaN, sim-koaN teh siuN7 hit peng5; an2-ni chu7-jian5 tek-khak boe7 oe7 seng5-kong.  Lang5 kong2, Sip8 ge7 kiu2 put seng5, ia7 kong2, Se3-siong7 bu5 lan5 su7, tou iu5 sim put choan, sit8-chai7 ko2-jian5 si7 an2-ni.
IuN5 chheng7 hou2 phe5
Iong5-chu2 bat kong2 U7 chit8 chiah iuN5, seng-khu moa chit8 nia2 hou2-phe5, kiaN5 kau3 ti7 khong3-ia2 nih8; chit8-e7 khoaN3-kiN3 chhau2 hoat kau3 chin ou-iu3, chiu7 hoaN-hi2 kau3 boe7 kou3 tit.  Chit8-e7 khoaN3-kiN3 chhai5-long5, chiu7 put-chi2 kiaN, ia7 khiok boe7 ki3-tit seng-khu u7 ta3 hit nia2 hou2-phe5.     
Chhin-chhiuN7 se3-kan u7 chit8 khoan2 ke2-ho2 e5 siau2- jin5, sui-jian5 si7 pah-poaN e5 iam2-sek, chng kau3 na2- chun2 cheng3-keng lang5, ke2 kau3 chin u7 kun-chu2 e5 khi3-khai3, m7-ku2 i e5 teh kiaN5-tah8 kap kong2-oe7, iu5- goan5 siong5-siong5 oe7 hian2-chhut i e5 pun2-siong3 lai5. Tai7-hak8 e5 chheh u7 kong2, U chin-sit8 ti7 sim-lai7, chiu7 oe7 hian2-chhut hit e5 heng5-iong5 ti7 goa7-bin7; chiu7-si7 kong2-khi2 lang5 e5 heng5-tong7 ku2-chi2 si7 boe7 ke2 choe3 tit. 
Hou5 ka2 hou2 ui
 Chai7-cha2 Chiau He5-sut choe3 Chhou2-kok e5 chaiN2-siong3; hit si5  Chhou2-kok e5 peng chin kiong5, liat8-kok long2 ui3-khu7 i; ti3-kau3 i e5 ong5 ia7 teh khi7-khek, siuN7 beh thai5 Chiau He5-sut, U7 chit8 jit8 Chhou2 Soan-ong5 che7 tian7 e5 si5, mng7  cheng3 jin5 sin5 kong2, Pak-hng e5 kok long2 kiaN Chiau He5-sut, che si7 sim2-mih8 ian5-kou3?  Cheng3 tiau5-sin5 long2 chai ong5 u7 beh thai5 i e5 i3-su3, sou2-i2 bo5 lang5 kaN2 chhap-chhui3.  Khiok u7 chit8 lang5, mia5-kio3 Kang It, chhut pan lai5 chau3 kong2, U7 chit8 chiah hou2 chhut-lai5 tho2 chiah8 e5 si5-chun7, tit-tioh8  chit8 chiah hou5-li5, hit chiah hou5-li5 chai-kio3 chau2 boe7 li7, chiu7 ka7 hou2 kong2, Li2 m7-thang chiah8 goa2, in-ui7 Thian-te3 u7 beng7-leng7 goa2 choe3 pah hang7 siu3 e5 si7-toa7; li2 na7 chiah8 goa2, sng3 si7 ui5-keh8 Thian-te3 e5 beng7-leng7.   Li2 na7 m7 sin3 goa2 e5 oe7, chhiaN2 li2 hou7 goa2 choe3 thau5-cheng5 kiaN5, li2 te3 goa2 ka-chiah-au7, ia7 ka7 khoaN3 pah hang7 siu3 kiN3-tioh8 goa2 e5 si5, tek- khak oe7 si3-soaN3 siam2-pi7 goa2.  Hou2 chiu7 beh chhi3-khoaN3 u7 iaN2 bo5, te3 hou5-li5 e5 ka-chiah-au7 khi3; ko2-jian5 pah hang7 siu3 kiN-tioh8 long2 chau2-pi7 i;  ia7 hit chiah hou2 m7 chai pah siu3 teh kiaN i, liah8-choe3 chin-chiaN3 u7 iaN2  teh kiaN hit chiah hou5-li5.  TaN Chiau He5-sut si7 choe3 Chhou2-kok e5 chaiN2- siong3, chiang2-koan2 kun-peng kap kok-lai7 e5 su7.  Sou2-i2 pak-hng e5 kok teh kiaN i, sit8-chai7 m7 si7 teh kiaN Chiau He5-sut, si7 teh kiaN tai7-ong5 e5 peng-be2 chiah-nih8 choe7.  Chhou2 Soan-ong5 thiaN-liau2 u7 cheng5-li2, chiu7 bo5 siuN7 beh thai5 Chiau He5-siut.  
Lun7 kau3 Hou5 ka2 Hou2 ui chit khoan2, se3-kan lang5 khah choe7 si7 an2-ni; na7 hit e5 lang5 u7 tam7-poh8 chiN5- chai5 a2 se3-lek8, chiu7 tai7-ke long2 ai3 khi3 kap i kau-poe5. U7 si5 ia7 bo5 siu7-tioh8 i e5 ho2-le2 chih-chiap saN khoan2- thai7, na7 chhut-lai5 kau3 te3 chiu7 phin2-phong2 hit e5 lang3 si7 chham i joa7 ho2 tu2 joa7 ho2.  Ki5-sit8 ia7 bo5 iaN2 bo5 chiah, put-ko3 si7 hit cheng2 ai3 kho3 lang5 e5 se3-e5, ka-ki7 chong7-chhut-lai5.  U7 si5 ia7 m7  
saN-bat, ia7 tui3 pat8 lang5 phin2 kong2 si7 in e5 sim2-mih8 chhin-chiaN5.  Na7-si7 chit ho7 lang5, to chiaN3 si7 beh kho3 lang5 e5 se3, thang khi3 khi-hu7 lang5.  M7-ku2 iau2 u7 chit8 khoan2, hit e5 u7 se3-lek8 e5 lang5, bo5 boeh hou7 lang5 kho3, ia7 hit e5 teh kap  i kau-poe5 e5 lang5, ia7 bo5 beh kho3 i e5 se3-lek8; chong2- si7 u7 teh kap i lai5-ong2 e5 si5, chiu7 tak8 lang5 ia7 khah khu7-phaN3; ki5-sit8 in long2 bo5 chun5 sim-mih8 m7 ho2 e5 sim-koaN.  Chhin-chhiuN7 chap8-sou3 ni5 cheng5, u7 pah goa7 e5 thou2-hui2 chu7-chip8 ti7 A-li2-kang2 e7, oa2 Ka-lah8-pou hit e5 soaN kap koaN-peng teh ti2-khong3.  Au7-lai5 Cheng3-hu2 u7 phai3 kun-tui7 beh khi3 biat8 in; chit ho7 tai7-chi3 boe7 bian2-tit u7 hit ho7 ho2 lang5 hou7 phaiN2 lang5 lian5-lui7 e5 su7. 
Cheng3-hu2 chai-kio3 lan2 kau3-hoe7 e5 lang5 khah bo5 chhap chit ho7 e5 tai7-chi3, in-ui7 chai-kio3 lan2 bo5 siu7 hiah e5 sia5-sut8 e5 be5-hek8, chiu7 na7 teh sou-sek e5 si5, khah bo5 kiau2-jiau2 tioh8 lan2 e5 hoe7-lu2, tak8 e5 khoaN3 liau2 siuN7 che khah oe7 kho3 tit; chiu7 ai3 beh chioh thiaN to7-li2 e5 mia5 thang po2-hou7 in e5 sin-ka.  Tak8 jit8 le2-pai3-tng5 e5 lang5 long2 chat8 thong2-thong2, na7 tu2-tioh8 le2-pai3-jit8 kui chng e5 lang5 choe3 chit8-e7 piaN3-lai5, khia7 kau3 koe- lou7 tiaN5-nih8 long2 tiN7 that-that.  Bo5 siuN7 kau3 sou-sek e5 su7 chit8-e7 ke3-khi3 chiu7 tit8-tit8 liu-khi3; taN hian7-si5 chin leng2-tam7.  Hai3--ah!  Chhin-chhiuN7 chit khoan2 oe7 hiau2 kou3 jiok8-the2, ia7 boe7 hiau2-tit kou3 leng5-hun5; si7 bo5 koh-iuN7 kap hit e5 kho3 lang5 e5 se3-lek8 sio- siang7.   
Eng7 Chin-chu toaN7 chiau2-a2
Chai7-cha2 Sui5 Hou5 u7 tit-tioh8 chit8 liap8 chin-chu, chin toa7 liap8  koh chin chheng-liang7; sng3 si7 se3-kai3 bo5 te3 thang chhu2 e5 po2-poe3.  U7 chit8 e5 lang5 khoaN3-kiN3 khong-tiong chit8 chiah chiau2,  in-ui7 sim-lai7 put-chi2 i3-ai3, chiu7 theh8 Sui5 Hou5 hit liap8 chu, chun2 choe3  toaN7 chi2, lai5 toaN7 khong-tiong hit chiah chiau2.  Bo5 siuN7 hit chiah  chiau2 phah to bo5 tioh8, ia7 hit liap8 chu soa3 m7 chai ka-lauh8 tui3 toh-loh8  khi3 lah.     
TaN lan2 tak8 lang5 ka7-ki7 e5 mia7 si7 bo5 siang tiau5, kiam2 m7 si7 bo5 te3  thang khi3 chhu2 e5 po2-poe3 mah?  Kiam2 m7 si7 pi2 Sui5 Hou5 e5 chu khah tui3- tiong7 mah?  Kho2-sioh se3-kan lang5 choe7-choe7 si7 in-ui7 in e5 su-iok8 khoaN3 choe3 ho2 e5 sou2-chai7, chiu7 phe-mia7 khi3 choe3. Kiam2 bo5 chhin-chhiuN7 eng7 Sui5 Hou5 e5 chu teh toaN7 chiau2-a2 chit8 poaN-iuN7?  Siok8-gu2 kong2, Jin5 ui7 chai5 su2, niau2 ui7 sit8 bong5; chit ho7 oe7  
chin chiaN3 si7 hou5- tou5.  Chhi3 mng7 khoaN3 lang5 oe7 eng7 sim2-mih khi3 oaN7 i e5 siN3-mia7 tit a2 boe7.  M7-ku2 lang5 choe7-choe7 si7 oe7 hiau2-tit an2-ni kong2, ia7 m7 kheng2 pang3-sak su-iok8 lai5 kou3 si3-mia7, siuN7-liau2 chin thang thou2-khui3. 
Tham sio2 Sit toa7
Chian3 kok e5 si5, oa2-kun7 Chin3-kok e5 sou2-chai7, u7 chit8 kok sio2 kok kio3 choe3 Kiu5-iu5.  Chin3-kok e5 chaiN2-siong3 Ti3-pek siong5-siong5 siuN7 beh khi3 biat8 i, m7-ku2 hit e5 lou7-chhau2 chin oeh8 chin soe3 tiau5, koh  choan khiN-kau liau2-liau2 chin phaiN2 kiaN5, siuN7 liau2 long2 bo5 ki-hoe7.  Au7-lai5 chiu7 siuN7 chit8 e5 hoat-tou7, tiau5-kou3-i3 chu3 chit8 e5 chin toa7 e5 cheng, pi2  chhia-lou7 u7 nng7 pe7 khoah; chiu7 phai3 lang5 khi3 ka7 Kiu5-iu5 kok e5 ong5  kong2 chit e5 cheng beh sang3 i.  Kiu5-iu5 kok ong5 chiu7 beh phai3 lang5 khi3  siu-li2 to7-lou7, chiong hit e5 khah koaiN5 e5 phiN hou7 ke7, ia7 chiong hiah e5 khiN-kau thun7 khi2--lai5, pi7-pan7 thang ho2 un7-poaN chit e5 toa7 cheng.
