I u7 chit8 e5 jin5-sin5, mia5-kio3 Chhek-chiong Ban7-chi, khou2-khng3 i kong2, Kou2-cha2 e5 si u7 teh kong2, Chi2 u7 tioh8 siu2 hoat-tou7 chiah oe7 hou7 kok-nih8 peng5-tiaN7; lan2 thai3 thang bo5 ian5 bo5 kou3 seng5-siu7 i Ti-pek chit8 e5 toa7 cheng?  Chiau3 khoaN3 Ti3-pek e5 choe3 lang5 si7 tham-sim koh bo5 sin3-sit8, tek-khak si7 in-ui7 beh kong-phah lan2, siuN7 liau2 bo5 ki-hoe7,sou2-i2 chu3 chit8 e5 pi2 chhia-lou7 siang pe7 toa7 e5 cheng lai5 sang3 hou7 tai7-ong5;  tai7-ong5 na7 khi3 ngia5-chih chit e5 cheng, tioh8 koaiN5 e5 hoaN7 thoaN2  hou7 i piN5, khiN-kau thun7 hou7 i tiN7, i chiu7 thang than3 chit e5 ki- hoe7 chin3-peng lai5 kong-phah lan2.  I chiong chit ho7 oe7 lai5 khou2-khng3  i e5 ong5 chin ku2.  I e5 ong5 long2 m7 thiaN i, hoan2-tng2 kong2, In sng3 si7 toa7 kok beh kap lan2 kau-poe5, lan2 na7 m7 seng5-siu7  tek-khak oe7 hou7 in koe3-siau3.  Sui5-si5 chhe lang5 khi3 thun7 lou7, soa3 khi3 ngia5-chih hit e5 toa7 cheng.  Chhek-chiong Ban7-chi the3-tiau5 to3- lai5 chiu7 kong2, Choe3 lang5 e5 jin5-sin5 na7 bo5 chit8 tiam2 chin7-tiong e5 sim-koaN  sng3 choe3 si7 u7 choe7; na7 si7 lan2 u7 chit8 tiam2 chin7-tiong e5 sim, ong5 bo5 beh thiaN lan2, an2-ni lan2 tioh8 siam2-pi7 khah hng7 leh.  Sui5-si5 tui3 sio2-lou7 to5- chau2 khi3 Oe7-kok; ke3 u7 chhit jit8 ku2 na7-tiaN7 hit e5 Kiu5-iu5 kok ko2-jian5 hou7  Ti3-pek biat8-khi3.     
 
Koh u7 chit8 e5 kou3-su7 iu5-goan5 kap chit-e5 beh saN-tang5.  Pi2 teng2-bin7  sou2 kong2 chit chan5 khah cha2 oa2 u7 nng7 pah ni5, ia7 si7 ti7 Chin3 kok-nih8.  Hit si5 si7 Hian3-kong teh che7 ui7.  Hian3-kong siuN7  beh khi3 biat8 Kek-kok; m7-ku2 tioh8 tui3 Gu5-kok keng-ke3, chiah oe7-tit kau3 Kek e5 toe7-hng.  An2-ni siuN7-liau2 chin bo5 hoat-tou7, chiu7  kap i e5 jin5-sin5 chham-siong5.  I u7  chit8 e5 bou5-su7, mia5-kio3 Sun5 Sek chhut- lai5 kong2 tioh8 tui3 Gu5-kok ka7 i chioh lou7 ke5.  Hian3-kong kong2, Gu5-kong beh thai3 kheng2 chioh lan2?   Sun5 Sek chiah kong2, Goa2 chai Gu5-kong e5 lang5 si7  chin tham-sim; na7 eng7 Sui5-kek e5 po2-gek8 kap Khut sou2 chhut e5 po2 be2 chit nng7 hang7 lai5 khi3 sang3 i, i chiu7 oe7 chioh lan2 ke3.  Hian3-kong kong2, Chit nng7 hang si7 lan2 kok-nih8 e5 po2-poe3, thai3 thang khi3 sang3 pat8 lang5?  Sun5 Sek kong2, Che si7 na2 chhin-chhhiuN7 kia3 i khng3, au7-lai5 chiah ka7 i tho2.  Hian3-kong thiaN-liau2 u7 cheng5-li2, chiu7 chiong gek8 kap be2 kau-tai7  Sun5 Sek khi3 sang3 Gu5-kong.  Gu5-kong chhiu2-nih8 theh8 hit te3 po2-gek8, bak8-chiu teh khoaN3 po2 be2, sim-lai7 toa7 hoaN-hi2.  I ia7 u7 chit8 e5 gau5 e5 jin5-sin5 mia5-kio3 Kiong Chi-ki5 kan3-cheng3 i kong2, Tek-khak m7-thang siu i chit nng7 hang7 le2-mih8.  Na7 siu i e5 si5 tek-khak tioh8 lou7 chioh i ke3, iah8 au7-lai5 chin3 biat8 Kek-kok liau2-au7 chong2 bo5 tiaN7-tiaN7  ka7 lan2 chioh lou7 khi3 koan2 hia e5 peh-siN3; tek-khak lian5 lan2 e5 kok ia7 oe7  bo5--khi3.  Lang5 kong2, Tun5-bong5 chhi2-han5 (chhui3-tun5 bo5-- khi3, chhui3-khi2 chiu7 oe7 koaN5)chiu7-si7 chit e5 i3-su3.  Sou2-i2 tek-khak m7 thang chun2 i e5 peng tui3 chia ke3.  Chong2-si7  Gu5-kong e5 sim-koaN i2-keng hou7 hit e5 po2 be2 kap po2- gek8 be5 khi3, chiu7 in3 Kiong Chi-ki5 kong2, Chin3 kap Gu5 sng3 si7 siang7 ji7-siN3 e5 kok, i kaN2 put-jim2 lai5 biat8 goa2.  Koh goa2 teh che3-su7 put-chi2 khian5-seng5, ia7 eng7 chin choe7 ho2 mih8 an2-ni sin5-beng5 tek-khak oe7 po2-pi3 goa2.  Kiong Chi-ki5 kong2, Che long2 boe7 kho3 tit e5 su7, Chin3 oe7 hiah toa7 kok ia7  si7 u7 thun-chiam3 chong-chok8 lai7 kui2-na7 kok, koh hian7-si5 beh khi3 biat8 i e5 Kek-kok, kiam2 m7 si7 iu5-goan5 siang7 chong-chok8?  Iah8 hit e5 sin5-beng5 e5 su7 sng3-si7 bong5-bong5 biau2-biau2, bo5 iaN2 bo5 chiah; siat-su2 Chin3 na7 chiong Gu5-kok biat8 khi3 liau2, ia7 iu5-goan5 eng7 ho2 mih8 lai5 che3-hian3,  hit e5 sin5-beng5 kiam2 u7 kong2 oe7 thou3 chhut lai5 heng5 i mah?  So2-i2  che long2 si7 boe7 kho3 tit e5 su7.  Kiong Chi-ki5 an2-ni u7 chhui3 kong2 kau3 bo5 noa7, m7-ku2 bo5 hoat-tou7 thang i-ti7 Gu5-kong e5 tham-sim.  Sou2-i2 Gu5-kong m7 thiaN i khou2-khng3; keng3-jian5 tui3 Chin3-kok e5 su3-chia2 tah-eng3 lou7 beh chioh i ke3.  Kiong Chi-ki5 chiu7 to3-khi3, kau3 in chhu3 e5 si5  chiu7 tui3 lang5 kong2, Lan2 e5 jin5-kun kong2 kio3 sin5-beng5 oe7 po2-pi3 i, goa2  khoaN3 chiah e5 sin5-beng5 kin-ni5 e5 ji7-kau2-mi5 bo5 thang koh-chai3 chiah8 tioh8 Gu5-kok e5 che3-mih8.  Kong2-liau2 chiu7 chiong i e5 bou2-kiaN2 ia7 soa3  poaN chhut kok-goa7, chau2 khi3 tiam3 ti7 Cho5-kok.  Ko2- jian5 ti7 hit ni5 e5 ni5-be2, Chin3 e5 peng khi3 biat8 Kek-kok liau2-au7 khai2-soan5 beh to3-lai5 e5  si5, iu5-goan5 tui3 Gu5-kok keng-ke3, chiu7 sun7-soa3 chiong Gu5-kok ka7 I biat8 khi3, soa3 liah8 Gu5-kong kap in e5 tai7-hu-koaN Pek-li2 He5 to3-khi3 in kok-nih8.     
Lang5 kong2, Chai thang kau3-giah8 chiu7 boe7 siu7 leng5-jiok8, chai thang hioh-khun3 chiu7 boe7 u7 gui5-hiam2.  Che si7 teh keng2-kai3 lang5 tioh8 an-hun7 siu2-ki2, m7 thang sim-koaN siuN toa7 e5.  Chong2-si7 kong2 khiok si7 khah khoai3; na7-si7 beh chiau3 an2-ni lai5 kiaN5 si7 chin oh.  In-ui7 chit8 tiam2 tham e5 sim-koaN chin oh-tit tu5 khi3.  Tui3 kou2-cha2 kau3 taN u7-e5 biat8 kok, u7- e5 kheng ka, u7-e5 pai7-hoai7 mia5-siaN, u7-e5 sit-loh8 siN3-mia7, choe7-choe7 si7 tui3  chit ji7 lai5.  U7-e5 khah li7-hai7 e5 piN3 kau3 hong5-te3 choe3 ke3 chhiu2, siN3-mia7  chiah bo5--khi3.  U7-e5 be7-cheng7-be7 su7 chiu7 phoa3, hou7 koaN--lang5 liah8- khi3 teng7 si2-heng5; bo5 m7 si7 ui7-tioh8 tham lai5 khi2-kian3.  Sou2-i2 tui3 soe3-han3 e5 si5 eng-kai tioh8 seng tui3 chit hang7 e5 siu-sin lai5 ti3-i.  Chiu7-si7 tak8 lang5 bo5 m7 tioh8 eng7 teng2-bin7 hit nng7 cham7 e5 kou3-su7 lai5 choe3 keng2-kai3.  Siok8-gu2 u7 kong2, Tham--ji7 pin5--ji7 khak, sou2-i2 lang5 na7 oe7 chai-chiok chiu7 sim-koaN ho5 si5 m7 peng5-an.  Seng3-keng ia7 u7 kong2, Tham-chai5 si7 choe3 ban7 hang7 phaiN2 e5 kun-goan5.  Ki5-sit8 bo5 lun7 sim2-mih8 su7 na7 u7 chit ji7 tham--ji7 ti7 sim-lai7, chiu7 long2 kau3-giah8 thang hai7 lang5.   
Oe7 siu2 chiah si7 Gau5
Tio7 Siong-chu2 khi3 kong-phah Tek8-kok u7 tek-seng3.  Tek8-kok u7 nng7 e5  siaN5 kio3-choe3 Tiong-jin5 Lo2-jin5.  Teh kou3 hit nng7 e5 siaN5 e5 koaN-hu2 u7 chhe su3-chia2 lai5 beh kiN3 Siong-chu2, kam-goan7 chiong in e5 siaN5-ti5 lai5 kui-hang5; hit-si5 Siong-chu2 tu2-a2 teh chiah8 e7-tau3 thiaN-liau2 ia7 bo5 sim2-mih8 hoaN-hi2 e5 khoan2,I e5 kun-lang5  
khoaN3-liau2 chin ki5-koai3; chiu7 mng7 i kong2, Chit8 jit8 e5 tiong-kan, tit-tioh8 nng7 cho7 e5 siaN5-ti5, iu7-koh bo5 sim2-mih8 toa7 chhut-lat8, a2-si7 liau2 siuN choe7 pun2, an2-ni sng3 si7 chit8 kiaN7 thang hoaN-hi2 e5 tai7-chi3, chaiN2-iuN7 chu2-kong e5 bin7 hoan2-tng2  u7 iu-chhiu5 e5 khoan2, che hou7 goan2 chin boe7 hiau2-tit.  Siong-chu2 chiu7 in3 i kong8, Hit-ho7 kang-ho5 e5 toa7 lau5-chui2, put-ko3 saN nng7 jit8 chiu7 chiam7-chiam7 the3 khi3; hit ho7 he7-thiN e5 toa7 hong-hou7 kek8-ku2 chit8 poaN3  jit8 ia7 chiu7 peng5-cheng7.  Hian7-chai7 lan2 Tio7-kok bo5 u7 sim2-mih8 toa7 tek- heng7, chit8 jit8 tit-tioh8 nng7 cho7 e5 siaN5-ti5, i2-keng sng3 choe3 si7 kiaN5 kau3 kek8  koaiN5 e5 sou2-chai7; kiaN oe7 tui3 an2-ni liau2-au7 chiu7 chiam7-chiam7 soe-pai7 khi3 lah.     
Hit si5 Khong2-chu2 thiaN-kiN3 chit e5 tai7-chi3 chiu7 kong2, Tio7-kok si7 teh beh heng e5 tiau7-thau5; tui3 kou2-cha2 i2-lai5 hoan5-lo2 iu-chhiu5 si7 oe7 hou7 lang5 heng- ong7; hoaN-hi2 khoai3-lok8 si7 oe7 hou7 lang5 pai7-bong5.  Oe7 tek-seng3 boe7 kong2- tit si7 oh e5 su7, tioh8 oe7 po2-siu2-tit kau3 kiu2-oan2, he chiah si7 ui5-lan5 e5 tai7-chi3.     
Kou2 lang5 gian5 kong2, Hian7-si5 e5 se3-kai3, m7-tan7-na7 chhong3 su7-giap8 ui5-lan5, beh lai5 oe7 po2-siu2-tit ia7 m7 si7 iong5-iN7 e5 su7, sit8-chai7 chin u7-iaN2.  Chong2-si7 lang5 na7 ti7 khoai3-lok8 e5 si5 m7 thang boe7 ki3-tit kan-khou2 hit-tiap8, ia7 m7 thang chiah8 pa2 boe7 ki3-tit iau si5.  An2-ni chiah lioh8-a2 oe7 po2-tit i chit8-si3 lang5 boe7 siuN li7-keng; na7 bo5 chiu7 nng7-lin3-poaN3 iu7-koh peng2-loh8 lai5.  Chong2-si7 lan2 kau3-hoe7 lai7 e5 lang5 ia7 tioh8 ai3 chin soe3-ji7.  U7 chit8 khoan2 e5 houe7 iu2 chit8-e7 jip8-kau3, iah8 chiu7 hia-hia pai-pai ka-ki7 chin tek-i3, na2-chhin-chhiuN7 thian- kok e5 so2-si5 i2-keng ti7 i chhiu2 tiong-ng-nit8, hit e5 thian-kok e5 bian2-liu5 i2-keng ti7 i hau-pau-a2 lai7.  Long2 bo5 siuN7 kau3 Seng3-keng-nih8 ia7 u7 beng5-beng5 kong2-ke3. KiN3-na7 chheng-hou goa2, Chu2 ah, Chu2 ah hit ho7 e5 lang5 bi7 pit-jian5 long2 oe7 chin3-jip8 thian-kok.  An2-ni thang chai chit ho7 jip8-kau3 e5 su7, sui-jian5 si7 chin iau3-kin2,  chong2-si7 hit ho7 chin-chiaN3 kau3-iu2 e5 tek-heng7, si7 keng3 koh khah tioh8 iau3-kin2.   
Chit8 lang5 chit8 hang7 tioh8
 Chai7-cha2 ti7 Chi-na2 SoaN-tang Che5 Lou2 nng7 kok e5 kau-kai3, hit sou2-chai7 u7 chit8 e5 lang5 siN saN e5 kiaN2; in lau7-pe7 chiu7 the3 i chhe7 chhut-mia5 e5 sian-siN lai5 ka3-si7 i  
jin5-gi7 e5 to7-li2.  Au7-lai5 kau3 chut-giap8 to3-lai5, in lau7-pe7 mng7 in kong2, Jin5-gi7 e5 to7-li2 chaiN2-iuN7 kong2?  Hit e5 toa7 kiaN2 chiu7 in3 kong2, Jin5-gi7 si7 kio3 goa2 tioh8 thiaN3-sioh seng-khu, jian5-au7 choe3-chiaN5 ho2 e5 mia5-siaN.  Hit e5 te7 ji7 kiaN2 kong2, Jin5-gi7 si7 kio3 goa2 tioh8 pang3-sak seng-khu, lai5 chiaN5 jin5-ai3 e5 mia5-siaN.  Hit e5 te7 saN kiaN2 kong2, Jin5-gi7 si7 kio3 goa2 tioh8 po2-hou7 seng-khu, chiau3-kou3 mia5-siaN, nng7 hang7 long2 oe7 chiau5-chng5.  TaN in chit saN e5 hiaN-ti7-a2 siang7 si7 chit8 e5 sian-siN ka3-si7 in, m7-ku2 in tai7-ke e5 kian3-kai2 long2 si7 toa7-toa7 bo5 saN-tang5. 
Ti7 In3-tou7 e5 sou-chai bat u7 lang5 khan chit8 chiah chhiuN7 tui3 koe-chhi7-nih8  ke3,u7 lang5 kong2 hit chiah chhiuN7 si7 ou-e5, u7 lang5 kong2 hit chiah chhiuN7  si7 peh8-e5, u7 lang5 kong2 hit chiah chhiuN7 si7 hoe-sek e5; tai7-ke chiN3 kau3 khia7  chin khia7 hian7, long2 m7 kheng2 sio-niu7, tit8-tit8 beh oan-ke khi2 lai5.  Au7-lai5  lang5 chiah khi3 chha5 khoaN3 tau3-ti2 si7 sim2-mih8 sek, chiah chai saN lang5 sou2 kong2 e5 oe7 long2 u7 chit8 hang7 tioh8.  In-ui7 hit chiah chhiuN7 chit8 peng5 si7 ou-e5,  chit8 peng5 si7 peh8-e5.  Ti7 chiaN3 peng5 e5 kan-ta khoaN3-kiN3 peh8-sek, sou2-i2  kong2 si7 peh8 chhiuN7; ti7 to3-peng5 e5 kan-ka khoaN3-kiN3 ou sek, sou2-i2 kong2  si7 ou chhiuN7.  Ia7 hit e5 ti7 thau5-cheng5 e5 khoaN3-kiN3 ia7 u7 peh8 ia7 u7 ou, sou2-i2  kong2 si7 hoe-sek e5 chhiuN7.   
Koh u7 chit8 hang7 chhin-chhiuN7 hoa3-seng e5 lui7.  U7 chit8 khoan2 thang5,  chham kim-ku beh saN-siang7 khoan2, chong2-si7 i e5 sek-ti7 chit8 jit8 piN3  kui2-na7 sek.  Bat ti7 cha2-khi2 si5 liah8 lai5 ka7 i khoaN3 si7 kim e5 sek-ti7; kau3  e7-pou ka7 i khoaN3 piN3 choe3 chhiN-e5; bin5-a2-cha2 khi2 iu7 piN3 choe3 ou-e5, a2-si7  piN3 choe3 hoe-sek e5, long2 bo5 tiaN7-tioh8.  Si7 chhin-chhiuN7 lang5 teh chhi7 chham5-a2 (niu5-a2); cha2-khi2 khoaN3 si7 thang5, e7-pou khoaN3 chit8 liap8 phok8-a2(chham5-kian2); bin5-a2-chai3 ka7 theh8 chhut lai5 khoaN3-liau2 chit8 liap8 chhin-chhiuN7 thou5-tau7-jin5; keh chit8 poaN3 jit8 iu7 piN3 chiah be2-iah8 chhut-lai5;  iah8 chiu7 oe7 kang-bu2 saN thin7, koh pang3 nng7 lai5 piN3-choe3 chham5-a2.   Chong2-si7 na7 he long2 m7 bat khoaN3-kiN3 e5 lang5, thiaN-lian2 chiu7 chin giau5-gi5.   
Ia7 koh chit8 khoan2 kou3-chip put-hok8-jin5 e5, chhin-chhiuN7 khoaN3-kiN3 chhiuN7 e5 chit8 peng5, chiu7 liah8 choe3 i bak8-chiu sou2 khoaN3 si7 an2-ni, chiu7 ngi7-ngi7 liah8 choe3 an2-ni tioh8.  Chong2-si7 na7 chhin bak8 khoaN3-kiN3 an2- ni chiN3 iau2 oe7 kong2-tit.  U7 chit8 cheng2 hiah e5 be5- sin3 kui2-sin5 e5 su7, beng5-beng5 to bo5 iaN2 e5 tai7-chi3 ia7 saN- kap hu7-hoe7 chong7 kau3 chin tu2 chin, hian7 tu2 hian7, boh8-kioh bak8-chiu u7 khoaN3-kiN3 e5 su7, chu7-jian5 tek- khak si7 beh chiN3 kau3 iaN5.  An2-ni kho2-kian3 se3-kan su7 si7 chin  
khoah, m7 thang eng7 ka-ki7 sio2-khoa2 e5 ti3- sek, chiu7 beh ka7 i toan3 kong2 si7 chaiN2-iuN7; long2 tioh8 khoaN3 hit e5 su7-the2 u7 hap8 to7-li2 than3 hoat-tou7 a2 bo5, chiah thang khi3 kiaN5.  
Oe7 chiu7 bo5 Ui5-lan5
Hok8 Chu2-chian7 teh choe3 Sian7-hu2 e5 toe7-hng koaN, hit si5 Iu2-jiok8 khi3  chhe7 i; khoaN3-kiN3 i piN3 chin siau-san2, chiu7 mng7 i si7 sim2-mih8 ian5-kou3.    Hok8 Chu2-chian7 in3 i kong2, Li2 long2 m7 chai mah?  Goa2 si7 bo5 lou7-eng7 e5 lang5, phai3 goa2 lai5 choe3 Sian7-hu2 e5 toe7-hng koaN; in-ui7 tai7-chi3 chin choe7, put- chi2 bo5 eng5, sim-lai7 ia7 chin hoan-lo2, sou2-i2 seng-khu chiah oe7 chiah-nih8 siau-san2 lah.  Iu2-jiok8 kong2, Kou2-cha2 e5 si5, Sun3 teh choe3 hong5-te3, i toaN5 ngou2-hian5 e5 khim5, chhiuN3 lam5-hong e5 si, choe3 i an-han5 chu7-chai7, thong kok iu5-goan5 si7 liau7-li2 kau3 ho2-se3 ho2-se3.  Hian7-chai7 chit e5 sio2-sio2 khoa2-khoa2 e5 Sian7-hu2 na7-tiaN7, li2 chiu7 hoan5-lo2 kau3 long2 boe7 hiau2-tit thang ti7-li2; siat-su2 hou7 li2 choe3 hong5-te3 lai5 koan2 kui kok, iah8 beh an2-chaiN2-iuN7 leh?     
Lan2 lang5 ti7 chit se3-kan, tioh8 u7 hit-hang7 e5 pun2- su7, chiah oe7 pan7 tit hit-hang7 e5 su7-giap8.  Siat-su2 to bo5 hit ho7 toa7 chai5-tiau7, kan-ta siuN7 beh choe3 hit ho7 toa7 su7-giap8, tek-khak si7 chiong hiah e5 tioh8- boa5 kui ti7 khang-khang.  Siok8-gu2 kong, Ti3 chioh8 cheng-khu7 teh thiau3 ka-koan; chhut chin choe7 lat8 koh m7 ho2 khoaN3, chiu7-si7 chit e5 i3-su3.  Chong2-si7 teng2-bin7 sou2 kong2, Hok8 Chu2-chian7 choe3 Sian7-hu2 e5 toe7-hng koaN, sui5-jian5 si7 bo5 toa7 chai5-tiau7, khiok ia7 chin7 sim lai5 liau7-li2; sou2-i2 boa5 kau3 ka-ki7 e5 sin-the2 long2 siau-san2 khi3.  M7-ku2 Sian7-hu2 e5 kau3-hoa3 toa7 heng-khi2, an2-ni sng3 si7 toa7 ho2 e5 koaN-oan5.  Na7 pi2- pheng7 iau2 chit8 khoan2, chhin-chhiuN7 chit ho7 chai5- tiau7 iu7 bo5, chi3-khi3 iu7 toa7, kan-ta kou3 i ka-ki7 oe7 pui5, m7 koan2 peh-siN3 chaiN2-iuN7 kan-khou2, che chiu7 thian chha ti7 ian lah.   
KhoaN3 kun7 bo5 khoaN3 hng7
Bou2 sou2-chai7 u7 chit8 ui7 toa7-ke khau2-cheng3 e5 lang5, in e5 chau3-kha tun2  kau3 chit8 tui chha5, ia7 hit e5 ian-tang5 chau3-chhui3 koh tu2 ho2 ng3 ti7 hia.  U7 chit8 e5 lang5 khoaN3-liau2 chiu7 siuN7 an2-ni put-chi2  gui5-hiam2; chiu7 tui3 chu2-lang5 kong2, Tioh8 chiong ian-tang5 chhui3 soa2 tui3  piN-a2 khi3, ia7 chiong hiah e5 chha5-chhau2 poaN-soa2 khi3 pat8-ui7, chiah bo5 gui5-hiam2; na7 bo5, kiaN-liau2 u7 he2-chai.  Chu2-lang5 m7 thiaN i.   
Ke3 bo5 joa7-ku2, ko2-jian5 tui3 hiah e5 chha5-chhau2 e5 tiong-kan khi2 he2, chiu7 u7 kui2-na7 lang5 lai5  kap i tau3 kha-chhiu2, phah he2 hou7 hoa.  Chong2-si7 tai7-ke i2-keng sio kau3 chhau3-thau5 noa7-hi7; au7-lai5 chu2-lang5 pi7-pan7 ian5-siah8, lai5 ka7 tai7-ke seh to-sia7, chiu7 chhiaN2 hiah e5 chhau3-thau5 noa7-hi7 e5 che7 toa7-ui7; ia7 hit e5 ka3 i soa2 ian-tang5 poaN chha5-chhau2 e5 lang5, khiok bo5 khi3 chhiaN2 i.  Sou2-i2 hian7- si5 e5 lang5 u7 chit8 ku3 oe7 kong2, Khiok tut2 su2 sin, bu5 un-tek8; chiau thou5 lan7 gek8 ui5 siong7 khek.  (Chiu7-si7 kong2, tai7-seng kah i ti5-hong5, oaN7 ian-tang5 chhui3, soa2-khui chha5-chhau2, chit ho7 liong7-cha2 tiuN-ti5 e5 khui3-lat8 chin7 toa7, in long2  bo5 siau3-liam7 i e5 un-tek.  Ia7 thoe3 in phah he2 hiah e5 lang5 u7-e5 sio kau3 chhau3 thau5, u7-e5 noa7 hiah8, in chiu7 siuN7 kong2, Che kiu3 lan2 e5 kin2-kip kong-lo5 chin choe7, chiu7 chhiaN2 in lai5 choe3 siong7-teng2 e5 lang5 kheh). 
Se3-kan u7 chin choe7 hit ho7 ui5-hui chok-tai2, tak8 hang7 kaN2 choe3 e5 lang5, ia7 siong5-siong5 u7 lang5 khou2-khng3 i tioh8 hoan2-hoe2 koe2-piN3 lai5 kui Siong7-te3  e5 chin-li2, thang bian2-khi3 au7-lai5 e5 chai-e7; ia7 m7 bian2 choe3 kau3 au7-lai5 su7  phoa3 hoan7-choe7, siu7 kaN-lo5 e5 kan-khou2.  Chong2-si7 in long2 bo5 beh thiaN i.  Kau3 au7-lai5 i na7 ti7 hit e5 kan-khou2 hoan7-lan7 e5 tiong-kan, na7 lang5 theh8 tam7-poh8-a2 chiN5 pang-chan7 i, i chiu7 kam2-un put-chin7; ia7 khiok bo5  siuN7 kau3 hit e5 khou2-khng3 lan2 hoan2-hoe2 e5 lang5 si7 ho2 sim; i e5 kong-lo5  pi2 eng7 chiN5-chai5 chin2-che3 lan2 e5 si7 khah toa7; in-ui7 lan2 na7 thiaN i e5 chhui3, kin-a2-jit8 m7 bian2 kau3 chit e5 toe7-pou7.  Chong2-si7 khah choe7 long2 bo5 siuN7  an2-ni; khah choe7 si7 kap teng2-bin7 e5 kou3-su7 hit e5 chu2-lang5 sio-siang7.   
Kin2-sin7 sou2 kiaN5
Sam-kok chheh ki3 chit8 cham7 Koan Hun5-tiong2 po2-hou7 in nng7 e5 hiaN-so2 beh kap Cho5 Chho3 chiuN7 kiaN khi3.  Ti7 lou7-nih8 Cho5 Chho3 tiau5-kou3-i3 eng7 chit8 keng pang5 hou7 in saN lang5 toa3, i3-su3 si7 beh hun-loan7 in kun-sin5 e5 le2-sou3.  Chong2-si7 Koan Hun5- tiong2 choe3 i tiam2 lah8-chek chhut lai5 chhu3- goa7 khoaN3 chheh kau3 thiN-kng, long2 bo5 sio2-khoa2 ia3-lan2 e5 bin7-sek.  Cho5 Chho3 khoaN3-kiN3 an2-ni, na2 koh-khah keng3-tiong7 i.     
Koan Hun5-tiong2 e5 sou2 choe3 sng3 kun-chu2 e5 sou2 kiaN5 si3-chiaN3 kong-beng5; long2 bo5 kou3-i3 chng-choe3. KhoaN3 Sam-kok chheh e5 lang5 long2 kong2 i si7 ai3 kou3- i3 choe3 kun-chu2 e5 mia5-siaN, chiah an2-ni lai5 siam2-pi7 hiam5-gi5; na7-si7 chai7 Koan  
Hun5-tiong2 e5 i3-su3 chiu7 bo5 an2-ni kong2, in-ui7 Koan Hun5-tiong2 sou2 kou3 chiu7-si7 Lau5 Pi7 e5 bin7-chiuN7, kap in hiaN-so2 e5 tek-heng7. Cheng3 lang5 e5 lam7-sam2 kong2 tioh8 m7-tioh8 i long2 bou5 khoa3-i3.     
Chiau3 an2-ni ka7 i siuN7, lan2 kau3-hoe7 lai7 e5 hoe7-iu2 na7 oe7 chiau3 i e5 hoat-tou7 lai5 kiaN5, u7 kun-chu2 e5 kah-pou7, kiam2 m7-si7 chin ho2 mah?  KiN3-na7 u7 hiam5-gi5 e5 sou2- chai7, chhin-chhiuN7 chiu2-lau5, hi3-hng5, hoa-ke liu2-hang7, kiau2-tiuN5, che long2 m7-thang khi3, m7 tau7-na7 po2-choan5 ka-ki7 e5 mia5-siaN, chiu7 lan2 e5 Chu2 kap kau3-hoe7 e5 mia5- siaN koh-khah iau3-kin2 tioh8 po2-choan5.     
Seng3-keng u7 kong2, ¡§Sou2 kiaN5 tioh8 toan-chiaN3, chhin-chhiuN7 ti7 jit8-si5; boh8-tit hong3-chhiong3 chiu2- chui3, boh8-tit houN3-sek sia5-im5, boh8-tit saN-chiN oan3- tou3.¡¨(Lo5-ma2 13:13)
Cheng3 tau7 siu tau7
 Chi-na2 chian3-kok e5 si5, ngou2-pa3 chai7-lai7 hit e5 Chin5 Bok8-kong, u7 chit8 pai2 khi3 Niu5-soaN e5 sou2-chai7 phah lah8.   Hit mi5-hng phah m7 kiN3kui2-na7 chiah e5 ho2 be2, chiu7 phai3 lang5 si3-koe3 khi3 chhe7.  Keh bo5 joa7 ku2 u7 lang5 lai5 po3 kong2, Ti7 Ki-soaN e5 lam5-peng5, u7 chha-put-to saN  pah e5 thou2 lang5, i2-keng chiong be2 thai5 khi3 lah; hian7-si5 teh chu2 beh khi3 chiah8; na7 am3-chiN7 phai3 peng khi3, oe7 long2-chong2 liah8 tioh8.  Chin5 Bok8-kong thiaN-liau2 thou2-khui3 kong2, Goa2 phai3 lin2 khi3 chhe7, si7 ng3-bang7 oe7 koh tit- tioh8 hiah e5 be2.  TaN be2 i2-keng si2, hoan7- choe7 e5 lang5 iu7 hiah-nih8 choe7, na7 long2 ka7 i liah8 lai5 pan7, boe7 bian2-tit hou7 lang5 kong2 goa2 khoaN3 cheng-siN khah tui3-tiong7, liah8 lang5 e5 siN3-mia7 khoaN3 khah khin.  Koh goa2 thiaN-kiN3 kong2, chiah8 ho2 be2 e5 bah, bo5 chiah8 chiu2 khi3 chan7 i siau-hoa3, chiu7 oe7 ti3 piN7; hiah e5 thou2 lang5 long2 m7 chai chit khoan2 e5 li7-hai7.  Chiu7 kio3 lang5 chiong i sou2 toa3 lai5 e5 ho2 chiu2, taN khi3 hou7 hiah e5 thou2 lang5, kah in sui5-e5 pun tam7-poh8 khi3 chiah8; hiah e5 lang5 thiaN-liau2 put-chi2 kam2-kek.   
Au7-lai5 keh u7 chit8 ni5 ku2, Chin5 Bok8-kong kap Chin3 kok e5 peng ti7 Han5 e5  sou2-chai7 kau-chian3, Bok8-kong toa7 pai7, Chin3 e5 peng i2-keng chiong Bok8-kong e5 chian3-chhia ui5-teh.  Chin3 e5 nia2 peng koaN Niu5 Iu5-bi2 ia7 i2-keng khiu2 tioh8 Bok8-kong sou2 che7 hit tiuN chhia e5 be2.  Tng hit cham7 chin gui5-kip e5 si5, hut-jian5  
khoaN3-kiN3 saN pah goa7 lang5, ia7 bo5 khia5 be2, ia7 bo5 che7 chhia, chhiu2-nih8 kiah2 toa7 to, tak8-e5 chit8 khia7 chit8 tho3 koaiN5, hiong5 kai3-kai3 tit8-tit8 phah jip8 lai5, khoaN3-ki3 Chin5 Bok8-kong hou7 Chin3 kok e5 peng ui5-teh, chiu7 phe si2 mia7, chiong hiah e5 peng phah the3, m7-na7 kiu3-chhut Chin5 Bok8-kong, hoan2-tng2 chiong Chin3 Hui7-kong liah8-lai5.  Bok8-kong khoaN3-liau2 chin hoaN-hi2, chiu7 tiau3 in lai5 mng7 kong2; Lin2 si7 toh-loh8 e5 lang5, siaN2-su7 kin-a2-jit8 lai5 kiu3 goa2?  Hiah e5 lang5 kong2, Goan2 chiu7-si7 ku7-ni5 thau-khan kun-ong5 e5 ho2 be2 hiah e5 lang5; kam2-liam7 kun e5 toa7 un-tek, bo5 pan7 goan2 e5 choe7 , koh kiaN goan2 phoa3-piN7.  In-ui7 kun7-jit8 thiaN-kiN3 ti7-chia teh sio-thai5, sou2-i2 saN-kap lai5 beh pang-chan7 kun kau-chian3; taN chin-chiaN3 u7 than3 goan2 po3-tap kun e5 sim.  Bok8-kong thiaN-liau2 thou2-khui3 kong2, Cheng3 koe tit-tioh8 koe, cheng3 tan7 siu-seng5 tau7.  Siat-su2 goa2 ku7-ni5 chiong chiah e5 lang5 liah8 khi3 pan7 choe7, in-a2-jit8 thai3 oe7 tit-tioh8 in e5 lat8 lai5 kiu3 goa2 leh?  Chiu7 mng7 in kong2, Lin2 kam-goan7 jip8 iaN5 choe3 peng m7?  Tak8-e5 kong2, Goan2 si7 thou2 lang5, boe7 hiau2 siu2 kui-ku2, m7 kaN2 choe3 kun-peng.  Bok8-kong chiu7 kio3 lang5 theh8 kim-gun5 chai5-po2 siuN2-su3 in; in ia7 long2 m7 siu, choe3 in sio si5 to3-khi3.  
Se3-kan e5 lang5, thang hun choe3 saN teng2.  U7 chit8 teng2 e5 lang5, li2 na7 eng7 un-hui7 khoan2-thai7 i, i hoan2- tng2 eng7 phaiN2 lai5 po3 li2; che mia5 kio3 kui2 to7.  U7 chit8 teng2 e5 lang5, li2 na7 eng7 ho2 khoan2-thai7 i, i ia7 eng7 ho2 po3-tap li2; che kio3 choe3 jin5-to7.  Ia7 u7 chit8 teng2- ho7 e5 lang5, li2 eng7 phaiN2 khoan2-thai7 i, i khiok eng7 ho2 lai5 khoan2-thai7 li2; che kio3 choe3 thian-to7.  Chhin-chhiuN7 Bok8-kong teh khoan2-thai7 hiah e5 thau-khan be2 e5 lang5, chiau3 khoaN3 boe7 bian2-tit u7 siuN2-hoat8 put beng5; m7-ku2 choe7 put kip8 chiong3, saN pah goa7 lang5 long2 in-ui7 hit kui2 chiah be2 lai5 siu7 choe7, khiok iu7 siuN7-liau2 put jim2, iu7-koh chai hiah e5 thou2 lang5 si7 long2 boe7 hiau2-tit hoat-lut8 kap li7-hai7.  Sou2-i2 put-ju5 choe3 cheng5 hou7 in, m7 si7 ai3 tit lang5 in-ui7 an2-ni lai5 o-lo2 i, a2 si7 u7 ng3-bang7 in au7-lai5 e5 po3-tap i, sou2-i2 u7 thang kho2-chhu2.  Chhi3 siuN7 hian7-si5 u7 chit ho7 e5 lang5 a2 bo5; phah-sng3 bo5.  Khah choe7 long2 si7 hit  ho7 bo5 siuN7 lan2 khoan2-thai7 lang5 chaiN2-iuN7, kan-ta oe7 hiau2 hiam5 lang5 phaiN2 khoan2-thai7 i.  Ia5-sou kong2, Tioh8 thiaN3 li2 e5 tui3-tek8; iau tioh8 hou7 i chiah8, chhui3-ta tioh8 hou7 i lim; che chiu7-si7 eng7 un-hui7 lai5 po3-tap phaiN2 khoan2-thai7 lan2 e5 lang5.   
 
Kau chhian2 gian5 chhim
Song3-kok u7 chit8 e5 ho2-giah8 lang5, in chhu3 e5 chhiuN5-a2 in-ui7 chim3-chu3 hou7 loh8 siuN ku2, soa3 hou7 pang chit8 khiah khi3.  In hau7-siN ka7 i kong2, Chit e5 chhiuN5-a2 na7 bo5 siu-li2, kiaN-liau2 oe7 hou7 chhat8 jip8 lai5.  In e5 chhu3-piN chit8 e5 lau7 lang5 ia7 si7 an2-ni kong2. Bo5 siuN7 hit e5-hng, ko8-jian5 u7 chhat8 lai5 thau chin choe7 mih8 khi3.  Hit e5 ho2-giah8 lang5 chiu7 chin o-lo2 i e5 kiaN2 si7 chhong- beng5, ia7 giau5-gi5 chhu3-piN hit e5 lau7 lang5 choe3 chhat8 lai5 thau i.     
TaN chiau3 an2-ni ka7 thiaN, hit e5 ho2-giah8 lang5 e5 kiaN2, kap in chhu3-piN lau7-lang5 sou2 kong2 e5 oe7, si7 siang7 chit8 iuN7, i khiok o-lo2 in kiaN2 chhong-beng5, giau5-gi5 chhu3-piN e5 lang5 choe3 chhat8; in-ui7 in kiaN2 kap chhu3-piN u7 chhin-soe e5 hun-piat.  Sou2-i2 siang7 chit8 khoan2 e5 oe7, u7 nng7 khoan2 e5 khoan2-thai7 i.  Kho2- kian3 hoan7-su7 tioh8 chiong sim-koaN phang5-piN5 lai5 siuN7; na7 bo5, long2 boe7 bian2-tit u7 chun5 than2 chhin e5 sim ti7-teh.
